Multi-cloud strategies are increasingly adopted by modern enterprises to improve agility and resilience and to reduce vendor lock-in. Integrating workloads across providers, such as Amazon Web Services (AWS) and Alibaba Cloud, remains challenging due to interoperability and migration issues. This paper presents a comparative analysis of AWS and Alibaba Cloud, focusing on architectural, service, and policy differences affecting workload migration. Using both provider-native and open source Infrastructure-as-Code tools, we conduct an exploratory case study about the migration of Internet of Things (IoT) workloads. The results highlight key technical trade-offs and best practices for secure multi-cloud deployments, offering guidance for organizations pursuing AWS and Alibaba Cloud interoperability.

### [59] [Efficient Domain Decomposition for the Helmholtz Equation on GPUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21695)

*Amit Rotem*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出了一种基于块级区域分解和WaveHoltz子域求解器的GPU并行方法，用于高效求解亥姆霍兹方程，在A100上相比MINRES实现了2-25倍加速。

#### Problem

亥姆霍兹方程的不定性使其难以用迭代方法求解，且将高效求解器映射到现代GPU架构上仍面临挑战，主要瓶颈在于设备级同步和全局内存流量过大。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察在于：(1) 将每个子域分配给单个线程块，所有子域求解在一个内核启动中并发执行，消除了设备级同步；(2) 采用WaveHoltz定点迭代作为子域求解器，其内存占用极小且无归约操作，天然适配GPU执行模型，可将子域数据主要驻留在L1/L2缓存中。

#### System/Method Design

提出了块级区域分解方案（每个子域对应一个线程块，单内核启动并发求解），配合WaveHoltz子域求解器。探索了两种线程策略：小规模子域采用每线程一个自由度，大规模子域采用每线程多个自由度。实现基于CUDA，利用共享内存和寄存器级操作替代全局内存访问。

#### Experiments

在NVIDIA A100 GPU上进行基准测试，对比MINRES方法。WaveHoltz实现取得2倍到25倍的加速比，优势随子域增大而增长。此外，使用单精度代替双精度求解子域可获得额外2-10倍加速，而MINRES在降精度下因Krylov向量正交性丢失而难以获得类似收益。

#### Why It Matters

该工作证明了通过精心设计的区域分解策略和合适的子域求解器选择，可以在现代GPU上高效求解具有挑战性的亥姆霍兹方程，同时展示了利用低精度计算加速的可行性（这是传统迭代方法难以实现的），对大规模波传播模拟具有实际意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然本文聚焦于科学计算（亥姆霍兹方程），但其系统设计思路对LLM系统研究有启发意义：(1) 块级并发计算+单内核启动的策略可类比MoE中的专家并行或注意力头分组计算；(2) 消除全局同步、最小化全局内存访存的优化思想对KV cache管理和推理加速有参考价值；(3) 低精度计算在保持求解质量前提下大幅提速的经验，与LLM推理中量化技术的动机一致；(4) 每线程分配自由度的策略对GPU上混合精度和计算负载均衡设计有借鉴意义。

#### Abstract

The Helmholtz equation governs wave propagation in acoustics, electromagnetics, and seismology, but its indefinite nature makes it difficult to solve with iterative methods. Domain decomposition methods are a natural fit for massively parallel architectures, yet mapping efficient Helmholtz solvers onto modern GPUs remains a challenge. We address both with two key contributions: (1) a block-level domain decomposition scheme, in which each subdomain is assigned to a single thread block and all solves run concurrently in a single kernel launch, and (2) WaveHoltz as the subdomain solver. WaveHoltz is a fixed-point iteration that is uniquely well-suited to the GPU execution model due to its minimal memory footprint and no reduction operations. Together, these eliminate device-level synchronizations and replace global memory traffic with shared memory and register-level operations, keeping subdomain data largely resident in L1 and L2 cache. We explore two threading strategies: one degree of freedom per thread for small subdomains, and multiple degrees of freedom per thread for larger ones. Benchmarks of our CUDA based implementation on a NVIDIA A100 show that WaveHoltz achieves 2x-25x speedup over MINRES, with the advantage growing with subdomain size. Crucially, evaluating the subdomain solver in single rather than double precision yields an additional 2x-10x speedup--a benefit largely unattainable by MINRES due to loss of Krylov vector orthogonality under reduced precision.

### [60] [BatchGen: An Architecture for Scalable and Efficient Batch Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21712)

*Tairan Xu,Leyang Xue,Zhan Lu,Jinfu Deng,Hongyang Xiao,Yinsicheng Jiang,Congjie He,Matej Sandor,Le Xu,Luo Mai*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** BatchGen 提出序列协程计算模型，将每个序列建模为细粒度事件驱动协程，实现动态工作重组，大幅提升批推理吞吐和GPU利用率。

#### Problem

现有推理引擎专为交互式服务设计，无法应对批处理场景下运行时才暴露的极端序列内/序列间负载变化，也无法在大规模GPU集群上维持高利用率，导致大量吞吐损失。

#### Key Idea

将每个序列表示为细粒度的、事件驱动的协程，通过暴露表达性原语让运行时系统能够动态重组工作负载，例如形成更大的专家级批次、缓解掉队者、跨设备重新分配工作。

#### System/Method Design

提出**序列协程计算模型**作为批推理的新架构基础：每个序列是一个事件驱动的协程，运行时系统利用该抽象提供的原语动态组织计算。在此模型上实现了生产级系统 BatchGen，可在集群规模上运行。

#### Experiments

在128-GPU集群上，BatchGen 将批完成时间最多降低2.3倍；在受内存限制的加速器上，比最强的卸载基线快最多9.6倍。系统将被开源。

#### Why It Matters

批推理已成为AI计算的核心模式，但缺乏专门的执行架构。BatchGen 首次从架构层面重新设计了批推理的执行模型，在高吞吐、高利用率和异构设备适配方面具有重大意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。批推理是LLM服务的关键场景；支持更大专家级批次直接对应MoE模型；缓解掉队者和跨设备工作重分配对分布式系统和大规模并行计算至关重要；适配内存受限GPU涉及推理加速和KV缓存优化。

#### Abstract

Batch inference has become a central mode of AI computation, yet existing inference engines still rely on execution models designed for interactive serving. When scaled to millions of sequences, batch workloads reveal two fundamental requirements: the ability to handle extreme inter- and intra-sequence load variation that emerges only at runtime, and the ability to sustain high utilization across large fleets of GPUs. Existing systems fail to meet these requirements, losing substantial fractions of achievable throughput.
  We introduce a new architectural foundation for batch inference: the sequence coroutine compute model, which represents each sequence as a fine-grained, event-driven coroutine. This model exposes expressive primitives that allow the runtime to reorganize work dynamically, enabling larger expert-level batches, mitigating stragglers, reallocating work across devices, and maintaining utilization even on cost-effective or memory-constrained GPUs. Building on this abstraction, we implement BatchGen, a production-ready system that uses the coroutine model at cluster scale. On a 128-GPU cluster, BatchGen reduces batch completion time by up to $2.3\times$, and on memory-constrained accelerators it outperforms the strongest offloading baseline by up to $9.6\times$. We will open-source BatchGen at https://github.com/batchgen-project/batchgen

### [61] [Rethinking Burst Buffer Optimization: Enabling Layout Heterogeneity via Hybrid Analysis and LLM Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21852)

*Yuhan Cai,Huijun Wu,Zhuo Tang,Kehua Guo,Wenzhe Zhang,Zhenwei Wu,Zhouyang Jia,Ruibo Wang,Yong Dong*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** Proteus 是一种语义感知的突发缓冲区（Burst Buffer）系统，通过结合静态代码结构和轻量级运行时信号动态选择最优数据布局，以消除固定布局与 I/O 模式不匹配带来的性能下降。

#### Problem

现有突发缓冲区文件系统因采用固定数据布局，无法适配多样化的应用 I/O 行为，导致结构性性能退化；而基于机器学习的优化方法仅调整存储栈参数，当 I/O 模式与底层数据组织存在根本性不匹配时收效甚微，且通常需要昂贵的训练或侵入式性能分析。

#### Key Idea

应用 I/O 意图可以通过协同结合静态代码结构与轻量级运行时信号来重建，从而在正式运行前确定最优数据布局，无需预先训练或详尽的性能分析。

#### System/Method Design

Proteus 采用混合流水线，通过单次执行探针（single execution probe）提取潜在语义线索，在正式生产运行前确定最优数据布局。它把数据布局视为一等优化维度，而非仅调优存储栈参数。

#### Experiments

使用代表性 HPC 负载进行评估，Proteus 达到 91.30% 的布局决策准确率；面向写密集型负载实现最高 3.24 倍加速，面向元数据密集型负载实现最高 2.9 倍加速。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次将数据布局提升为 HPC 突发缓冲区的一等优化维度，提出了一种免训练、低开销的语义感知方法，在不依赖历史数据或大量性能剖析的前提下显著提升 I/O 性能，对高性能计算 I/O 栈的设计具有重要参考价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然本文直接面向 HPC 突发缓冲区场景，但其语义感知的自适应数据布局思想对 LLM 训练/推理中的 I/O 瓶颈缓解有借鉴意义——MoE 模型训练中不同专家的数据访问模式差异巨大，类似方法可用于优化专家参数在存储层（如分布式文件系统、KV 缓存卸载）的布局。此外，文中轻量级语义探针的设计思路可应用于 LLM 推理系统中预取策略和缓存策略的自适应优化。

#### Abstract

Burst buffers (BBs) are essential for mitigating I/O bottlenecks in modern HPC systems. However, existing BB file systems often suffer from structural performance degradation due to fixed data layouts that fail to align with diverse application behaviors. While current machine-learning-based optimizations focus primarily on tuning storage stack parameters for a given layout, they offer diminishing returns when a fundamental mismatch exists between I/O patterns and the underlying data organization. Furthermore, these approaches typically incur prohibitive costs due to extensive training or intrusive profiling. To bridge this gap, we present Proteus, a semantic-aware BB system that treats data layout as a first-class optimization dimension. The core insight of Proteus is that application I/O intent can be reconstructed by synergetically combining static code structures with lightweight runtime signals. Through a hybrid pipeline and a single execution probe, Proteus extracts latent semantic cues to determine the optimal layout prior to production runs-eliminating the need for prior training or exhaustive profiling. Evaluation with representative HPC workloads shows that Proteus achieves 91.30\% decision accuracy, delivering up to 3.24$\times$ and 2.9$\times$ speedups for write-intensive and metadata-intensive workloads, respectively.

### [62] [StickyInvoc: Rethinking Task Models for High-throughput Workflows in the LLM Era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22175)

*Thanh Son Phung,Douglas Thain*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** StickyInvoc提出了两种新型任务模型（sticky task和invocation task），通过解耦计算状态的创建与销毁，将LLM推理的昂贵状态初始化开销分摊到大量任务上，实现高吞吐工作流的显著加速。

#### Problem

传统HPC任务模型在LLM推理工作流中存在严重的"创建-销毁"开销：每个任务都必须从头创建包含多GB模型参数的计算状态（从存储到本地磁盘、CPU内存再到GPU内存），任务结束后再销毁，这一开销在数千任务的规模下构成了显著的性能瓶颈。

#### Key Idea

将计算状态的创建与执行解耦：让"sticky task"负责创建并持久化计算状态（但不执行实际计算），而后续的"invocation task"继承该状态执行实际推理，且退出时不销毁状态，从而将高昂的状态初始化成本分摊到大量推理请求上。

#### System/Method Design

StickyInvoc设计了两种新型任务模型：sticky task根据用户提供的模板在计算节点上创建持久化状态但不执行实质性计算；invocation task继承sticky task的状态执行实际LLM推理，退出时不销毁状态。两者形成共生关系，使得LLM模型参数可以一次加载、多次使用。

#### Experiments

在一个包含150k次推理的claim verification工作流上进行评估：在稳定的20 GPU测试平台上获得3.6倍加速；通过增量扩展到186个原本闲置的GPU，该工作流在仅784秒内完成。

#### Why It Matters

该工作针对LLM推理与HPC高吞吐工作流融合这一新兴领域的关键性能瓶颈，提出了一种轻量级、实用的任务模型改进方案，能够大幅降低推理工作流的启动开销，并有效利用HPC集群中异构、可抢占的空闲GPU资源。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。该工作聚焦于LLM推理在HPC集群上的系统级优化，针对的是LLM推理的高启动开销（模型参数加载）这一核心问题。虽然不涉及MoE架构本身，但其提出的状态持久化思想可推广到其他需要重复加载大模型的场景（如MoE模型的参数加载），也与推理加速、分布式资源调度、GPU利用率优化等系统研究方向密切相关。

#### Abstract

The integration of LLMs into high-throughput workflows is creating a new class of workloads on HPC clusters that promises to accelerate advances in scientific discovery with unprecedented generative capabilities. However, the traditional task model imposes a prohibitive overhead in this new domain: each task must create its computational state from scratch and destroy it upon completion. For each LLM inference task, this "create-destroy" model forces the repeated and costly transfer of multi-gigabyte model parameters from a long-term, reliable storage to a compute node's local disk, its CPU memory, and finally its GPU memory. This overhead, compounded by the inherently high startup cost of LLM inference, the typical scale of thousands of tasks in high-throughput workflows, and the heterogeneous and preemptible nature of high-throughput resources, presents a significant performance barrier.
  To overcome this barrier, this paper presents StickyInvoc: a symbiotic relationship between two new task models for high-throughput workflows. Specifically, a "sticky" task creates a persistent state on a compute node from a user-provided template, but doesn't execute any goodput computation by itself. Instead, this state is then inherited by subsequent "invocation" tasks, which perform the actual computation without incurring the state creation overhead or destroying the state upon exit. StickyInvoc thus allows the decoupling of the creation and destruction of computational states, allowing the computational state of LLM models to be created once per sticky task and its cost amortized over many subsequent invocation tasks. Our evaluation shows that when rewritten in the StickyInvoc paradigm, a claim verification workflow consisting of 150k inferences achieves a 3.6x speedup on a stable testbed with 20 GPUs, and completes in just 784 seconds by incrementally scaling out to 186 otherwise idle GPUs.

### [63] [FeLoG: Scalable and Efficient Distributed Graph Embedding with Feedback Loop Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22180)

*Peng Fang,Arijit Khan,Ziqiang Wu,Zhenli Li,Yibo Zhou,Fang Wang,Dan Feng*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** FeLoG是一个面向大规模分布式图嵌入的反馈循环驱动系统，通过将采样与训练反馈耦合、活动感知通信压缩和轮次交错流水线，实现了27.9倍的平均加速和53.1%以上的通信开销降低。

#### Problem

现有图嵌入框架在分布式环境下采用采样-训练分离范式，存在三个关键问题：(1) 采样与嵌入质量解耦，导致对已充分训练的节点进行冗余探索，而对未充分训练节点欠采样；(2) 解耦导致分布式环境中的过度通信、串行执行和低资源利用率。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察是在图嵌入的采样与训练之间引入反馈闭环，根据实时的嵌入质量反馈动态调整采样优先级，优先处理未充分训练的节点，从而减少冗余计算并加速收敛。

#### System/Method Design

FeLoG包含三个核心设计：(1) 反馈耦合的采样与训练——根据实时嵌入质量反馈动态优先采样未充分训练节点；(2) 活动感知通信——压缩频繁出现的节点序列以减少PCIe流量，选择性同步频繁更新的嵌入以减少机器间通信；(3) 轮次交错流水线——将下一轮的采样与当前轮次的训练重叠执行，提升CPU-GPU利用率。

#### Experiments

在大型图上与六个最先进的基线系统进行对比实验，FeLoG实现了平均27.9倍的加速，通信开销降低超过53.1%，CPU-GPU利用率维持在80%以上。

#### Why It Matters

该工作解决了大规模图嵌入在分布式场景下的采样-训练解耦这一根本性效率瓶颈，其反馈驱动思路具有通用性，为构建可扩展的高效图学习系统提供了新的设计范式，对工业级GraphRAG、推荐系统和欺诈检测等应用有实际价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/MoE/系统研究高度相关：(1) 其反馈耦合的训练调度思路可类比于MoE中专家负载均衡或LLM训练中的数据重要性采样；(2) 活动感知通信压缩策略可应用于分布式LLM训练/推理中的梯度压缩和KV缓存传输优化；(3) 轮次交错流水线设计对GPU集群中LLM推理的prefill-decode流水线优化有借鉴意义；(4) 图嵌入是GraphRAG的核心组件，直接影响RAG系统的检索效率和质量。

#### Abstract

Graph embedding maps graph nodes into low-dimensional vectors to support applications such as recommendation, fraud detection, and graph-based retrieval-augmented generation (GraphRAG). As graphs scale to billions of edges, scalable and efficient graph embedding has become increasingly important. Existing frameworks commonly adopt a sampling-training paradigm, in which mini-batches are constructed by sampling nodes and their neighbors. However, sampling is typically decoupled from evolving embedding quality, causing redundant exploration of well-trained regions while under-sampling undertrained nodes. At the system level, such decoupling further leads to excessive communication, serialized execution, and low resource utilization in distributed environments. We present FeLoG, a feedback loop-driven system for scalable distributed graph embedding. (1) FeLoG introduces feedback-coupled sampling and training, dynamically prioritizing undertrained nodes according to real-time embedding-quality feedback, thereby reducing redundant computation and accelerating convergence. (2) It employs activity-aware communication that compresses frequently occurring node sequences to reduce intra-machine PCIe traffic and selectively synchronizes frequently updated embeddings to reduce inter-machine communication. (3) It adopts a round-interleaved pipeline that overlaps next-round sampling with current-round training to improve CPU-GPU utilization. Experiments against six state-of-the-art baselines on large-scale graphs show that FeLoG achieves an average speedup of 27.9x, reduces communication cost by more than 53.1%, and sustains over 80% CPU-GPU utilization.

### [64] [Hardwired Pattern Formation by Mobile Robots with Common Unit Distance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22386)

*Yuta Kojima,Sébastien Tixeuil,Yukiko Yamauchi*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出了一种新的"硬连线模式形成"（HwPTF）问题，要求移动机器人在指定尺寸下形成目标图案，并研究了在 oblivious（无记忆）和不同同步假设下可解决性的边界条件。

#### Problem

传统的模式形成（PTF）问题允许对目标图案进行平移、旋转和缩放，但许多实际场景中需要机器人在精确的指定尺寸下形成图案，而现有工作未考虑这一约束。

#### Key Idea

将"指定尺寸"作为硬性约束引入模式形成问题，从而定义新的 HwPTF 问题，并系统研究在不同同步模型（半同步/异步）和机器人能力（有无记忆、有无灯光）下该问题的可解性。

#### System/Method Design

（1）针对两个 oblivious 半同步机器人，证明无法解决多重性为2的 HwPTF（即 rendezvous 问题），但可以在无多重性条件下求解 HwPTF。（2）针对两个 oblivious 异步机器人，证明其无法求解 HwPTF，但如果配备 lights（灯光）则可以求解。（3）针对超过4个 oblivious 半同步机器人，提出了一种尺寸调整算法，该算法可与现有模式形成算法结合，得到完整的 HwPTF 算法。

#### Experiments

摘要中未明确提供实验设置、基准方法、指标或数值结果。本文为理论性工作，以可解性证明（可能性/不可能性结果）为主要贡献。

#### Why It Matters

该工作将经典的模式形成问题推向更严格的实用设定，揭示了在强制尺寸约束下 obliviousness（无记忆性）和同步性对分布式机器人协调能力的影响，为分布式机器人系统的能力边界提供了理论刻画。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

本文的研究主题（移动机器人分布式协调与模式形成）与 LLM/MoE/系统研究方向无直接关联。不过，其中关于 oblivious vs. non-oblivious、同步 vs. 异步、有限状态通信（lights）对分布式问题可解性影响的分析，在分布式系统理论层面具有一定借鉴意义。

#### Abstract

The pattern formation (PTF) problem requires mobile robots to form a specified target pattern. Existing papers investigated the PTF problem and revealed the effect of obliviousness and synchronization on distributed coordination of mobile robots. However, the PTF problem allows translation, rotation, and scaling of the target pattern. In this paper, we introduce a novel pattern formation problem, called the hardwired pattern formation (HwPTF) problem that requires the robots to form a given target pattern in a specified size. Although two oblivious semi-synchronous robots cannot solve the HwPTF problem of multiplicity two (i.e., the rendezvous problem), we show that they can solve the HwPTF problem without multiplicity. We also show that two oblivious asynchronous robots equipped with lights can solve the HwPTF problem, while oblivious asynchronous robots cannot. We finally present a size-adjusting algorithm for more than four oblivious semi-synchronous robots, that yields a HwPTF algorithm when combined with some existing pattern formation algorithms.

### [65] [ASAP: A Disaggregated and Asynchronous Inference System for MoE Prefill](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22541)

*Weiwei Chen,Shuang Chen,Lele Li,Qiang Hu,Han Li,Xin Ye,Ming Yan,Zhibin Yu*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** ASAP 是一个专为 MoE 模型预填充阶段设计的异步推理系统，通过解耦注意力与 MoE 阶段并消除全局同步屏障，将 SLO 合规的预填充吞吐量提升 90%。

#### Problem

现代 MoE 服务系统采用 DP（数据并行）+ EP（专家并行）的混合并行策略，在在线服务中请求到达率和序列长度的方差会导致 DP 不均衡，引发严重的同步停滞（synchronization stalls），降低首 token 延迟（TTFT）和系统吞吐量。

#### Key Idea

将注意力阶段和 MoE 阶段的执行完全解耦，通过异步通信原语和协同优化消除全局同步屏障，实现完全异步的执行流水线。

#### System/Method Design

ASAP 包含：（1）解耦注意力与 MoE 阶段的全异步执行流水线；（2）一组专用的异步通信原语；（3）跨请求调度和模型执行的四个协同优化，共同消除全局同步屏障。

#### Experiments

在 CloudMatrix384 超级节点上实现和评估，与最先进的同步服务方案相比，SLO 合规的预填充吞吐量提升了 90%。

#### Why It Matters

该工作直接解决了 MoE 在线服务中因 DP 不均衡导致的同步开销问题，是首个针对 MoE 预填充阶段设计异步推理系统的方案，显著提升了吞吐量和效率。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关：核心针对 MoE 模型的服务系统，涉及 LLM 推理加速、预填充阶段优化、混合并行策略（DP+EP）的同步瓶颈、异步执行流水线、通信原语与调度优化，是典型的 LLM 系统研究工作。

#### Abstract

Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models have become the de facto standard for scaling large language models. To maintain computational efficiency, modern MoE serving systems typically employ a hybrid parallelism strategy, combining Data Parallelism (DP) for attention stages with Expert Parallelism (EP) for MoE stages. However, this design necessitates frequent global synchronization barriers between attention DP groups and experts. In online serving, significant variance in request arrival rates and sequence lengths inherently leads to DP imbalance, causing severe synchronization stalls that degrade Time-to-First-Token (TTFT) and system throughput. We present ASAP, an asynchronous inference system specifically designed to accelerate the prefill phase of MoE models. ASAP disaggregates the attention and MoE stages and implements a fully asynchronous execution pipeline. This is achieved through a suite of specialized asynchronous communication primitives and four coordinated optimizations across request scheduling and model execution, which collectively dismantle global synchronization barriers. We implement and evaluate ASAP on CloudMatrix384 super-nodes, demonstrating that it improves SLO-compliant prefill throughput by 90% compared to state-of-the-art synchronous serving solutions.

### [66] [EchoFlow: A Workload-Aware Parameter Tuning Method for Blockchain Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22934)

*Ben Lian,Linpeng Jia,Xing Chen,Xiaofeng Chen,Yi Sun*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** EchoFlow 提出了一种基于分布式强化学习和遗传算法的区块链参数自适应调优框架，可根据工作负载特征动态调整配置以持续优化系统性能。

#### Problem

区块链系统存在大量可调参数，但实践中通常对所有工作负载使用单一参数配置，导致大量性能潜力未被利用。

#### Key Idea

结合分布式强化学习（多个 actor 并行采样以加速样本生成）与遗传算法（训练初期生成高质量样本以加速收敛），实现参数配置对工作负载特征的自适应调整。

#### System/Method Design

EchoFlow 是一个参数调优框架，包含两个核心组件：(1) 分布式强化学习，多个 actor 并行执行采样，缓解区块链环境中样本生成耗时长的问题；(2) 遗传算法，在训练初始阶段生成高质量样本以加速收敛过程。

#### Experiments

在多种不同工作负载场景下进行实验评估，EchoFlow 在所有场景中均持续优于现有方法，同时训练时间更短。具体基线、指标和数据集未在摘要中明确说明。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为区块链系统的性能优化提供了自动化、自适应的参数调优方案，能够释放被单一静态配置所浪费的性能潜力，具有实际部署价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

间接相关。虽然本文聚焦区块链系统，但其提出的分布式强化学习 + 遗传算法加速参数调优的思路（多 actor 并行采样、高质量初始样本生成）可类比至 LLM 系统和 MoE 场景中的超参数自动调优、配置搜索空间优化等系统研究问题。

#### Abstract

Blockchain systems expose a large number of tunable parameters that significantly influence system performance. However, in practice, a single parameter configuration is often applied across different workloads, leaving substantial unexploited performance potential. To address this, we propose EchoFlow, a blockchain parameter tuning framework that adaptively adjusts parameter configurations based on workload characteristics, enabling continuous performance optimization. EchoFlow employs a distributed reinforcement learning approach in which multiple actors perform parallel sampling to mitigate the substantial time required for sample generation in blockchain environments. To further accelerate convergence, we introduce a genetic algorithm during the initial phase of training to generate high-quality samples. Extensive experimental evaluations demonstrate that EchoFlow consistently outperforms existing methods across diverse workload scenarios while also reducing training time, highlighting its effectiveness and practical value.

### [67] [Decentralized Operations of Decarbonized Chemical Plants with Renewable-driven Transmission Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22973)

*Richard Reed,kazi Arman Ahmed,Saba Ghasemi,Zheyu Jiang,Paritosh Ramanan*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** 提出一种基于数据隔离的隐私友好型去中心化框架，利用带辅助系统级惩罚项的ADMM算法，联合优化电力系统机组组合与电气化乙烷裂解装置微电网调度，在不泄露工厂敏感数据的前提下实现协同运行。

#### Problem

电气化乙烷裂解工厂微电网与脱碳电力系统的联合运行规划受到工厂运营数据高度保密性的阻碍，传统集中式优化方法无法在保护隐私的前提下实现跨系统的协同决策。

#### Key Idea

通过数据隔离实现各子系统独立求解本地子问题，仅共享极少的协调信号；采用交替方向乘子法（ADMM）并引入辅助系统级惩罚项加速收敛，在保护隐私的同时实现接近集中式优化的效果。

#### System/Method Design

提出一个隐私友好的去中心化优化框架：将电力系统机组组合（UC）和化工厂微电网调度分别作为独立的子系统，采用ADMM算法进行分布式求解；在标准ADMM基础上增加一个辅助系统级惩罚项以加速收敛；各子系统仅交换少量协调信号，无需共享敏感的内部运营数据。

#### Experiments

在ACTIVSg2000测试案例（德克萨斯输电网的合成模型）上进行数值实验，将德克萨斯州实际分布的26家化工厂映射到最近的电网连接点。实验衡量了数据隔离对联合决策最优性的代价，结果表明：数据隔离导致的最优性差距始终很小；排放影响具有负载依赖性且呈现非单调性。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为解决跨行业关键基础设施协同优化中的隐私保护难题提供了可行方案，量化了隐私保护分解在电力-化工联合系统中的实际代价，对推动工业电气化脱碳具有重要的工程实践意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该论文主要面向电力-化工系统协同优化，与LLM/MoE/系统研究方向无直接关联。但其提出的带辅助惩罚项的ADMM去中心化优化框架，在思想上可类比于分布式机器学习中的联邦学习或分布式训练优化，可能对大规模分布式系统的隐私保护协同优化有启发意义。

#### Abstract

Electrification of ethane cracking offers a promising pathway to industrial decarbonization, provided that the electricity is sourced from renewable energy. However, integrating electrified chemical plant microgrids with a decarbonized power grid requires joint operations planning between Independent System Operators and chemical plants, which is hindered by the highly confidential nature of plant operational data. In this paper, we propose a privacy-friendly decentralized framework based on data isolation that jointly optimizes the Unit Commitment problem in the power system and microgrid scheduling in electrified ethane cracker plants. The framework employs the Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers, augmented with an auxiliary system-level penalty that accelerates convergence, allowing each subsystem to solve its local subproblem and share only minimal coordination signals. To reflect real-world conditions, numerical experiments are conducted on the ACTIVSg2000 test case, a synthetic model of the Texas transmission network, with 26 chemical plants identified from Texas mapped to their nearest grid connection points. In doing so, we characterize the cost of privacy-friendly decomposition on joint power and chemical system decisions, showing that data isolation results in consistently small optimality gaps, and that its emissions consequences are load-dependent and non-monotone.

### [68] [LiveServe: Interaction-Aware Serving for Real-Time Omni-Modal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22983)

*Xiangyu Zhi,Peiqi Yin,Sheng Guan,Chenguang Zheng,James Cheng,Xiao Yan*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** LiveServe是一个面向实时全模态语言模型（Omni-LM）的交互感知服务系统，通过暴露音频播放进度、语音活动和打断事件来优化调度与KV缓存管理，显著降低音频首次令牌时间并提升吞吐量。

#### Problem

现有全模态LM服务系统仍沿用面向吞吐量的LLM调度策略和LRU KV缓存卸载策略，忽略了音频播放进度和跨轮次重用的特点。这导致：1) 系统生成远超出用户实际听到的令牌，用户在打断（barge-in）后大量工作被浪费；2) LRU策略将下一轮对话需要的KV状态提前逐出，影响后续轮次性能。

#### Key Idea

将交互感知（playback progress、speech activity、barge-in events）显式融入服务管线，让调度器和KV管理器能感知音频播放状态和用户语音活动，从而避免无效生成并实现智能化的KV预加载。

#### System/Method Design

LiveServe包含两个核心组件：1) 交互感知调度器：优先调度首音频（first-audio）和接近欠载（near-underrun）的会话，同时限制生成进度不超过播放前沿（playback frontier）；2) 交互感知KV管理器：采用"下次使用感知"（next-use-aware）的逐出策略，并在用户语音期间预加载下一轮可能需要的KV状态，以隐藏重载延迟。

#### Experiments

基于vLLM-Omni实现，在两种Omni-LM和混合工作负载下评估。主要结果：P90音频TTFP（首次令牌时间）平均降低1.55倍，最多2.21倍；已完成请求吞吐量平均提升1.15倍，最多1.56倍；大部分KV重载工作被移出下一轮对话的关键路径。

#### Why It Matters

该工作针对实时语音交互场景中Omni-LM服务效率的低效问题（过度生成和KV重用差），首次将交互感知引入系统设计，对构建真正可用的实时语音对话系统具有重要实践价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。1) LLM推理系统：提出了超越传统吞吐量导向调度的交互感知调度策略；2) KV缓存管理：提出了next-use-aware逐出策略和基于语音活动的预加载，解决了多轮对话中KV重用的延迟问题；3) 实时系统：将音频播放进度作为调度信号，减少无效生成（wasted work），对构建低延迟交互式LLM服务有直接参考价值。

#### Abstract

Realtime omni-modal LMs support speech-centric conversations where users stream inputs, hear generated audio, and interrupt freely. Existing Omni-LM serving systems still rely on throughput-oriented LLM scheduling and LRU KV offloading. These policies ignore audio playback and multi-turn reuse: they may generate tokens far beyond what users hear, wasting work after barge-in, and evict KV state needed in the next turn. LiveServe is an interaction-aware serving system for realtime Omni-LM interaction. It exposes playback progress, speech activity, and barge-in events to the serving pipeline. The scheduler prioritizes first-audio and near-underrun sessions while limiting generation beyond the playback frontier. The KV manager uses next-use-aware eviction and preloads likely-needed KV during user speech to hide reload latency. On vLLM-Omni, LiveServe improves realtime serving across two Omni-LMs and mixed workloads. It lowers P90 audio TTFP by $1.55\times$ on average and up to $2.21\times$, while improving completed-request throughput by $1.15\times$ on average and up to $1.56\times$, and moves most KV reload work off the next-turn critical path.

### [69] [Nautilus: A Verifiable Hierarchical Federated Learning Framework for Vehicular-Edge-Cloud Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23017)

*Linyang Wu,Linpeng Jia,Hanwen Zhang,Tiantian Duan,Yi Sun*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** Nautilus 是一个面向车联网（IoV）场景的联邦学习框架，通过多维资源感知调度和零知识证明机制，在提升训练效率的同时保障调度公平性和客户端执行的隐私可验证性。

#### Problem

车联网中车-边-云资源的极端异构性严重限制了联邦学习的系统效率，且动态调度策略引入了新的信任问题：如何在不泄露隐私的前提下，验证调度决策的公平性以及客户端是否忠实执行了优化指令。

#### Key Idea

将多维资源感知的动态调度与零知识证明相结合，在提升异构环境下联邦学习训练效率的同时，提供调度公平性和客户端合规性的可验证隐私保护机制。

#### System/Method Design

Nautilus 包含两个核心组件：(1) 多维资源感知调度算法，根据车辆的带宽、延迟和计算能力动态分配压缩比和训练任务，以提升系统训练效率；(2) 零知识证明（ZKP）机制，确保调度策略生成的公平性和客户端执行的合规性，同时保护隐私数据不被泄露。

#### Experiments

实验结果表明该框架能有效降低通信开销并加速模型收敛，同时保持系统完整性。但摘要未提供具体的数据集、基线方法或量化结果。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次在车联网联邦学习场景中同时解决了异构资源调度带来的效率问题和信任问题，为隐私保护下的分布式机器学习系统提供了兼顾效率与可验证性的新范式。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM系统研究的交叉点：联邦学习中的通信压缩、异构资源调度和隐私验证技术可类比应用于分布式LLM训练/推理场景。零知识证明机制为模型训练中的隐私合规验证提供思路。但本文聚焦车联网场景，未涉及MoE架构或大模型特有挑战。

#### Abstract

Federated Learning (FL) enables privacy-preserving collaborative learning for Internet of Vehicles (IoV) scenarios, but the extreme heterogeneity of vehicular-edge-cloud resources severely limits system efficiency. While dynamic scheduling strategies can mitigate this issue, they introduce new trust concerns: how to verify that scheduling decisions are fair, and whether clients faithfully execute optimization instructions without disclosing private data? This paper proposes Nautilus, a verifiable and efficient federated learning framework. First, we design a multi-dimensional resource-aware scheduling algorithm that dynamically allocates compression ratios and training tasks based on vehicles bandwidth, latency, and computing power, significantly improving system training efficiency. Second, to address the trust deficit in the scheduling process, we introduce a Zero-Knowledge Proof (ZKP) mechanism that ensures the fairness of scheduling strategy generation and the compliance of client execution while preserving privacy. Experimental results demonstrate that the framework effectively reduces communication overhead and accelerates model convergence while maintaining system integrity.

### [70] [Solving Approximate Agreement on continuous and discrete spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23260)

*Augustin Albert,Sergio Rajsbaum*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** 本文研究了异步进程崩溃场景下近似一致问题的可解性条件，给出了连续空间（CUB空间）和离散空间（单纯复形）中该问题的充要可解性刻画。

#### Problem

在异步进程可能崩溃、通过共享读写寄存器通信的环境中，近似一致（Approximate Agreement）问题的可解性依赖于输入空间的性质、有效性条件以及进程数量。之前的研究对不同的输入空间（连续、离散、一维、多维）给出了不同的结果，但缺乏统一的刻画框架，尤其是当输入空间为一般度量空间或单纯复形时，可解性的精确条件尚不明确。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察是将近似一致问题联系到输入空间的拓扑连通性（特别是单纯复形的(n-1)-连通性），并引入CUB空间（一种具有唯一凸性定义的广义度量空间）来统一刻画连续情形下的可解性。

#### System/Method Design

论文从拓扑学角度分析近似一致问题。在连续情形下，定义了CUB空间（包含经典的一维ε-一致和m维近似一致），证明了ε-一致问题在所有CUB空间上都是可解的。在离散情形下（输入为单纯复形），采用单纯形有效性（simplex validity）条件——若输入张成单形σ，则输出必须在σ内；一致性要求输出张成一个单形——证明了对于n+1个进程，单纯形近似一致在单纯复形C上可解当且仅当C是(n-1)-连通的。

#### Experiments

摘要中未明确提供实验细节。论文给出了一些推论性结果，例如：平面上对所有n可解，但移除一个点后只对n≤2可解；对于图结构，n=2时可解当且仅当图连通，n≥3时要求图无环（acyclic）。此外还证明了一个Ledent猜想。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为异步分布式系统中近似一致问题的可解性提供了拓扑学层面的充要条件，统一并推广了此前分散在不同输入空间上的结果。这对于理解分布式共识问题的理论边界具有重要意义，并且证明了Ledent猜想。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

本文属于分布式计算理论范畴（异步进程、崩溃容错、共享内存），与LLM/MoE/推理加速等系统研究的直接关联较弱。但其对分布式一致性问题的拓扑刻画可能为分布式训练中的共识协议（如梯度聚合的去中心化近似一致）提供理论洞见。

#### Abstract

We consider $n$ asynchronous processes prone to crashes, communicating via shared read-write registers, and study the wait-free solvability of approximate agreement: given inputs, processes must output values that are close to each other, and satisfy a validity property. At the very least, if inputs are identical, all outputs must equal that input.
  The problem has been studied for various input spaces: continuous, discrete, one-dimensional or multidimensional. For metric spaces, validity requires outputs to lie in the convex hull of the inputs. For graphs, and more generally simplicial complexes, several conditions exist. We focus on simplex validity: if inputs span a simplex $σ$, then outputs are in $σ$. Agreement requires that outputs span a simplex.
  Solvability depends on the input space, validity condition, and number of processes. For example, the problem is solvable for all $n$ in the plane, but only for $n \leq 2$ when removing a point. For a graph, solvability for $n=2$ holds iff the graph is connected, but $n\geq 3$ requires acyclicity.
  In the continuous setting, we consider CUB spaces: a broad class of metric spaces admitting a unique convexity definition, subsuming classical $ε$-agreement on $[0,1]$ and $m$-dimensional approximate agreement. Our results show that $ε$-agreement is solvable in every CUB space. In the discrete case, we prove that simplex agreement on a simplicial complex $\mathcal{C}$ is solvable for $n+1$ processes iff $\mathcal{C}$ is $(n-1)$-connected. We discuss several consequences, including a proof of a conjecture by Ledent.

### [71] [When Staking Rewards Compound: Measuring the Impact of Ethereum's Pectra Upgrade](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23337)

*Mohammed Benseddik,Benjamin Kraner,Claudio J. Tessone*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** 本文通过模拟和实证分析，研究了以太坊Pectra升级引入的0x02复利验证者机制对共识层奖励、执行层优势以及不同质押者类型迁移意愿的影响。

#### Problem

以太坊信标链因32 ETH的历史质押上限导致验证者数量超过92万，造成网络效率低下。Pectra升级虽将最大质押额提升至2048 ETH并引入自动复利，但迁移至新型0x02验证者的经济激励和实际障碍尚不明确。

#### Key Idea

通过模拟和实证数据，系统分析0x02复利验证者在共识层APR提升中的边际效应递减规律，并结合不同质押者类型（个人质押者与大型服务商）的采纳行为，揭示经济激励与操作障碍之间的权衡。

#### System/Method Design

结合模拟（simulation）与实证分析（empirical analysis）：模拟不同余额规模下的共识层APR提升幅度，并对信标链所有活跃验证者的链上数据进行实证分析，比较0x02与传统验证者的中位CL APR差异。同时分析个人质押者与质押服务商的采纳模式、整合行为及迁移障碍。

#### Experiments

模拟显示：小额验证者复利带来约+5%的相对共识层APR提升，大型质押服务商提升幅度降至1%以下。实证分析：0x02验证者的中位CL APR略高于传统验证者。个人质押者的相对采纳率更高，但面临操作障碍；服务商则受限于基础设施成本和协议约束。

#### Why It Matters

该研究为以太坊网络效率优化提供了关键实证依据，揭示了复利机制的经济激励边际递减特性，并指出了在缺乏更强的奖励可访问性和经济激励时，网络效率提升的迁移将进展缓慢。对以太坊未来协议设计、质押经济模型和去中心化治理具有重要参考价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

相关性较低。本文主要关注以太坊区块链的共识层机制设计与质押经济模型，不涉及LLM系统、MoE、推理加速、KV缓存、分布式系统或计算机架构等研究方向。

#### Abstract

Ethereum's beacon chain hosts over 920,000 active validators, a number inflated by the legacy 32 ETH stake cap. The Pectra upgrade (May 2025) addresses this by introducing 0x02 compounding validators, raising the maximum stake per validator from 32 to 2,048 ETH and enabling automatic reward reinvestment. This paper examines how compounding affects consensus-layer rewards, whether higher balances provide execution-layer advantages, and whether the APR uplift justifies migration for different staker types. We analyse adoption patterns across solo stakers and staking providers, investigate the role of consolidation (merging multiple 32 ETH validators into one) in early migration, and identify barriers slowing the transition. Through simulation, we find that compounding provides roughly +5% relative consensus-layer APR uplift for small balances, diminishing to under 1% for large staking providers. Empirical analysis of all active beacon chain validators shows 0x02 validators achieving modestly higher median CL APR. Solo stakers show higher relative adoption but face operational barriers, whilst providers cite infrastructure costs and protocol constraints. The results suggest that without improved reward accessibility and stronger economic incentives, 0x02 migration will remain gradual despite its network efficiency benefits.

### [72] [Development and Design of FLKit: A Structured Onboarding Toolkit for Federated Learning in Health and Life Sciences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23500)

*Ashkan Pirmani,Ilse Vermeulen,Goran Vinterhalter,Lotte Geys,Axel Faes,Muhammad Quamber Ali,Nishkala Sattanathan,Geert Vandeweyer,Yves Moreau,Liesbet M. Peeters*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** FLKit 是一个面向生命科学领域联邦学习项目的开源入门工具包，通过角色感知的入口点和结构化生命周期，帮助多学科团队克服联邦学习的实践启动障碍。

#### Problem

联邦学习方法和框架正在快速成熟，但实际障碍出现在更早的阶段：一个启动联邦项目的团队面对的是分散的工具、治理义务和陌生角色，没有适合其背景的、结构化的入门起点。

#### Key Idea

借鉴 ELIXIR 研究数据管理工具包的经验，设计一个面向多学科团队（临床、法律、治理、技术）的联邦学习全生命周期入门工具包，为每个贡献者提供角色感知的入口点，而非要求所有成员精通所有领域。

#### System/Method Design

FLKit 包含四个生命周期阶段（治理、基础设施、数据处理、分析）、11 个角色特定的入口点、跨学科术语表、可复用的 FAIR 对齐的 FL Story 模板（用于规划和记录项目），以及一个经过筛选的工具/框架/社区目录。

#### Experiments

自 2024 年 12 月演示以来，FLKit 已扩展到 8 个章节共 39 页，包含 7 个 FL Stories（记录已完成和进行中的项目），涵盖多发性硬化症残疾预测、炎症性肠病、基因组学和脑机接口等领域。工具包由多学科核心团队开发，并得到外部从业者的反馈验证。

#### Why It Matters

这项工作的意义在于解决了联邦学习在敏感数据共享场景（如医疗健康）中的实践启动瓶颈。它降低了一个需要临床、法律、治理和技术多方协作的领域中的入门门槛，为跨学科团队提供了可操作的起点，有望加速联邦学习在生命科学领域的实际采用。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该论文主要聚焦联邦学习的实践入门，而非 LLM/MoE 系统或推理加速等底层技术。但联邦学习作为分布式训练的一种范式，与分布式系统和隐私保护计算有共通之处。对于 LLM 系统研究而言，其"角色感知入口点"和"全生命周期管理"的设计思路可启发面向多方参与的分布式训练系统的工程落地和流程标准化。

#### Abstract

Federated learning lets institutions train shared models without moving their data, which makes it a natural fit for health and life sciences research under strict privacy regulation. The methods are maturing fast, but the practical barrier now comes earlier: a team starting a federated project meets a scattered mix of frameworks, governance obligations, and unfamiliar roles, with no structured place to begin that fits its own background. FLKit closes that gap. It is an open, community-maintained onboarding toolkit that takes a multidisciplinary team through the full federated learning lifecycle and gives every contributor, clinical, legal, governance, or technical, a role-aware entry point instead of assuming fluency across all four. We modeled it on the ELIXIR Research Data Management Kit and built it with a multidisciplinary core team, a wider consortium supplying milestone reviews and roadmap direction, and external practitioners interviewed to keep the content grounded in real practice. FLKit sits on four lifecycle stages, Governance, Infrastructure, Wrangling, and Analysis, and connects them through 11 role-specific entry points, a cross-disciplinary glossary, a reusable FAIR-aligned FL Story template for planning and documenting projects, and a curated directory of tools, frameworks, and communities. Since the December 2024 demo it has grown to 39 pages across eight sections, with seven FL Stories documenting completed and ongoing projects in multiple sclerosis disability prediction, inflammatory bowel disease, genomics, and brain-computer interfaces. It is openly available at https://uhasselt-biomedicaldatasciences.github.io/federated-learning-toolkit/ and welcomes contributions from across the life sciences.

### [73] [Concordia: JIT-Compiled Persistent-Kernel Checkpointing for Fault-Tolerant LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23521)

*Yuhang Gan,Yiwei Yang,Yuyi Li,Xiangyu Gao,Yichen Wang,Rain Jiang,Xiaoning Ding,Andi Quinn,Chen Qian*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** Concordia 提出了一种基于 GPU 驻留持久化内核的运行时系统，通过设备级检查点钩子实现 LLM 代理工作负载的容错，无需主机 CPU 介入关键路径。

#### Problem

长时间运行的 LLM 代理（如 KV 缓存、请求调度器、通信状态、在线适配器）将宝贵状态保留在 GPU 上，GPU 或通信故障会导致数分钟到数小时的工作丢失。现有恢复机制要么重启整个服务栈，要么需要在每个注意力组件和运行时组件中实现应用特定的检查点逻辑。

#### Key Idea

容错需要 GPU 驻留的执行上下文：检查点钩子必须在设备同步点执行，观察框架和库实际执行的二进制内核，并且恢复过程不将主机 CPU 置于关键路径上。

#### System/Method Design

Concordia 利用设备驻留持久化内核作为容错 LLM 推理的底层基座。它拦截 GPU 模块加载，支持 PTX 和 SASS 级别的插桩，在框架代码和库边界之下插入检查点和暂停钩子。对每个注册的 LLM 状态区域，Concordia JIT 编译专门的增量检查点处理器（如 KV 块扫描器、适配器页扫描器、恢复应用器），并热替换到持久化内核的操作符表中。持久化内核使用无锁环形缓冲区处理计算、检查点、追加日志和恢复任务，同一始终在线的执行器触发脏页检测、暂存增量数据，并将已提交记录追加到 CXL 内存或主机 DRAM 中的 CPU 可见日志。

#### Experiments

摘要中未明确描述实验设置、基线、指标和数值结果。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次提出了一种无需主机 CPU 在关键路径上的 GPU 驻留容错方案，通过持久化内核和 PTX/SASS 级插桩，在不修改上层框架和库的情况下实现对 LLM 代理状态的低开销检查点与恢复，对提升长周期 LLM 服务的可靠性具有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。直接针对 LLM 推理系统中 KV 缓存、调度器状态、在线适配器等 GPU 驻留状态的容错问题；涉及 GPU 内核级插桩、持久化内核设计、无锁环形缓冲区任务调度、CXL 内存/主机 DRAM 日志机制；对 MoE 系统中多个专家的状态恢复同样具有潜在适用性，属于 LLM 推理系统可靠性与底层 GPU 系统软件方向的重要贡献。

#### Abstract

Long-running LLM agents keep valuable state resident on GPUs: KV caches, request schedulers, communication state, and sometimes online adapters. Losing this state after a GPU or communicator failure can discard minutes to hours of work, yet existing recovery mechanisms either restart the whole serving stack or require application-specific checkpoint logic inside every attention and runtime component. This paper argues that fault tolerance for such workloads needs a GPU-resident execution context: checkpoint hooks must run at device synchronization points, observe binary kernels that frameworks and libraries actually execute, and recover without putting the host CPU on the critical path.
  We present Concordia, a runtime that uses a device-resident persistent kernel as the substrate for fault-tolerant LLM inference. Concordia interposes on GPU module loading and supports PTX- and SASS-level instrumentation, allowing checkpoint and pause hooks to be inserted below framework code and library boundaries. For each registered LLM state region, Concordia JIT-compiles a specialized delta-checkpoint handler -- for example, a KV-block scanner, adapter-page scanner, or recovery applier -- and hot-swaps it into the persistent kernel's operator table. The persistent kernel consumes a lock-free ring buffer of compute, checkpoint, append-log, and recovery tasks, so the same always-on executor triggers dirty-page detection, stages deltas, and appends committed records to a CPU-visible log in CXL memory or host DRAM.

### [74] [Kamera: Unified Position-Invariant Multimodal KV Cache for Training-Free Reuse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23581)

*Bole Ma,Jan Eitzinger,Harald Koestler,Gerhard Wellein*

Main category: `cs.DC`

**TL;DR:** 提出了一个免训练的低秩条件补丁（conditioning patch）方法，修复了位置无关KV缓存复用中丢失的跨块绑定信息，从而避免多模态agent在滑动窗口和迭代推理中对相同视觉帧的重复编码。

#### Problem

多模态agent在上下文窗口滑动或迭代推理时，反复回看相同的视频帧、UI截图等视觉内容，但由于前缀缓存仅服务于固定起始位置，每次回看都需要从零开始重新编码，造成了大量计算浪费。

#### Key Idea

跨块条件绑定（cross-chunk conditioning）的丢失是不对称的：直接读出可以通过标准状态合并精确恢复，但深层隐藏的扩散低秩残差会被盲复用法丢失，这正是多跳推理所需的关键信息。通过一个低秩补丁即可恢复这种绑定。

#### System/Method Design

提出一个轻量级、免训练的低秩条件补丁（low-rank conditioning patch），存储在每个位置无关的chunk旁边。复用时只需一个算子（兼容MLA、GQA、MHA）：精确的RoPE重旋转到任意目标位置，加上恢复跨块绑定的补丁。该方案支持三种窗口操作：重排序（一个补丁服务缓存集的任意排序）、滑动窗口存活（存活块仅通过旋转重定位，零重新编码）、召回（被驱逐的块通过补丁恢复，无需重新编码）。

#### Experiments

在跨块绑定基准MM-NIAH（覆盖两种注意力家族和两页文档QA）上，rank-m的补丁以极小的KV占用恢复了完整任务精度；在SGLang生产内核上，跨6个骨干网络的重构KV精度达到bf16舍入误差级别。

#### Why It Matters

揭示了位置无关KV缓存复用在跨块绑定上的失效模式，并给出了极低成本的修复方案，对多模态agent这类频繁回看视觉内容的场景具有显著效率提升潜力。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。（1）KV缓存优化：提出了一种免训练的低秩补丁方法，兼容主流注意力机制（MLA/GQA/MHA），大幅减少重复编码开销；（2）推理加速：通过旋转+补丁实现滑动窗口存活、召回等操作，零重新编码；（3）多模态系统：针对多模态agent反复回看视频/截图的重计算瓶颈给出了针对性方案；（4）系统实现：在SGLang生产内核上验证了精度达到bf16级别。

#### Abstract

Multimodal agents repeatedly re-examine the same video frames, UI screenshots, and rendered artifacts as their context window slides and reasoning iterates, yet every look-back re-encodes from scratch, because prefix caches serve reuse only at a fixed leading position. We show this recompute is avoidable, and identify exactly what naive KV reuse loses: the cross-chunk conditioning a chunk absorbs from its neighbours. This loss is asymmetric. The direct readout of a cached chunk is recovered exactly and for free by the standard state-merge. What remains is a diffuse, low-rank residue concentrated in deep layers, invisible to single-hop retrieval but precisely what multi-hop reasoning binds on. Blind reuse therefore leaves single-hop recall intact while halving multi-hop accuracy; this is the failure mode prior position-independent caches, designed for single-context or single-image reuse, do not address. We repair it with a small, training-free low-rank conditioning patch stored alongside each position-free chunk. Reuse reduces to one operator across MLA, GQA, and MHA: exact RoPE re-rotation to any target position, plus the patch that restores cross-chunk binding. This makes three window operations cheap: reorder (one patch serves every ordering of a cached set), sliding-window survival (surviving chunks relocate via rotation only, zero re-encode), and recall (an evicted chunk is rehydrated by its patch, never re-encoded). A rank-m patch recovers full task accuracy on cross-chunk-binding benchmarks, MM-NIAH across two attention families and two-page doc-QA, at a fraction of the KV footprint, and reconstructs re-prefill KV to within bf16 rounding in a production SGLang kernel across six backbones. The conditioning signal is strongest in redundant vision and video streams, making our solution most impactful where multimodal agents spend their recompute budget.

### [75] [Does Mixture-of-Experts Actually Help Inference on Consumer and Edge Hardware? An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21428)

*Alfarizy Alfarizy,Hung Truong Thanh Nguyen,René Richard,Roozbeh Razavi-Far,Hung Cao*

Main category: `cs.PF`

**TL;DR:** 通过在实际消费级和边缘硬件上对比基准测试，本文发现MoE语言模型的稀疏激活优势在带宽受限设备上大幅减弱，推理成本更接近总参数量而非活跃参数量。

#### Problem

MoE语言模型常被声称在资源受限推理场景中具有FLOPs优势，即每个token仅激活少量专家，计算量接近更小的稠密模型。但这种理论FLOP优势在实际硬件上是否能转化为真实的吞吐、能耗和内存优势尚不清楚。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察是：在带宽受限的边缘硬件上，推理成本主要跟踪总参数量而非活跃参数量，稀疏激活并不能弥补设备所缺乏的带宽资源。路由开销本身占比很小（<9%），性能差距主要来自总参数内存占用、专家分发和KV cache压力。

#### System/Method Design

在Apple M2 Pro（笔记本）和NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano 8 GB（边缘设备）上，通过llama.cpp基准测试框架，将OLMoE-1B-7B（活跃1.3B / 总6.9B）与三个稠密基线模型进行对比，测量吞吐量、内存占用和片上能耗。并通过对llama.cpp打补丁，对解码图进行逐节点计时以分析计算瓶颈。

#### Experiments

对比OLMoE-1B-7B与三个稠密基线模型。在Apple M2 Pro上，OLMoE比同等活跃参数量的Llama-3.2-1B慢约10%；在NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano上，OLMoE落后约31%，每token能耗为2.1倍，峰值内存触及8GB上限。逐节点分析表明路由开销在边缘后端的MoE块中占比不到9%。

#### Why It Matters

这项工作挑战了MoE模型在资源受限设备上天然高效的普遍假设，揭示了稀疏激活理论优势与硬件实际瓶颈之间的关键差距。对边缘部署MoE模型的设计（如专家分配策略、内存优化）有重要指导意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关：核心主题是MoE模型在实际硬件上的推理性能评估。涉及LLM推理加速、内存/KV cache压力分析、带宽受限硬件上的系统优化、以及MoE架构的工程落实现实（专家分发、总参数内存占用）。对分布式系统和计算机架构中内存带宽与计算效率的权衡有启示意义。

#### Abstract

Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) language models are often described as ideal for resource-constrained inference. Each token activates only a small subset of experts, so the per-token compute cost, in floating-point operations (FLOPs), resembles that of a much smaller dense model. Whether that FLOP advantage survives in practice is far less clear. We ask whether MoE models actually run faster and cheaper than comparable dense models on consumer-grade and edge hardware. We benchmark OLMoE-1B-7B (1.3 B active of 6.9 B total) against three dense baselines on an Apple M2 Pro and an NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano 8 GB through llama.cpp, measuring throughput, memory, and on-device energy. The answer is device-dependent: OLMoE's active-parameter advantage is only partly realised on the laptop (~10% behind the same-active Llama-3.2-1B) and erodes on the edge device (~31% behind, at 2.1$\times$ the energy per token, with peak memory at the 8 GB ceiling). Patching llama.cpp to time the decode graph node-by-node shows routing accounts for under 9% of MoE-block compute on the cleaner edge backend, so the gap reflects total-parameter memory footprint, expert dispatch, and KV-cache pressure rather than routing. The implication is that on bandwidth-bound edge hardware, inference cost tracks total parameters, not active ones, and sparse activation does not buy back what the device is constrained on. These findings are bounded to one MoE model at this parameter scale and two devices, and we release the full measurement harness and per-run data.

### [76] [Enabling Cloud-Level Accuracy in Edge AI through IoT Data Preprocessing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22496)

*Aygün Varol,Katarzyna Kołodziej,Łukasz Sobczak,Michał Romaszewski,Przemysław Głomb,Naser Hossein Motlagh,Mirka Leino,Johanna Virkki*

Main category: `cs.PF`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出一种结构化提示构建框架，通过在提示端对原始传感器数据进行分层次文本化预处理，显著提升本地小模型在物联网环境监测任务中的数值推理准确率，同时保持低延迟。

#### Problem

云端部署大语言模型在智能物联网环境中存在延迟高、隐私风险和连接性问题；而本地边缘小模型在面对原始传感器数值时数值推理能力较弱，导致准确率低下。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察在于：通过对原始传感器数据进行提示端的结构化预处理（逐步丰富的文本化表示：原始值→阈值感知描述→环境摘要标志），可以显著提升小模型的数值推理能力，从而在不增加模型复杂度的情况下改善准确率-延迟权衡。

#### System/Method Design

提出一种结构化提示构建框架，将原始空气质量与热舒适度传感器测量值转化为三种逐步丰富的文本表示：1) 原始数值（raw values）；2) 阈值感知描述（threshold-aware descriptions，基于阈值的定性描述）；3) 紧凑的环境摘要标志（compact environmental summary flags）。构建了二值LLM查询数据集，覆盖空气质量、热舒适度及联合环境条件三类任务。

#### Experiments

使用芬兰坦佩雷大学的室内Raspberry Pi/BME680数据集，以及赫尔辛基、卡托维兹、华沙的室外空气质量数据集。评估5个本地LLM和5个云端LLM，涉及3种提示变体、2种推理模式（有无思维链CoT）。主要结果：在无CoT模式下，本地模型准确率在室内从50.9%提升至81.7%，在室外从63.7%提升至89.3%。本地无CoT推理平均延迟约0.22秒，为最快配置；CoT显著增加推理时间。

#### Why It Matters

该工作表明轻量级的提示端预处理可以显著缩小本地小模型与云端大模型之间的性能差距，为低延迟、保护隐私的物联网边缘智能分析提供了一条实用且低成本的路径，无需修改模型本身或增加计算资源。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该论文直接涉及LLM系统研究中的推理效率与边缘部署问题：1) LLM推理加速——通过提示预处理而非模型压缩来优化准确率-延迟权衡；2) 边缘部署——研究本地小模型在资源受限设备上的实际延迟（~0.22s）；3) 系统设计——将数据预处理从模型内部移到提示端的架构思路，对MoE等稀疏模型的输入优化也有参考价值。

#### Abstract

Large language models (LLMs) offer a natural-language interface for interpreting Internet of Things (IoT) sensor data in smart environments; however, cloud deployment introduces latency, privacy, and connectivity concerns. Local LLMs can reduce these limitations, but compact edge-deployable models often show weaker numerical reasoning when raw sensor readings are provided directly. This paper investigates whether prompt-side preprocessing can improve the accuracy-latency trade-off of local LLMs for environmental monitoring. We propose a structured prompt construction framework that transforms raw air-quality and thermal-comfort measurements into progressively enriched textual representations: raw sensor values, threshold-aware descriptions, and compact environmental summary flags. The approach is evaluated using indoor Raspberry Pi/BME680 datasets from Tampere University and outdoor air-quality datasets from Helsinki, Katowice, and Warsaw. We construct a binary LLM query dataset covering air quality, thermal comfort, and joint environmental conditions, and evaluate five local and five cloud LLMs across three prompt variants and two inference modes, with and without chain-of-thought prompting. Results show that prompt enrichment substantially improves local-model accuracy. In No-CoT mode, local accuracy increases from 50.9% to 81.7% indoors and from 63.7% to 89.3% outdoors from the raw to the most enriched prompt. Local No-CoT inference is the fastest configuration, with mean latency close to 0.22 s, while CoT substantially increases inference time. These findings suggest that lightweight prompt-side preprocessing can narrow the local--cloud performance gap and support low-latency IoT analytics in smart environments.

### [77] [AOHP: An Open-Source OS-Level Agent Harness for Personalized, Efficient and Secure Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23449)

*Shanhui Zhao,Jiacheng Liu,Guohong Liu,Jichao Yan,Jialei Ye,Yuhao Yang,Hao Wen,Shizuo Tian,Yizhen Yuan,Yuxuan Chen,Yunxin Liu,Ju Ren,Ya-Qin Zhang,Chao Huang,Yao Guo,Yuanchun Li*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 提出 AOHP，一个基于 Android Open Source Project 构建的代理原生操作系统测试平台，将 AI 代理视为操作系统的一等公民，实现自适应 UI 和代理友好的运行时环境。

#### Problem

现有终端操作系统以应用为中心设计，对 AI 代理的原生支持不足，导致执行开销大、安全风险高，限制了代理的广泛应用。

#### Key Idea

将 AI 代理视为操作系统的一等公民（first-class OS actors），从底层系统机制层面为代理提供原生支持，而非在现有系统上打补丁。

#### System/Method Design

基于 AOSP 构建的代理原生操作系统；包含三个核心机制：个性化服务组合（personalized service composition）、高效代理接口（efficient agent interfaces）、安全信息流（secure information flow）。

#### Experiments

在覆盖 OS 代理关键能力的挑战性任务上进行初步实验，对比指标包括：任务完成率提升 21.12%，Token 成本降低 51.55%，以及在安全策略合规性上表现更优。

#### Why It Matters

为研究社区提供了首个开放的代理原生操作系统测试平台，有助于探索 AI 代理与操作系统交互的架构原语，推动代理在实际系统中的安全高效部署。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关：涉及 LLM 驱动的 AI 代理与操作系统的系统级集成，关注执行效率（Token 成本降低）和安全机制，属于大模型系统研究与操作系统交叉方向。

#### Abstract

AI agents are driving a new software paradigm, with the ability to autonomously call tools, extract information, manage memory, and complete tasks that span applications and data sources. Most existing end-user operating systems, however, are designed for application-centric workflows and offer little native support for AI agents. This mismatch limits the wider adoption of agents and leads to execution overhead and safety risks when running agents on conventional systems. While the concept of agent-native operating systems is emerging, the research community lacks an open testbed to explore the architectural primitives desired for agent-mediated interaction. We present AOHP (Android Open Harness Project), an OS-level agent harness built on the Android Open Source Project (AOSP). The core design principle of AOHP is to treat agents as first-class OS actors, enabling adaptive user interfaces and agent-friendly runtime environments. AOHP preserves the mature Android software and hardware ecosystem while introducing three agent-oriented system mechanisms: personalized service composition, efficient agent interfaces, and secure information flow. Based on preliminary experiments on challenging tasks covering key capabilities of OS agents, AOHP shows clear advantages in task completion (+21.12% completion rate), execution cost (-51.55% token cost), and security-policy compliance.

### [78] [On the Identifiability of User Adaptation in Co-Adaptive Neural Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20569)

*Philip Waggoner*

#### Problem

在共适应人机系统中，闭环系统的编码器估计无法唯一地识别用户的适应行为，导致对行为适应的解释存在歧义和混淆。

#### Key Idea

闭环编码器估计反映的是人机联合系统的整体属性，而非单纯的用户适应特性，因此不能作为用户行为的唯一标识。

#### System/Method Design

论文未提出具体系统或算法，而是从理论层面分析了共适应人机系统中闭环编码器估计的可辨识性问题，并提出了实现辨识的条件。

#### Experiments

摘要中未明确说明具体的实验设置、基线、指标或定量结果。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

#### Abstract

We analyze identifiability in co-adaptive human-machine systems. We show that closed-loop encoder estimates do not uniquely identify user adaptation, but instead reflect properties of the joint system. We discuss implications for interpreting behavioral adaptation and propose conditions for identification.

### [79] [Beyond Fixed Budgets: Characterizing the Inelasticity and Limitations of Tree-of-Thought Reasoning Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20599)

*Atkia Mahila,Avinash Maurya,M. Mustafa Rafique,Bogdan Nicolae*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 本文系统评估了两种Tree of Thought搜索方法（DPTS和SSDP）在不同计算预算、模型规模和问题难度下的表现，揭示了二者在低预算下的冷启动瓶颈和前沿耗尽问题，并指出需要自适应搜索策略。

#### Problem

Tree of Thought (ToT) 搜索方法在实际部署中，不同搜索策略在变化计算预算、模型规模和问题难度下的行为缺乏系统性的研究和理解。

#### Key Idea

通过系统对比两种代表性ToT方法（基于MCTS的DPTS和基于语义去重的SSDP），发现它们在资源受限和资源充裕场景下表现出相反方向的局限性——DPTS低预算时冷启动瓶颈严重，SSDP高预算时因前沿耗尽而无法提升，说明固定策略无法适配计算资源连续变化的需求。

#### System/Method Design

评估了两个代表性ToT方法：DPTS（基于蒙特卡洛树搜索）和SSDP（基于语义去重）。实验涉及两个数学推理基准（Math500和GSM8K）、两个模型规模（Llama-3B和Llama-8B）和四个token预算（3k-10k），未提出新方法，而是进行系统性的比较分析。

#### Experiments

在两个数学推理基准（Math500和GSM8K）上，使用Llama-3B和Llama-8B两个规模的模型，在四种token预算（3k-10k）下对比DPTS和SSDP的性能。结果显示：DPTS在低预算下因价值估计不准确而表现差（冷启动瓶颈），但在高预算下扩展性良好；SSDP能快速找到候选解，但激进地合并节点导致探索路径被永久丢弃（前沿耗尽），无法利用多余预算进一步提升性能。

#### Why It Matters

该研究揭示了现有ToT搜索方法在计算预算、模型规模和问题难度变化下的系统性缺陷，指出固定探索策略和固定剪枝策略均不足以应对计算资源连续变化的需求，为设计更高效、自适应的科学推理搜索策略提供了重要指导。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。该研究系统评估了LLM推理阶段的搜索策略（ToT）在资源约束下的行为，揭示了计算预算与搜索性能之间的权衡关系。对于LLM推理加速和系统优化（如MoE推理中的搜索预算分配、KV缓存管理下的推理深度控制）具有重要参考价值，尤其适用于需要在有限计算资源下最大化推理性能的场景。

#### Abstract

Tree of Thought (ToT) search has become a promising direction for improving the reasoning capabilities of large language models, but deploying these methods in practice raises a question that has received little systematic attention: how do different search strategies behave under varying compute budgets, model sizes, and problem difficulties? In this work, we evaluate two representative ToT methods; DPTS, a Monte Carlo tree search based approach, and SSDP, a semantic deduplication based approach, across two mathematical reasoning benchmarks (Math500 and GSM8K), two model scales (Llama-3B and Llama-8B), and four token budgets (3k--10k). Our analysis reveals that the two methods exhibit limitations that pull in opposite directions. DPTS suffers from a cold-start bottleneck at low budgets: it requires sufficient exploration before its value estimates become reliable, making it a poor fit for resource-constrained settings despite strong scaling behavior at higher budgets. SSDP, on the other hand, reaches candidate solutions efficiently but is prone to frontier depletion; its aggressive node merging permanently discards unexplored paths, leaving it unable to improve regardless of how much budget remains. Together, these findings suggest that neither a fixed exploration strategy nor a fixed pruning strategy is sufficient across compute continuum. We argue that effective search for scientific reasoning agents requires strategies that can adapt their behavior based on search progress and available resources.

### [80] [The New Associationism: Lessons from Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20600)

*Daniel Rothschild*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 本文论证现代AI的成功（尤其是监督学习）支持了一种温和但真实的联想主义学习理论，并反驳了联想机制不足以解释人类认知能力的传统观点。

#### Problem

传统观点认为联想主义学习机制过于简单，不足以解释人类复杂的认知能力。现代AI的快速发展对这一经典争论提出了新的挑战和启示。

#### Key Idea

监督学习（基于评价性反馈的学习）是现代AI系统的核心机制，从大语言模型到游戏智能体都依赖于这一统一、渐进、基于错误驱动的学习方式，这恰恰契合了联想主义的核心理念。同时，深度学习架构远超经典联想主义的设想，监督学习在其中只是一个组件而非全部。

#### System/Method Design

本文并非提出具体系统或方法，而是从哲学和认知科学的角度进行论证：将现代AI（监督学习）视为人类学习模型，分析其与联想主义理论的关联。文中指出不同AI系统的差异主要在于生成相关反馈信号所需的工作量不同。

#### Experiments

摘要中未明确说明具体的实验设置、基线、指标或定量结果。本文属于理论论证型研究。

#### Why It Matters

本文在AI与认知科学的交叉点上提供了重要理论贡献：一方面用AI的成功为联想主义学习理论提供了新的辩护，另一方面也揭示了现代深度学习架构对传统联想主义的超越，有助于更深入地理解人类学习机制与AI学习机制之间的关系。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

本文与LLM/系统研究的直接技术关联性较低，属于认知科学与AI的交叉理论探讨。但文中以大语言模型和游戏智能体作为监督学习成功案例进行分析，为理解LLM的学习本质提供了认知科学视角。对于MoE、推理加速、分布式系统等硬件/架构方向无直接关联。

#### Abstract

What can the success of modern AI tell us about how humans learn? This paper argues that taking AI seriously as a model of human learning supports a modest but genuine associationism. The central finding is that supervised learning -- learning driven by evaluative feedback -- underlies a surprisingly wide range of contemporary AI systems, from large language models to game-playing agents, differing primarily in how much work is required to generate the relevant feedback signal. This vindicates associationist ideals of a uniform, gradual, error-driven learning mechanism operating across domains, and defuses the once-influential argument that associationist mechanisms are too limited to account for human cognitive capacities. At the same time, the successes of deep learning depend on computational architectures that go well beyond anything classical associationists envisaged, and supervised learning operates within these as one component rather than a complete account of learning.

### [81] [Specifying AI-SDLC Processes: A Protocol Language for Human-Agent Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20615)

*Ylli Prifti*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 提出一种面向AI软件开发生命周期（AI-SDLC）的领域特定语言（DSL），用于形式化地表达人-智能体之间的责任边界、审批门控和治理约束，将策略与机制分离，并通过原型实现验证了可行性。

#### Problem

AI智能体已广泛参与软件开发生命周期，但缺乏一种正式的规范语言来表达人类与智能体之间的责任边界、审批门控和治理约束。现有方法要么将流程编码在易漂移的prompt中，要么只针对相邻领域（工作流管理、业务流程）或只解决碎片化问题（访问控制、审批门控），缺乏统一的、形式化的规范手段。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是将AI-SDLC流程视为协议（protocol），并设计一种领域特定语言来形式化表达这些协议。关键洞察是将"策略（policy）"（声明的意图）与"机制（mechanism）"（结构性强制执行）分离，通过验证令牌（validation tokens）和能力边界（capability boundaries）等原语来约束流程中的非确定性行为。

#### System/Method Design

提出一种用于AI-SDLC流程规范的DSL，包含：形式语法（formal syntax）、良构性条件（well-formedness conditions）、操作语义（operational semantics）和执行不变性（enforcement invariants）。语言区分策略与机制：策略表达意图，机制提供结构性约束。核心原语包括验证令牌（validation tokens）和能力边界（capability boundaries）。还提出了2+N团队模式（两个人类管控角色+N个专业化智能体成员），正式化了AI-SDLC中的职责分离原则。

#### Experiments

论文提供了失效速率分析（failure rate analysis）：结构性强制执行将系统失效率控制在智能体和验证器速率的加权乘积范围内，而行为合规性（behavioral compliance）则允许累积或接近饱和的增长。实证评估被标记为未来工作。仅提及了工作原型实现证明了可行性。

#### Why It Matters

该工作填补了AI-SDLC领域缺乏统一规范语言的空白，为人-智能体协作开发提供了形式化的流程约束手段。通过分离策略与机制，能够更可靠地管理流程中的非确定性，降低系统失效率。2+N团队模式的引入为多智能体协作中的治理和责任划分提供了形式化基础，对构建安全、可控的AI辅助软件开发流程具有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM系统和AI智能体系统高度相关。该工作直接针对多智能体协作场景下的流程规范与治理问题，与MetaGPT等多智能体框架对标。虽然不直接涉及MoE、KV缓存或推理加速等系统优化问题，但为LLM驱动的智能体在软件开发流程中的安全执行和可控性提供了形式化基础，对大规模AI系统的可靠性保障有参考价值。

#### Abstract

AI agents now participate as first-class team members across the software development lifecycle, yet no specification language exists for expressing the human-agent responsibility boundaries, approval gates, and governance constraints this collaboration requires. Existing approaches encode process in agent prompts (subject to drift), target adjacent domains (workflow management, business processes), or address only fragments (access control, approval gates).
  We propose a domain-specific language for specifying AI-SDLC processes as protocols, with formal syntax, well-formedness conditions, operational semantics, and enforcement invariants. The language distinguishes policy (declared intent) from mechanism (structural enforcement), enabling implementations to bound process non-determinism through primitives such as validation tokens and capability boundaries.
  Three results follow. A failure rate analysis shows that structural enforcement bounds system failure rates at a weighted product of agent and validator rates, while behavioral compliance permits cumulative or near-saturating growth. The 2+N team pattern (two human-in-control roles plus N specialized agent members) formalizes classical Separation of Duties for AI-SDLC. Kleene closure of orchestration loops and reflexive protocol-adherence validation emerge as design properties rather than special-case constructs.
  We position the contribution against multi-agent frameworks (MetaGPT), workflow specification (FlowAgent, BPMN extensions), and capability-based security (SAGA): the novelty lies in the specific integration, not any single primitive. A working implementation demonstrates feasibility; empirical evaluation is future work.

### [82] [PEAR: Permutation-Equivariant Adaptive Routing Multi-Agent Debate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20621)

*Yang Feng,Ziwei Xu,Xia Hu,Fengxiang He*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** PEAR提出了一种置换等变自适应路由多智能体辩论协议，通过动态重配置通信角色和稀疏拓扑结构来消除固定辩论框架中的位置偏差，提升LLM推理可靠性。

#### Problem

固定拓扑结构的多智能体辩论存在三个关键问题：持续性的位置偏见、不可靠智能体的影响力被放大、对角色分配高度敏感，导致辩论质量和推理可靠性受限。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是设计一个置换等变的自适应路由机制，在连续辩论轮次之间根据智能体状态动态切换角色分配和稀疏通信拓扑，防止任何智能体永久占据特权网络位置，实现影响力的更均衡分布。

#### System/Method Design

PEAR是一个推理时协议，包含：(1) 自适应路由机制，根据演化中的智能体状态动态重新配置通信角色；(2) 稀疏拓扑结构，降低通信复杂度；(3) 置换等变稀疏路由器，保证在智能体重标记下输出不变性，同时降低路由复杂度并提升泛化能力。

#### Experiments

在四个推理基准测试和六种不同的LLM骨干网络上进行了全面评估，PEAR相比最强的辩论基线方法在平均准确率上有显著提升。具体实验设置、基线方法和指标细节在摘要中未明确说明。

#### Why It Matters

该工作通过理论保证（置换等变性）和动态拓扑设计解决了多智能体辩论中的系统性偏差问题，为提升LLM推理可靠性提供了可扩展且理论扎实的新范式。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关：涉及LLM推理可靠性提升方法；其自适应稀疏路由机制与MoE中的动态路由、分布式系统中智能体通信拓扑优化有紧密联系；置换等变路由设计对系统层面减少通信开销和负载均衡有借鉴意义。

#### Abstract

Multi-agent debate improves the reliability of large language models (LLMs) through iterative peer critiques. However, fixed topologies often introduce persistent positional biases, amplify unreliable agents, and cause high sensitivity to role assignments. We introduce \textit{Permutation-Equivariant Adaptive Routing Multi-Agent Debate (PEAR)}, an inference-time protocol that dynamically reconfigures communication roles and sparse topologies across consecutive debate rounds. By strategically switching agent-to-role assignments based on evolving agent states, PEAR prevents any agent from permanently occupying a privileged network position or distributes influence more evenly across the debate. We theoretically characterize PEAR as an equivariant sparse router: it preserves accuracy under agent relabeling while reducing routing complexity and improving generalization. Comprehensive empirical evaluations across four reasoning benchmarks and six diverse LLM backbones demonstrate PEAR significantly improves average accuracy over the strongest debate baselines. The code is at https://github.com/EVIEHub/PEAR.

### [83] [Learning Filters with Certainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22786)

*Yuval Banoun,Daniel Sadoc Menasche,Ori Rottenstreich*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出利用计数布隆过滤器（CBF）中的计数器信息来估计成员指示的确定性，并在结合布隆过滤器与机器学习模型的架构中利用这种确定性信号。

#### Problem

传统哈希数据结构（如布隆过滤器）仅返回元素是否属于集合的二元指示，但由于哈希冲突导致的假阳性问题，系统只能返回阳性结果以避免假阴性，无法提供关于该指示的确定性或置信度信息。

#### Key Idea

计数布隆过滤器（CBF）中的计数器不仅支持插入和删除操作，还包含了可用于估计阳性成员指示确定性（certainty）的额外信息，这种确定性信号本身可以被利用来改善系统性能。

#### System/Method Design

论文聚焦于计数布隆过滤器（Counting Bloom Filters），利用其计数器提供的额外信息来量化阳性成员查询的确定性程度，并提出在结合布隆过滤器与机器学习模型的混合架构中利用这一确定性信号。

#### Experiments

摘要中未明确说明具体的实验设置、基线、指标或量化结果。

#### Why It Matters

该工作将布隆过滤器从二元决策设备提升为能提供置信度信息的工具，使得缓存、异常检测和机器学习管道等网络系统中的决策可以基于不确定性程度进行更精细的权衡，尤其在布隆过滤器与ML模型结合的架构中具有实用价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/MoE/系统研究的关联较为间接。布隆过滤器常用于分布式系统和大规模推理系统中的缓存机制（如KV缓存管理、模型参数查找），本文提出的确定性信号机制可以优化缓存决策的质量。在MoE路由或专家缓存等场景中，利用确定性信息可以更智能地决定是否查询缓存或回退到计算，从而降低延迟和提高系统效率。

#### Abstract

Hash-based data structures such as Bloom filters are widely used in network systems for tasks including caching, anomaly detection, and machine learning pipelines. They typically provide binary indications of whether an element belongs to a set of interest, e.g., the contents of a cache. When uncertainty arises due to hash collisions, a positive indication is returned to avoid false negatives. We argue that the certainty associated with such indications can itself be useful information. This work focuses on Counting Bloom Filters (CBFs), a Bloom-filter variant that maintains counters rather than bits. Besides supporting insertions and deletions, these counters provide additional information that can be used to estimate the certainty of positive membership indications. We show how this certainty signal can be exploited in architectures that combine Bloom Filters with machine learning (ML) models.

### [84] [Darwin Mobile Agent: A Roadmap for Self-Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20622)

*Daniel Beechey,Derek Yuen,Jianheng Liu,Dezhao Luo,Tiantian He,Weilin Luo,Jun Wang,Kun Shao*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 提出 Darwin Mobile Agent 框架，以移动 GUI 作为"大世界"代理，通过无人类先验的异步强化学习实现自主演化智能体。

#### Problem

现有 AI 智能体过度依赖人类先验知识（人工设计的任务课程、结果验证机制和记忆管理），无法在开放环境中实现真正自主、自演化的通用智能；同时在真实移动交互场景中面临数据收集瓶颈。

#### Key Idea

受"Bitter Lesson"启发，系统性地移除人类先验，让智能体通过与比自身复杂多个数量级的"大世界"（以移动 GUI 为实际代理）交互，自然涌现出通用适应行为。

#### System/Method Design

Darwin Mobile Agent 是一个开源基础设施，通过跨并行云手机实例的异步智能体-环境循环，解决真实移动交互中的数据收集瓶颈；为自演化智能体的三大支柱（任务课程、结果验证、记忆管理）提供了逐步移除人类先验的概念路线图。

#### Experiments

验证了 Darwin 基础设施在 GUI 领域策略优化的第一阶段具备所需的稳定性和可扩展性。具体基线、指标和详细实验结果在摘要中未明确说明。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为构建真正自主、自演化的 GUI 智能体奠定了实践和理论基础，为 AI 从依赖人类先验走向完全自主学习提供了可操作的路径和基础设施。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与 LLM 系统和推理加速的关联不直接，但该工作的异步并行框架设计（跨云手机实例）、数据收集瓶颈解决方案以及自主智能体的记忆管理机制，对分布式系统、强化学习系统和自主智能体架构研究有参考价值。

#### Abstract

The goal of artificial intelligence is to create agents capable of general, adaptive behaviour in open-ended environments. Guided by the "Bitter Lesson", we argue that the most effective path toward this goal is to systematically remove human priors and allow intelligence to naturally emerge through interaction with a "Big World" that is orders of magnitude more complex than the agent itself. We propose the mobile Graphical User Interface (GUI) as a practical proxy for such a world and introduce Darwin Mobile Agent, an open-source infrastructure designed as a foundation for autonomous reinforcement learning in this domain. This framework addresses the data-collection bottleneck in real-world mobile interactions by using an asynchronous agent-environment loop across parallel cloud-phone instances. We further propose a conceptual roadmap to systematically remove human priors from three fundamental pillars of a self-evolving agent: task curricula, outcome verification, and memory management. We validate that the Darwin infrastructure provides the stability and scalability required for the first stage of this roadmap: policy optimisation in the GUI domain. This work establishes the practical and theoretical foundation necessary to move toward truly autonomous, self-evolving GUI agents.

### [85] [Path-dependent program induction under resource constraints explains human sequence learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20623)

*Hanqi Zhou,David G. Nagy,Peter Dayan,Charley M. Wu*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出层次化适应文法（HAG）来建模人类在有限认知资源下，如何通过顺序经验构建抽象、可复用的知识，并将其形式化为受记忆和计算约束的有界程序归纳。

#### Problem

人类如何在有限认知资源（有界记忆和计算）下，从顺序经验中构建抽象、可复用的知识，现有方法（如固定文法或浅层分块方法）无法很好地解释这种能力。

#### Key Idea

将率-失真理论与程序归纳相结合，用层次化适应文法（HAG）形式化先验知识如何影响未来结构的编码成本与可发现性，并通过局部（任务内）和全局（跨任务）库的联合约束来建模记忆和计算限制。

#### System/Method Design

层次化适应文法（HAG）包含两个不同层级的库：局部库（within-task，任务内模式）和全局库（across-task，跨任务抽象模式），由记忆和计算约束联合控制。该方法将结构学习形式化为有界程序归纳问题。

#### Experiments

模拟实验表明HAG比固定文法和浅层分块方法实现了更优的率-失真权衡和更强的泛化能力。在线旋律序列学习实验中，参与者的回忆错误反映了系统性的简化，反应时间在推断的程序边界处增加。逐试次拟合显示，层次化库在解释个体差异（包括回忆和续写选择）方面优于所有替代模型。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为理解人类在有限认知资源下如何通过顺序经验构建抽象知识提供了计算框架，将学习形式化为有界程序归纳，并预测了经验顺序对未来抽象知识构建的影响。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

论文与LLM系统的核心关联在于：HAG的层次化库（局部+全局）结构与MoE（混合专家）中的路由和专家选择机制有概念上的相似性；有界程序归纳框架对理解LLM的归纳偏置和泛化能力具有理论意义；任务内/跨任务知识分离的思想可用于设计更高效的记忆系统和知识复用机制；率-失真框架可用于分析LLM的压缩表示与泛化性能之间的权衡。

#### Abstract

How do people build abstract, reusable knowledge from sequential experience under bounded cognitive resources? To answer this question, we integrate rate-distortion theory with recent advances in program induction to describe how prior knowledge shapes which future structures are cheap to encode and easy to discover. We formalize this in a hierarchical Adaptor Grammar (HAG) with distinct local (within-task) and global (across-task) libraries, governed jointly by constraints on memory and computation. In simulations, HAG achieves better rate-distortion trade-offs and stronger generalization than fixed grammars or shallow chunking methods. In an online melodic sequence-learning experiment, participants' recall errors reflected systematic simplifications and reaction times increased at inferred program boundaries. Trial-by-trial fits further showed that hierarchical libraries best explained individual differences in both recall and out-of-sample continuation choices, outperforming all alternative models. These findings cast structured learning as bounded program induction in which the order of experience shapes future abstractions a learner builds.

### [86] [In LLM Reasoning, there is Irrationality on top of Value Misalignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20624)

*Kejiang Qian,Fengxiang He*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出"理性价值风险"概念来形式化描述对齐后的LLM在推理时仍无法最大化对齐价值的差距，并通过实验验证该风险普遍存在且无法被对齐完全消除。

#### Problem

即使LLM在（后）训练阶段已经与目标价值函数取得了良好的对齐，模型在推理时仍然可能无法实际最大化该对齐价值，存在训练与推理之间的效用差距。

#### Key Idea

将训练后LLM在推理时偏离理性（即最大化期望效用的最优推理策略）的差距形式化为"理性价值风险"，并将其估计误差分解为三个来源：有限候选、有限提示和不完美验证器。

#### System/Method Design

论文提出理性价值风险（Rational Value Risk）的数学形式化定义：模型部署推理策略与其理性对应策略（在最陡方向上最大化期望效用的响应）之间的效用差异。进一步将估计误差分解为三个可量化的组成部分。

#### Experiments

覆盖Llama-3.1、Qwen-2.5、Tülu-3系列（7B-72B）、GPT-5.2、GPT-5.5、DeepSeek-V4等模型，在UltraFeedback、AlpacaEval、GSM8K、MATH、HumanEval、MathArena等基准上验证。主要发现：(1)理性价值风险普遍存在；(2)价值对齐可以降低风险但无法消除；(3)风险对推理时的策略高度敏感；(4)更长的推理能改善理性但边际收益递减。

#### Why It Matters

该工作揭示了LLM对齐中一个被忽视的关键问题：训练阶段的对齐不足以保证推理阶段的理性行为，为理解LLM推理中的价值偏差提供了理论框架和实证基础，对改进推理策略和评估方法具有指导意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关于LLM推理加速与推理策略优化：论文发现推理时策略对理性价值风险高度敏感，且更长推理的收益递减，这对LLM推理系统设计（如推理步数控制、计算预算分配）有重要指导意义。同时，理性的形式化定义也为评估不同推理架构（包括MoE）的效用最大化能力提供了理论工具。

#### Abstract

Significant progress has been made in aligning LLMs with target value functions. We argue that, even when an LLM has been well aligned in (post-)training, it may still fail to maximise the aligned value in reasoning. We mathematically formalise this gap as rational value risk: the utility discrepancy between a model's deployed reasoning strategy and its rational counterpart, which is defined to be the responses that maximise expected utility in the steepest direction. The estimation error of rational value risk is further decomposed into three components from finite candidates, finite prompts, and imperfect verifiers. Extensive experiments are conducted, covering models Llama-3.1, Qwen-2.5, T{\"}ulu-3 families (7B-72B), GPT-5.2, GPT-5.5, and DeepSeek-V4, and benchmarks UltraFeedback, AlpacaEval, GSM8K, MATH, HumanEval, and MathArena. The results validate that (1) rational value risk is widespread; (2) value alignment can reduce, but cannot eliminate, it; (3) the risk is highly sensitive to inference-time reasoning strategy; and (4) longer reasoning improves rationality with diminishing returns. The code is at https://github.com/EVIEHub/LLM-Rationality.

### [87] [AlphaMemo: Structured Search-Process Memory for Self-Evolving Alpha Mining Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20625)

*Hang Yu,Zifan Zheng,Jeff Z. Pan,Tongliang Liu,Zhiyong Wang,Fengxiang He*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** AlphaMemo 是一个将结构化搜索过程记忆引入 LLM 智能体的自进化 Alpha 挖掘框架，通过 AST 差异提取编辑模式、置信门控残差记忆与非对称否决控制，在 CSI 500 和 S&P 500 上提升了因子挖掘的样本外表现和发现效率。

#### Problem

LLM 智能体在金融 Alpha 因子挖掘中面临四个核心问题：组合搜索空间巨大、噪声非平稳反馈、冗余发现过多，以及因简单复用历史成功经验导致的过拟合风险。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察是：不应仅记忆最终因子或完整轨迹，而应记录可复用的零散证据——在特定父因子上下文中，哪些编辑模式（edit motifs）有效或失败，从而实现结构化的搜索过程记忆。

#### System/Method Design

AlphaMemo 包含三个关键设计：1) 从抽象语法树（AST）差异中提取编辑模式（motifs）；2) 在搜索分类账先验（search-ledger prior）之上使用置信门控残差记忆（confidence-gated residual memory）；3) 采用非对称否决控制（asymmetric veto control）来抑制高置信度的失败模式。

#### Experiments

在 CSI 500（A股）和 S&P 500（美股）两个数据集上进行实验，衡量指标为样本外表现（out-of-sample performance）和固定预算下的发现效率（fixed-budget discovery efficiency）。消融实验验证了残差学习、置信门控、AST 差异编辑模式以及否决记忆各自的有效性。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为 LLM 智能体在复杂、高噪声、非平稳的搜索空间中进行自动化因子挖掘提供了一种结构化的记忆管理方法，本质上是将经验学习从"记住结果"升级为"记住条件化的模式知识"，对于提升 Alpha 挖掘的鲁棒性和可解释性有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关：1) 属于 LLM Agent 在专业领域（金融）的推理与搜索应用；2) 提出的结构化搜索过程记忆（AST-diff motifs + 置信门控残差记忆）可视为一种轻量级的专家经验路由机制，与 MoE 中稀疏激活和专家选择的思路有类比性；3) 非对称否决控制类似于推理时的安全抑制机制；4) 该方法对搜索空间剪枝和记忆效率的改进思路，可迁移至 LLM 推理加速（如减少无效搜索分支）、KV 缓存等场景中的冗余控制问题。

#### Abstract

LLM agents are promising for alpha mining via combining financial priors, symbolic reasoning, executable factor generation, and feedback-driven refinement. Yet, they face a combinatorial search space, noisy non-stationary feedback, redundant discoveries, and overfitting risks from naively reusing past successes. To address these challenges, we propose AlphaMemo, a self-evolving alpha mining agent with Structured Search-Process Memory. Rather than memorizing only final factors or full trajectories, AlphaMemo records reusable evidence about which edit motifs work or fail under specific parent-factor contexts. It extracts motifs from Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) differences, applies confidence-gated residual memory on top of a search-ledger prior, and uses asymmetric veto control to suppress high-confidence failure patterns. Experiments on CSI 500 and S\&P 500 show improved out-of-sample performance and fixed-budget discovery efficiency, with ablations validating the roles of residual learning, confidence gating, AST-diff motifs, and veto memory. Code is at https://github.com/jarrettyu/AlphaMemo.

### [88] [Latent Goal Prediction from Language for Model-Based Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20627)

*Samuel Barbeau,Simon Roy,Giovanni Beltrame,Christian Desrosiers,Nicolas Thome*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** LAGO提出了一种从语言指令中预测隐空间子目标序列的框架，通过动态分解指令为局部可解的隐子目标并结合软最小轨迹代价规划，实现了长时域上鲁棒且精确的规划，避免了传统方法的复合预测误差和跨模态对齐问题。

#### Problem

基于世界模型的规划面临两个主要瓶颈：(1) 复合预测误差随规划步长累积导致性能急剧下降；(2) 难以定义可优化的目标——视觉目标提供精确局部梯度但缺乏远距离引导，语言目标灵活但受限于噪声跨模态对齐或依赖不适合高采样模型规划的大规模生成模型。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是从语言指令中显式预测一系列中间隐空间子目标（而非仅一个全局目标），并在规划中动态更新这些子目标，结合软最小轨迹代价（soft minimum trajectory cost）选择路径，使得智能体能在同一隐空间中完成子目标预测与动作条件 rollout，从而实现长时域上的连贯轨迹跟踪。

#### System/Method Design

LAGO框架在同一隐空间内同时完成两项任务：(1) 从语言指令中预测一系列中间隐状态子目标序列；(2) 进行动作条件 rollout（预测状态轨迹）。规划时，它动态在线更新这些子目标，并使用软最小轨迹代价函数来评估和选择轨迹，避免陷入单一全局目标优化的困境，将长程任务分解为一系列局部可解的隐空间子问题。

#### Experiments

在多个环境（不同规划时域长度）下进行评估，与先前方法相比，LAGO避免了性能的急剧退化（sharp degradation），在长时域规划中保持鲁棒性和精确性。摘要未提供具体基准方法、评测指标和数值结果。

#### Why It Matters

LAGO弥合了视觉目标精确引导与文本灵活控制之间的鸿沟，使得纯粹基于语言指令的长时域鲁棒规划成为可能。这对机器人在复杂、长时域任务中的语言引导控制具有重要价值，突破了传统模型规划方法在长时域上的性能衰减瓶颈。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/系统研究的相关性中等。LAGO使用语言作为规划指导信号，涉及语言到隐空间的映射，与多模态LLM有交叉；但核心贡献在于机器人规划算法中的子目标分解与轨迹优化，而非LLM系统优化、MoE路由、KV cache或分布式训练等。对希望将语言模型能力融合进机器人规划系统的研究者有参考价值。

#### Abstract

Planning with world models is bottlenecked by compounding prediction errors and the difficulty of defining optimizable goals. Visual targets provide precise local gradients but poor distant guidance, while language is flexible yet limited by noisy cross-modal alignment or dependence on large generative models unsuited for the high-sampling nature of model-based planning. To address these challenges, we introduce Latent Goal Prediction from Language (LAGO), a framework that predicts both sequences of intermediate goal states from language instructions and action-conditioned rollouts, all within the same latent space. Rather than optimizing toward a single global objective, LAGO dynamically decomposes instructions into explicitly predicted, locally tractable latent subgoals. By updating these subgoals online and using a soft minimum trajectory cost during planning, LAGO enables an agent to follow coherent latent trajectories over long horizons. Evaluation across multiple environments planning horizons shows that LAGO avoids the sharp degradation of prior methods. By achieving robust and precise long-horizon planning purely from language, LAGO bridges the precision of visual goals with the flexibility of text-guided control.

### [89] [Human Decision-Making with AI Assistance under Correlated Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20628)

*Yanru Guan,Naveen Raman,Fei Fang*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 本文证明当特征相关时，AI辅助决策中推荐测试的最优策略必须遵循"先探索后承诺"结构，并提出了相应算法来平衡短期决策质量与长期人类学习。

#### Problem

当不同特征（如医学检验结果）存在相关性时，AI应如何推荐测试以平衡短期决策质量和长期人类学习效果？先前的静止策略（反复推荐相同测试）在特征独立时是最优的，但在特征相关时表现极差。

#### Key Idea

最优策略必须采用"先探索后承诺"（explore-then-commit）结构：初始阶段AI应提供多样化的测试，使人类能够学习准确的特征系数；之后AI再承诺使用单一测试集，探索长度取决于特征相关程度。

#### System/Method Design

论文证明计算最优策略是NP难的，提出了一个基于动态规划的算法来求解有限时域下的最优策略。此外，还开发了一种近似方法：规划较短时域并附加一个静止后缀，实现接近最优的性能。

#### Experiments

实验结果表明，特征相关性越强，最优策略所需的探索阶段越长，与理论分析一致。

#### Why It Matters

该工作揭示了特征相关性对AI辅助决策中"探索-利用"权衡的根本性影响，为AI系统如何设计推荐策略以促进人类长期学习提供了理论基础，对医疗诊断等高风险人机协作场景具有重要指导意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该论文研究的是AI辅助决策中推荐策略的优化问题，属于人机协作决策理论范畴。虽然不直接涉及LLM系统、MoE、推理加速、KV缓存等系统研究方向，但其中关于探索-利用权衡、动态规划算法以及特征相关性的分析思路，对AI系统（包括LLM系统）中如何进行策略设计与资源分配具有参考价值。

#### Abstract

Humans increasingly make decisions with AI assistance; for example, doctors may follow AI-recommended diagnostic tests and base their diagnoses on the results. A natural question is which tests should AI recommend to balance short-term decision quality and long-term human learning when different features (e.g., test results) are correlated. While prior work establishes that stationary policies that recommend the same tests repeatedly are optimal when features are independent, we prove that feature correlations lead such policies to perform arbitrarily poorly. Instead, we prove that any optimal policy must follow an explore-then-commit structure; initially, the AI should offer diverse tests so humans can learn accurate feature coefficients, then the AI should commit to a single set of tests, with exploration length that depends on the degree of feature correlation. We prove that computing the optimal policy is NP-hard and derive a dynamic programming-based algorithm that finds the optimal policy for finite horizons. We additionally develop an approximation that plans for shorter horizons and appends a stationary suffix, achieving near-optimal performance. Our empirical results complement our theory by showing that stronger feature correlation leads to longer exploration phases.

### [90] [Harnessing Agent Skills: Architectural Patterns and a Reference Architecture for Skill-Mediated LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20631)

*Boming Xia,Liming Zhu,Zhenchang Xing,Qinghua Lu,Dino Sejdinovic,Xiwei Xu*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出了一套关于LLM智能体技能利用（skill harnessing）的架构模式与参考架构，系统化描述了技能从静态工件到运行时"技能在用"（skill-in-use）的转换过程及其对应的架构责任。

#### Problem

在LLM智能体系统中，技能（agent skills）作为可复用的行为知识工件，在运行时需要经历选择、绑定上下文、由随机智能体解释并记录证据的复杂过程。然而，这些从静态技能工件到动态"技能在用"的转换、执行约束绑定及证据捕获等架构责任缺乏系统化的分析和设计指导。

#### Key Idea

将技能视为"静态时是工件、运行时是关系"（skill-in-use），并围绕技能工件到技能在用之间的转换、执行约束、证据捕获等核心责任，提炼出可复用的架构模式。

#### System/Method Design

本文基于经验归纳提出了10个架构模式（5个核心模式+5个支撑模式），并将其综合为一个包含四个责任层的参考架构：供应链层（Supply Chain）、中介层（Mediation）、执行控制层（Execution Control）以及证据与反馈层（Evidence & Feedback）。

#### Experiments

通过在8个选定的智能体系统中进行跨实例化（cross-instantiation）来评估该参考架构的有效性。摘要未明确提及具体数据集、基线或量化指标。

#### Why It Matters

为LLM智能体系统的技能管理与运行时执行提供了一个通用的词汇表和诊断框架，帮助研究人员和工程师系统化地分析、设计和比较不同智能体系统中技能利用相关的架构责任。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。该工作聚焦于LLM智能体系统中技能的架构设计，涉及技能的供应、中介、执行控制和证据反馈，对构建可演化、可归因、可修复的LLM智能体系统具有指导意义。虽然未直接涉及MoE或推理加速，但其系统层面的架构抽象对分布式智能体系统、模块化技能编排等场景有参考价值。

#### Abstract

Agent skills externalise reusable agent-facing behavioural knowledge and guidance as persistent artefacts that can be discovered, activated, and interpreted by LLM agents. Although a skill artefact is static at rest, its architectural responsibilities arise in use, when the artefact is selected for a run, bound to context and authority constraints, interpreted by a stochastic agent, and recorded as run evidence. We call this run-specific relation skill-in-use. This paper studies agent skill harnessing: the architectural responsibilities that govern the transition from skill artefacts to skill-in-use, bound the executable consequences associated with skill-in-use, and capture evidence for attribution, verification, repair, and evolution. This paper provides a catalogue of ten empirically grounded architectural patterns (five core, five supporting) for skill harnessing and synthesises them into a reference architecture with four responsibility layers: Supply Chain, Mediation, Execution Control, and Evidence & Feedback. We evaluate the architecture through cross-instantiation across 8 selected systems. The resulting patterns and reference architecture provide a vocabulary and diagnostic frame for analysing skill-harnessing responsibilities across agent systems.

### [91] [DEMM-Bench: A Cross-Regime Benchmark for Agent-Runtime Governance-Evidence Sufficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20634)

*Oleg Solozobov*

Main category: `cs.AI`
