A temporal stabilization module further improves prediction consistency in real-time interaction settings.The generated instruction sequence is then passed to a downstream VLA policy for sign-conditioned robotic manipulation. Experimental results demonstrate stable real-time sign recognition and successful execution of manipulation tasks driven by sign-language inputs. Our findings suggest that lightweight temporal sign recognition can serve as an effective and practical accessibility layer for multimodal embodied intelligence.

### [121] [When Do Intrinsic Rewards Work for Code Reasoning? A Comprehensive Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20881)

*Xiaolong Jin,Xuandong Zhao,Wenbo Guo,Xiangyu Zhang,Dawn Song*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 对基于内在奖励（intrinsic reward）的强化学习方法在代码生成任务上进行了系统性的实证研究，发现此类方法虽然初期有效但最终必然导致模型崩溃。

#### Problem

在代码生成任务中，使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）依赖昂贵的ground-truth监督；近期提出的基于模型自身信号（如多数投票、置信度）的内在奖励方法在数学推理上成功，但能否有效迁移到结构复杂、语义等价但语法不同的代码生成任务尚未被探索。

#### Key Idea

对代表性基于置信度的内在奖励方法（RLIF，Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback）在代码生成场景下进行系统评估，揭示其早期有效但最终必然崩溃的根本性局限。

#### System/Method Design

系统性地评估了基于置信度的内在奖励方法（RLIF），在LiveCodeBench基准上、不同训练场景和超参数设置下进行广泛实验。具体对比了使用内在奖励初始化RLVR训练与从头训练的效果差异。

#### Experiments

在LiveCodeBench基准上进行实验。主要发现：(1) 基于置信度的方法初期有效但最终必然崩溃，模型逐步缩短输出并丧失推理能力；(2) 崩溃速度对样本大小和温度参数敏感；(3) 用RLIF预训练初始化RLVR相比从头训练没有显著提升。

#### Why It Matters

首次系统揭示了内在奖励方法在代码生成任务中的根本性缺陷（模型崩溃），为未来代码推理模型和智能体的训练提供了重要的经验指导和实践建议，有助于避免对这类方法的不当依赖。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。研究LLM推理模型的强化学习训练方法，评估了内在奖励信号的有效性和局限性，涉及代码生成这一LLM关键应用场景。对理解LLM训练中奖励信号设计、模型推理能力的保持与退化机制有重要启示。

#### Abstract

Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has driven substantial progress in large language model reasoning, but relies on ground-truth supervision that is costly or infeasible, especially in coding tasks. Recent work addresses this by deriving rewards from a model's own signals, such as majority voting or confidence-based scores, achieving notable success on mathematical reasoning benchmarks. However, code generation poses distinct challenges: programs are structurally complex, semantically equivalent solutions may differ syntactically, and verification typically requires execution. Whether these intrinsic reward methods transfer effectively to code remains unexplored. In this work, we present a systematic empirical study of intrinsic reward methods for code generation. We conduct extensive experiments on LiveCodeBench, systematically evaluating representative certainty-based Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF) approaches under different training scenarios and hyperparameter settings. Our experiments reveal that certainty-based methods yield early gains but inevitably collapse: models progressively shorten outputs and lose reasoning capability, with collapse speed sensitive to sample size and temperature. When used to initialize RLVR training, RLIF pre-training offers no significant improvement over training from scratch. We also provide actionable recommendations for using intrinsic rewards for training code reasoning models. Our study shows both the promise and limitations of intrinsic reward methods for code, informing future work on code models and agents.

### [122] [Neurosymbolic Clinical Trial Matching via LLM-Driven Abduction and Logical Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20895)

*Baiyang Qu,Leonardo Ranaldi,Xi Wang,Marco Valentino*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 提出一个结合LLM与溯因逻辑推理的神经符号混合框架αNeSy-CTM，用于自动化的临床试验匹配，在复杂入组标准验证中显著优于纯LLM基线。

#### Problem

LLM在处理复杂临床试验入组标准的确定性验证时表现不足，而纯符号方法在面对不完整的患者记录和有噪声的临床证据时也会失效。

#### Key Idea

利用LLM的语言和世界知识，结合溯因逻辑推理（abductive reasoning），在嘈杂和未充分指定的临床文本上实现鲁棒的自动推理，弥补纯LLM与纯符号方法之间的鸿沟。

#### System/Method Design

αNeSy-CTM是一个溯因神经符号学框架，将LLM与逻辑验证相结合。它利用LLM处理非结构化临床文本，并通过溯因推理机制对不确定和不完整的信息进行推理，最终输出可审计的匹配结果。

#### Experiments

与独立LLM基线（包括零样本基线）进行对比，αNeSy-CTM实现了最高30%的相对提升；与不使用溯因推理的神经符号学基线相比，在准确性、特异性和鲁棒性上均有改进；此外，αNeSy-CTM与思维链（CoT）推理表现出高度互补性。

#### Why It Matters

这项工作证明了神经符号学方法在自动化临床试验匹配中的有效性，为实现可审计、LLM驱动的下一代临床应用程序提供了可行路径。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM系统推理能力增强直接相关，特别是将LLM与符号逻辑推理（溯因推理）结合的神经符号学混合架构；涉及LLM在医疗领域高精度、可审计决策场景下的应用改进；与MoE/系统研究的间接关联在于其提出的混合路由策略（CoT与αNeSy-CTM互补）可能启发MoE中专家的路由设计。

#### Abstract

Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a promising path to automate Clinical Trial Matching (CTM), but still struggle with the deterministic verification required for complex eligibility criteria. Conversely, purely symbolic methods provide formal rigour but break down when faced with incomplete patient records and noisy clinical evidence. To bridge this gap, we investigate a hybrid framework for CTM combining LLMs with logical verification. In particular, we introduce an abductive neurosymbolic CTM framework (αNeSy-CTM), which leverages the linguistic and world knowledge in LLMs to support reasoning over noisy and underspecified clinical text. Extensive evaluation demonstrates that αNeSy-CTM substantially outperforms standalone LLM baselines, achieving up to 30% relative improvement over zero-shot baselines. In addition, our analyses confirm the impact of abductive reasoning on CTM, with αNeSy-CTM exhibiting improved accuracy, specificity, and robustness over a non-abductive neurosymbolic setting. Furthermore, αNeSy-CTM and Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning prove highly complementary, highlighting the potential for a hybrid routing policy. Ultimately, this paper demonstrates the impact of neurosymbolic methods for automating CTM, providing a path toward the next generation of auditable, LLM-driven clinical applications.

### [123] [Root Cause Analysis with Latent Confounders using Partial Ancestral Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20912)

*Henrique O. Caetano,Rafael Arone,Carlos Dias Maciel*

Main category: `cs.AI`

**TL;DR:** 提出PAG-RCA框架，通过将系统故障建模为部分祖先图（PAG）上的参数干预，并结合部分识别方法，在存在未观测潜变量和数据稀缺的条件下实现鲁棒根因分析。

#### Problem

现有基于因果理论的根因分析（RCA）方法假设因果充分性（即所有相关变量可观测），无法处理现实系统中普遍存在的未观测潜变量，导致在潜变量存在时性能退化。

#### Key Idea

将系统故障视为部分祖先图（PAG）上的参数干预，利用标准因果识别算法量化因果效应；当效应不可识别时，首次在RCA领域引入部分识别方法，通过分析性因果界对候选根因进行评分排序。

#### System/Method Design

PAG-RCA框架首先用PAG对系统进行建模以容纳潜变量，将故障视为参数干预；然后使用因果识别算法判断干预效应是否可识别：可识别时基于精确干预效应排序候选根因，不可识别时采用部分识别方法计算分析性因果界来评估和打分候选根因。

#### Experiments

在合成数据、微服务异常基准测试和电力网络级联故障数据集上评估，以多个SOTA数据驱动RCA方法为基线。PAG-RCA在所有场景下一致优于基线方法。

#### Why It Matters

首次将部分识别方法引入RCA领域，解决了现有方法在潜变量和数据稀缺场景下的根本性局限，提升了复杂部分可观测系统中自动化故障诊断的鲁棒性和可靠性。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高相关性。LLM/MoE推理系统是典型的部分可观测复杂系统（如分布式训练/推理中的故障诊断），PAG-RCA的潜变量建模和部分识别方法可直接应用于LLM服务集群的根因分析，尤其适合数据稀缺场景下的异常定位。

#### Abstract

Finding the source of failures, known as Root Cause Analysis (RCA), is essential for identifying the root causes of anomalies and maintaining the reliability of complex systems. While causal theory has advanced data-driven RCA, existing frameworks assume causal sufficiency, failing to account for the unobserved latent variables prevalent in real-world environments. To address this gap, we propose PAG-RCA. This framework models system failures as parametric interventions over Partial Ancestral Graphs (PAGs) to perform RCA in the presence of latent variables. We use standard causal identification algorithms to find the source of failures by quantifying causal effects over the PAG. When an effect is identifiable, candidate root causes are ranked based on their exact intervention effects. When effects are structurally unidentifiable, our framework (for the first time in the RCA literature) integrates partial identification to evaluate and score candidates using analytical causal bounds. By integrating latent variables and partial identification at once our framework ensures robust RCA even under data scarcity and latent-variable scenarios where traditional methods degrade. Evaluations on synthetic data, microservice anomaly benchmarks and power-grid cascading failures demonstrate that PAG-RCA consistently outperforms state-of-the-art data-driven baselines. By improving data-driven RCA performance under data scarcity, this methodology advances reliable automated diagnostics in partially observable complex networks.

### [124] [Apple Neural Engine: Architecture, Programming, and Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22283)

*Spencer H. Bryngelson*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** 本文通过逆向工程和直接测量，详细记录了Apple Neural Engine (ANE) 从A11到A18、M1到M5各代芯片的硬件架构、数据通路、编译器、程序格式、权重压缩方案、内核驱动及固件协议，提供了基于实测的完整技术规格。

#### Problem

ANE是Apple SoC中的专用矩阵加速器，但其硬件细节、编程接口和底层协议仅通过Core ML框架暴露给开发者，缺乏公开的底层技术文档，阻碍了研究人员对芯片进行精确的性能分析和底层优化研究。

#### Key Idea

通过直接测量（在M1和M5上）和对私有运行时、编译器、内核驱动及固件的静态分析，逆向还原ANE的完整技术栈，并将所有论断标注为"实测"、"反编译推导"或"预测"三类，明确记录方法和待解决问题。

#### System/Method Design

研究采用逆向工程方法：1) 对Apple Silicon进行直接硬件测量；2) 静态分析私有的Core ML运行时、ANE编译器、内核驱动和固件。文档覆盖：数据通路与Roofline模型（限制吞吐量和能耗的边界）、Core ML之下的调度路由、编译器和磁盘上的程序格式、权重压缩方案、内核驱动/固件/命令协议。涵盖A11-A18和M1-M5各代，提供逐芯片目标参数表和按设备/运算的兼容矩阵。

#### Experiments

直接测量在M1和M5芯片上进行；所有芯片族（A11-A18, M1-M5）均有逐芯片规格表。未提及具体性能数字或基准测试对比，测量聚焦于硬件参数和吞吐/能耗边界（Roofline模型）的标定。

#### Why It Matters

这是首个系统性地公开ANE底层技术细节的逆向工程报告，为硬件研究社区提供了过去仅有Apple内部团队才掌握的ANE架构信息。更重要的是，它披露了可从普通用户空间直接调用的底层路径（虽未文档化且版本脆弱），使得研究人员可以绕过Core ML进行精确测量和探索性工作，为Apple硬件加速器的深入研究打开了大门。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。ANE是Apple SoC中专用于矩阵乘法的固定功能加速器，直接对标LLM推理中最核心的矩阵运算。本文提供的Roofline模型、数据通路、程序格式和权重压缩方案，对于在Apple硬件上部署和优化LLM推理（包括MoE模型的矩阵计算）具有直接参考价值。底层直接调用路径的披露使得研究者可以绕过Core ML框架，进行更底层的推理延迟和吞吐量优化研究。此外，ANE的固定功能架构与GPU/TPU的对比也是异构计算系统研究的重要参考。

#### Abstract

The Apple Neural Engine (ANE) is the fixed-function matrix accelerator that has shipped in Apple systems-on-chip since the A11-class iPhone and iPad chips and the M1-class Mac chips, exposed to applications only through the Core ML model framework. This guide reports a reverse-engineered account of the engine, based on direct measurement on Apple silicon and static analysis of the private runtime, compiler, kernel driver, and firmware. It documents the datapath and the roofline that bound the engine's throughput and energy, the dispatch route that reaches it below Core ML, the compiler and on-disk program format, the weight-compression scheme, and the kernel driver, firmware, and command protocol beneath them. The account covers the A11 through A18 and M1 through M5 families, with per-chip target tables and an operation-by-device matrix; the direct measurements are on the M1 and M5. Claims are labeled as measured, decompile-derived, or predicted, and the methodology and open questions are recorded. The direct route is callable from ordinary user space but remains undocumented, unsupported, and version-fragile; it is intended for measurement, research, and on-device work, not for shipping software, where Core ML remains the supported path.

### [125] [FPGA-Accelerated Neuromorphic Vision System for Real-Time Orbital Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20727)

*Diego Hernández,Sebastián Valdivia,Vicente Westerhout,Esteban Vera,Daniel Yunge*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出了一个基于事件相机和FPGA加速的开源框架，用于轨道空间目标（RSO）检测，在8.5W功耗下实现97%检测精度和低于62ms的确定性延迟。

#### Problem

轨道空间日益严重的拥堵问题需要先进的监测解决方案，现有方法在能效、实时性和分布式部署方面存在不足。

#### Key Idea

利用事件相机（EBC）的低功耗、高时间分辨率特性，结合FPGA进行快速空间量化加速，并通过软硬件协同架构（FPGA+软件客户端）实现高效的分布式空间目标检测。

#### System/Method Design

系统架构包含三个关键部分：(1) 单台事件相机作为传感器；(2) FPGA可编程逻辑执行快速的网格聚类空间量化（grid clustering）；(3) 软件客户端负责聚类形成。采用分布式处理架构，将空间量化与聚类计算分离到硬件和软件层。

#### Experiments

基于EVAS数据集的夜间天空观测数据进行系统采样验证，达到了97%的RSO检测准确率。系统总功耗8.5W，确定性处理延迟低于62ms。

#### Why It Matters

该工作提供了首个开源的事件相机+FPGA空间目标检测框架，其极低功耗（8.5W）、高精度（97%）和确定性低延迟特性，使其成为分布式空间监测网络的有力候选方案。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

尽管本文专注于空间目标检测而非LLM/MoE，但其提出的FPGA加速网格聚类架构、软硬件协同分布式处理设计（FPGA+软件客户端分离计算负载），以及面向低功耗、低延迟的硬件加速思路，对LLM推理系统中的硬件加速（如FPGA加速注意力机制、KV cache offloading）和分布式系统设计具有参考价值。

#### Abstract

The escalating congestion in orbital space demands advanced monitoring solutions. This work presents a comprehensive open-source framework for neuromorphic resident space object (RSO) detection, adapting the foundational grid clustering algorithm for FPGA acceleration. The system integrates a single event-based camera (EBC) with a custom, distributed processing architecture, where rapid spatial quantization is executed in programmable logic (FPGA) and cluster formation is managed by a software client. We validate this architecture through systematic sampling of night-sky observations from the EVAS dataset, demonstrating 97% detection accuracy for RSOs. The implementation, which serves as a foundational toolkit for event-based FPGA processing, achieves efficient throughput with a total power consumption of 8.5 W and deterministic processing latencies below 62 ms. The architecture's energy efficiency and high-precision detection position it as a viable solution for distributed space surveillance networks.

### [126] [A3C3: AI Algorithm and Accelerator Co-design, Co-search, and Co-generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20869)

*Selin Yildirim,Yingbing Huang,Deming Chen*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出A3C3，一种联合优化神经网络架构与硬件加速器的协同设计、搜索与生成方法论，以自动生成在精度、延迟、吞吐量、能效和硬件利用率之间更好权衡的模型-加速器对。

#### Problem

传统AI部署流程将模型设计和硬件映射分离，先开发算法追求精度，之后再适配硬件约束，导致系统整体性能次优，尤其难以应对现代AI工作负载的异构性、内存密集性和平台依赖性。

#### Key Idea

将算法和加速器的设计空间统一参数化，并进行联合搜索（协同设计与协同搜索），而非顺序独立优化，从而自动生成端到端更优的模型-加速器组合。

#### System/Method Design

A3C3（AI算法与加速器协同设计、协同搜索、协同生成）是一个整体方法论，将神经网络架构与硬件实现的设计空间同时参数化，并联合搜索最优的模型-加速器对，实现从算法到硬件的自动化协同生成。

#### Experiments

摘要中未明确提供实验设置、基线、数据集、指标或具体数值结果，仅说明该工作是《嵌入式机器学习手册》的一章。

#### Why It Matters

该工作打破了算法与硬件分离设计的传统范式，为异质化、内存密集的现代AI工作负载提供了自动化联合优化的新路径，有助于在资源受限的嵌入式场景中实现更高效的AI部署。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接关联LLM系统和硬件加速研究：LLM推理面临内存带宽瓶颈和计算密集问题，A3C3的协同设计思想可推广至LLM模型（如Transformer架构）与专用加速器（如NPU、FPGA）的联合优化；对MoE模型而言，其异构路由特性更需算法-硬件协同设计来优化负载均衡和通信开销。此外，该工作涉及延迟、吞吐量、能效和硬件利用率等系统级指标，对分布式推理和边缘部署有参考价值。

#### Abstract

We present a holistic methodology for artificial intelligence algorithm and accelerator co-design, co-search, and co-generation (A3C3), which jointly optimizes neural network architectures and their hardware implementations to address the inefficiencies of traditional top-down AI system design flows. Conventional AI deployment often treats model design and hardware mapping as separate stages: an algorithm is first developed for accuracy, and only afterward adapted to meet latency, throughput, energy, or resource constraints. This separation can lead to suboptimal systems, particularly as modern AI workloads become increasingly heterogeneous, memory-intensive, and platform-dependent. A3C3 instead parameterizes both algorithmic and accelerator design spaces and searches them jointly, enabling the automatic generation of model-accelerator pairs that better balance accuracy, latency, throughput, energy efficiency, and hardware utilization. This article is a book chapter of the Handbook of Embedded Machine Learning, edited by Sudeep Pasricha and Muhammad Shafique, Springer Nature.

### [127] [Closing the Loop on LLM-Generated RTL Assertions with Quality-Aware Formal Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21451)

*Ramesh Krishnamurthy,Danial Chitnis,Themis Prodromakis*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** 提出一个轻量级开源框架，通过突变引导的精炼、求解器选择与因果叙事合成三个环节闭环提升LLM生成的RTL断言质量，解决形式化验证中断言弱、求解成本波动大、失败跟踪难解释的问题。

#### Problem

基于LLM的RTL断言生成在形式化验证中面临三个实际问题：1) 生成的断言可能因错误原因通过验证（如空虚断言）；2) 不同设计间证明代价差异巨大；3) 失败轨迹难以解释。

#### Key Idea

将断言生成后的质量感知闭环作为关键步骤，通过突变引导剔除弱断言、基于RTL结构选择SMT求解器、以及因果叙事合成来解释证明失败原因，形成一体化框架。

#### System/Method Design

框架包含三个核心组件：1) 突变引导的精炼（mutation-guided refinement），用于拒绝弱断言（包括空虚断言和无法区分故障行为的断言）；2) 求解器选择阶段（solver-selection stage），根据RTL结构从候选SMT后端中自动选择；3) 因果叙事合成（causal narrative synthesis），生成基于反例轨迹的失败解释。

#### Experiments

在多个不同的RTL设计上评估：1) 提升了生成断言的置信度；2) 相比固定求解器选择，减少了运行时波动；3) 生成的失败解释始终基于反例轨迹。具体基线、指标和量化结果在摘要中未明确说明。

#### Why It Matters

指出"质量感知闭环"（而非仅断言生成本身）是LLM辅助形式化验证中缺失的关键步骤，将LLM生成能力与形式化验证的严谨性有效衔接，对提升硬件验证自动化水平有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接关联LLM系统：利用LLM生成RTL形式化断言，并解决LLM输出质量不可靠的核心系统问题。求解器选择涉及运行时优化与调度，因果叙事合成涉及可解释性，均属LLM系统推理与可靠性研究方向。但与MoE、KV cache、分布式训练等方向无直接关联。

#### Abstract

Large language model (LLM) based assertion generation is making formal verification more accessible for Register Transfer Level (RTL) designs, but three practical issues remain. Generated properties can pass for the wrong reason, proof cost can vary widely from one design to another, and failing traces are hard to interpret. This paper presents a lightweight, open-source framework that addresses these issues in one loop. Our method combines mutation-guided refinement to reject weak assertions, including vacuous ones and those that fail to distinguish faulty behaviour, a solver-selection stage that chooses among candidate Satisfiability Modulo Theories (SMT) backends using RTL structure, and causal narrative synthesis to explain why a proof failed. Across diverse RTL designs, the framework improves confidence in generated assertions, reduces runtime variability over fixed-solver choices, and produces failure explanations that remain grounded in the counterexample trace. The results suggest that quality-aware closure, rather than assertion generation alone, is the missing step for practical LLM-assisted formal verification.

### [128] [COMPOSE: Static Timing-driven Composable Reconfigurable Architecture for Accelerating Recurrence-Bound Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21454)

*Rohan Juneja,Vishruti Ranjan,Rakshith Harish,Li-Shiuan Peh*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** COMPOSE 提出一种可组合的粗粒度可重构架构（CGRA），通过编译时基于静态时序信息动态形成处理单元（PE），实现跨循环迭代的空间融合与松弛利用，从而提升吞吐量并降低能耗。

#### Problem

传统 CGRA 使用固定大小的处理单元（PE）静态绑定操作，导致跨迭代依赖必须通过串行调度解决，限制了循环级并行度；同时静态调度无法利用操作间的时序松弛，造成资源利用率低和延迟增加；频繁的中间结果注册加剧了寄存器文件和局部存储的压力，引入冗余的数据移动开销，降低能效。

#### Key Idea

在编译时利用静态时序信息指导 PE 的动态可组合形成：通过空间融合跨循环迭代的操作来消除串行化依赖，选择性利用时序松弛减少延迟浪费，并延迟输出注册以减少寄存器文件压力和冗余内存流量。

#### System/Method Design

COMPOSE 是一种可组合 CGRA 架构，核心在于 PE 在编译时根据静态时序信息动态形成，而非固定的静态绑定。通过空间融合（spatial fusion）将跨循环迭代的操作组合在一起，解决迭代间依赖；通过选择性利用时序松弛实现低延迟执行；通过推迟中间结果的输出注册（当结果可被局部消费时）来降低寄存器文件压力和内存流量。

#### Experiments

在多种工作负载上进行评估，以性能提升和 EDP（Energy-Delay Product）作为指标，与现有最先进（SOTA）CGRA 方案对比。平均实现 1.6 倍性能提升和 2.9 倍 EDP 降低，且面积和功耗开销极低。具体的基准测试、基线方法和数据集未在摘要中详述。

#### Why It Matters

该工作突破了传统 CGRA 因固定 PE 结构和静态调度导致的并行度瓶颈与能效限制，为可重构架构在高并行度、低延迟和低能耗场景下的应用提供了新的设计范式，对计算密集型加速器设计有重要参考价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽不直接针对 LLM 或 MoE，但 CGRA 架构与 LLM 推理加速（如矩阵乘法、卷积等计算密集型算子）以及边缘/嵌入式场景下的低功耗部署高度相关。COMPOSE 在提升并行度、减少数据移动和降低能耗方面的思路，对设计面向 LLM 推理的专用加速器或可重构 AI 芯片有借鉴意义。

#### Abstract

Coarse-Grained Reconfigurable Architectures (CGRAs) provide a spatially programmable substrate well suited for accelerating compute-intensive workloads with abundant parallelism. However, traditional CGRA execution models rely on rigid, fixed-size processing elements (PEs) that are statically bound to individual operations, which forces inter-iteration dependencies to be resolved through serialized scheduling. This limits throughput and reduces parallelism across loop iterations. Moreover, static execution schedules often fail to exploit available timing slack between operations, leading to resource underutilization and increased latency. The frequent registering of intermediate results further exacerbates pressure on register files and local memories, introducing data movement overheads that reduce energy efficiency, particularly in power or memory constrained environments.
  To address these challenges, we introduce COMPOSE, a composable CGRA architecture that enables dynamic formation of PEs at compile time guided by static timing information. By spatially fusing operations across loop iterations and selectively utilizing slack, COMPOSE resolves inter-iteration dependencies that limit throughput and enables low latency execution by reducing slack wastage. Additionally, the architecture reduces register file pressure by deferring output registration when intermediate values remain locally consumable, which significantly lowers redundant memory traffic. Across a diverse set of workloads, COMPOSE on average delivers 1.6x performance improvement and 2.9x EDP reduction over state-of-the-art (SOTA), at minimal area and power overheads.

### [129] [Row-Based Layout Synthesis for Analog Circuits Using Height-Quantized Primitives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21767)

*Endalk Y. Gebru,Ramprasath S.,Ramesh Harjani,Sachin S. Sapatnekar*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** 提出了一种针对先进工艺节点（如FinFET）下模拟与混合信号电路的量化行高布局综合方法，通过将模拟模块映射到量化高度的行中，有效缩小了仿真到硅片的性能差距。

#### Problem

在FinFET等先进工艺节点中，严格的设计规则和强烈的版图依赖效应使得模拟与混合信号电路的版图自动化越来越困难，传统设计方法难以在电气性能和物理布局之间取得良好平衡。

#### Key Idea

通过将模拟构建块映射到量化高度的行中，并基于电路需求和版图约束优化行高结构（row height fabric），从而在保持自动化效率的同时缩小仿真到硅片的性能差距。

#### System/Method Design

提出了一种量化行高版图综合方法：首先根据电路需求和版图约束优化行高结构，然后将模拟构建块映射到量化高度的行中，最终生成满足设计规则的版图。该方法在不牺牲自动化程度的前提下引入了量化高度约束。

#### Experiments

在多个测试用例上与约束较少的自定义基线设计进行对比。量化高度设计将原理图到后仿真性能差距缩小了最高68.5%，在大多数测试用例中面积更小，最大面积缩减达24.1%。

#### Why It Matters

随着工艺节点不断演进，AMS版图自动化成为关键瓶颈。该工作提供了一种实用的综合方法，在自动化流程中显著缩小了仿真到硅片的性能差距，同时实现了面积优化，对先进工艺下的AMS电路设计自动化具有实际价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该论文主要聚焦于模拟/混合信号电路的版图自动化，与LLM系统、MoE、推理加速、KV缓存等方向的直接关联较低。但其在物理设计自动化中的布局优化思路（量化约束下的结构化映射）可能对芯片设计自动化（EDA）中的AI辅助布局布线方法有一定启发意义。

#### Abstract

Restrictive design rules and strong layout-dependent effects have tightened the coupling between physical layout decisions and electrical performance in advanced process nodes, such as FinFET, making analog and mixed-signal (AMS) layout automation increasingly difficult. This paper presents a quantized row-height layout synthesis methodology for AMS circuits, a methodology that has previously been shown to reduce the simulation-to-silicon gap. The proposed flow optimizes a row height fabric from circuit requirements and layout constraints while mapping analog building blocks into quantized-height rows. Results on multiple testcases demonstrate that the proposed flow synthesizes layouts with similar postlayout performance relative to less-constrained custom baseline designs, with comparable performance metrics. Our quantized-height designs are shown to reduce the schematic-to-postlayout performance gap by up to 68.5% and result in lower area for most of our testcases, with a maximum area reduction of 24.1%.

### [130] [AgentDSE: Reasoning-Augmented Architectural Design Space Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21836)

*Chenyu Wang,Jiahe Caroline Shi,David Kong,Duane S. Boning,Zishen Wan,Yilun Du,Vijay Janapa Reddi*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** AgentDSE 提出一种由通用大语言模型（LLM）编程智能体驱动的模拟器内循环方法，将架构设计空间探索（DSE）从黑箱优化转变为可解释的推理驱动过程，在多个任务上以少两个数量级的评估次数达到接近或更优的设计质量。

#### Problem

传统架构设计空间探索（DSE）效率极低，通常需要数万次模拟器评估，根本原因在于传统方法将模拟器视为黑箱预言机，无法像人类架构师那样利用物理约束、性能瓶颈、数据复用和工作负载结构等知识进行推理引导。

#### Key Idea

利用通用大语言模型（LLM）编程智能体自动化人类架构师的推理循环，让智能体"理解"模拟器输出、进行架构推理，并生成下一步探索决策，从而将黑箱优化转变为可解释的推理驱动过程。

#### System/Method Design

AgentDSE 是一种模拟器内循环方法，核心是一个通用 LLM 编程智能体。该方法无需模型微调、预计算设计数据库或领域特定的优化器代码。智能体读取模拟器反馈，通过架构推理自动生成下一步设计决策，形成闭环探索流程。

#### Experiments

在三个任务上评估：DNN 加速器映射搜索、硬件/软件协同设计、CPU 缓存层次结构优化。与现有方法相比，AgentDSE 以少两个数量级（up to 100x）的模拟器评估次数，达到了具有竞争力或更优的设计质量。

#### Why It Matters

该方法不仅大幅提升了 DSE 的效率（评估次数减少两个数量级），还生成了可追溯的探索轨迹，能够揭示架构假设、性能瓶颈、隐式先验和模拟器伪影，使每次搜索决策都可追溯而不再埋没在优化器状态中，为架构设计提供了可解释性和新的洞察能力。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该工作直接展示了 LLM（通用大语言模型）作为智能体在计算机架构系统设计自动化中的应用，属于 LLM for Systems 方向。其方法涉及硬件/软件协同设计、DNN 加速器映射和缓存优化，对 LLM 推理系统的硬件架构设计、编译器映射优化以及系统级设计空间探索有参考价值。同时，AgentDSE 的高效探索范式可启发将 LLM 智能体应用于分布式系统配置调优、MoE 路由策略搜索等系统优化问题。

#### Abstract

Traditional architectural design space exploration (DSE) is highly inefficient, typically requiring tens of thousands of simulator evaluations across various optimization methods. This inefficiency arises because conventional methods treat the simulator as a black-box oracle. In contrast, human architects effectively guide exploration by reasoning through physical constraints, performance bottlenecks, data reuse, and workload structures. To bridge this gap, we introduce AgentDSE, a simulator-in-the-loop methodology driven by a general-purpose large language model (LLM) coding agent. AgentDSE automates this architectural-reasoning loop without requiring model fine-tuning, precomputed design databases, or domain-specific optimizer code. Across deep neural network (DNN) accelerator mapping, hardware/software co-design, and CPU cache-hierarchy optimization, AgentDSE achieves competitive or better design quality with up to two orders of magnitude fewer evaluations. AgentDSE also produces inspectable traces that surface architectural hypotheses, performance cliffs, implicit priors, and simulator artifacts, making every search decision traceable rather than buried in optimizer state.

### [131] [DejaVu: Why You Should Write to Your DRAM Rows Twice, Carefully](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22297)

*Haocong Luo,İsmail Emir Yüksel,Ataberk Olgun,Nisa Bostanci,Orhun Ecemiş,Abdullah Giray Yağlıkçı,Onur Mutlu*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** 本文首次实验证明了DejaVu现象：先前写入DRAM单元的数据会影响DRAM对读干扰的脆弱性。

#### Problem

DRAM读干扰（Rowhammer）的脆弱性评估通常忽略数据写入历史的影响，导致对实际可靠性和安全边界的估计不准确。

#### Key Idea

DRAM单元中已写入的数据状态会影响后续读干扰下的电荷泄漏行为——写入相反数据会降低抗干扰能力（ACmin降低），写入相同数据两次则会提升抗干扰能力（ACmin升高）。

#### System/Method Design

在112颗来自三大制造商的商用DDR4 DRAM芯片上进行实验表征，定义了ACmin（引发位翻转的最小攻击行激活次数）作为关键指标，对比了三种数据初始化模式：基线（仅写入一次）、写入相反数据、写入相同数据两次。提出了两种假设解释：1）相反数据写入导致单元电荷恢复不足；2）电荷陷阱态变化影响泄漏电流。

#### Experiments

使用112颗COTS DDR4 DRAM芯片（三大制造商）。相比基线（仅写入一次）：1）写入相反数据会降低ACmin（使DRAM更脆弱）；2）写入相同数据两次会增加ACmin（增强鲁棒性）。此外，在32行MAJ-3 PUD操作中，用DejaVu模式初始化DRAM行后，失效位线数量平均减少32.7%。

#### Why It Matters

该发现揭示了DRAM可靠性评估中一个被忽视的关键因素——数据写入历史，对DRAM测试方法学、安全性评估和读干扰缓解技术设计都有重要影响。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM推理系统中的DRAM可靠性直接相关：1）大型模型推理依赖大量DRAM，DejaVu影响内存子系统的位错误率；2）PUD（Processing-Using-DRAM）操作为近内存计算提供新思路；3）读干扰缓解阈值需额外降低6.3%（20%阈值缩减）带来性能开销，影响内存密集型LLM推理系统的整体效率。

#### Abstract

We provide the first experimental demonstration of DejaVu, a phenomenon where the data previously written to DRAM cells affects DRAM's vulnerability to read disturbance. Our experimental characterization using 112 COTS DDR4 DRAM chips from all three major manufacturers shows that, compared to the baseline where we initialize the victim row by writing to it only once, 1) overwriting it with the opposite data reduces ACmin, the minimum aggressor row activation count to induce a bitflip, and 2) writing the same data twice increases ACmin. We provide two hypotheses to explain DejaVu. First, we hypothesize that overwriting the victim row with opposite data values causes under-restoration of charge in DRAM cells. Second, we hypothesize that overwriting the victim row changes charge trap states in the active region, affecting read-disturbance-induced cell leakage current. We conduct controlled characterization to provide insight into these hypotheses. We further characterize the reliability of Processing-Using-DRAM (PUD) operations with DRAM rows initialized with DejaVu patterns. Our characterization of 32-row MAJ-3 operation shows that overwriting the DRAM rows used in the operation reduces the number of bitlines that fail to reliably perform MAJ-3 by 32.7% on average compared to the baseline where rows are written only once. Based on our observations, we describe two major implications of DejaVu. We show how DRAM testing and characterization methodologies should account for DejaVu to accurately characterize read disturbance vulnerability under fixed data patterns and rigorously study data-pattern effects without unintended interference from DejaVu. We also evaluate the performance overhead of read disturbance mitigation techniques when thresholds need to be lowered to be secure against DejaVu, showing a 6.3% overhead when reducing the threshold by 20%.

### [132] [NeutronSparse: Coordinating Heterogeneous Engines for Sparse Matrix Multiplication on NPUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22482)

*Xin Ai,Zeyu Ling,Hao Yuan,Qiange Wang,Yanfeng Zhang,Yutao Peng,Ge Yu*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** NeutronSparse 是一个面向 NPU (Ascend 910B) 的协调优先 (coordination-first) 稀疏矩阵乘法框架，通过异构计算单元的自适应负载均衡和数据 tile 的局部性感知编排，在稀疏计算场景下首次超越 GPU 库 (cuSPARSE) 性能。

#### Problem

NPU 上高性能 SpMM 面临数据管理挑战：不规则稀疏性对数据组织和调度提出高要求。在 Ascend 910B 上，官方 MindSpore 实现仅达到 GPU (NVIDIA A100) cuSPARSE 库 36.3% 的性能，核心瓶颈在于 tile 执行模型下异构计算单元之间缺乏高效的协调机制。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察是：NPU 上 SpMM 的性能瓶颈不在于计算能力不足，而在于异构计算单元间缺乏协调配合；通过"协调优先"的设计思路，可以释放 NPU 在稀疏计算上的潜力，甚至超越 GPU。

#### System/Method Design

NeutronSparse 包含两大关键技术：(1) 稀疏感知的异构引擎协调 (Sparsity-aware coordination of heterogeneous engines) —— 根据稀疏模式自适应地划分和平衡异构计算单元间的工作负载，保持各单元持续忙碌；(2) 局部性感知的 tile 编排 (Locality-aware tile orchestrating) —— 对数据 tile 进行重组和重用，减少冗余计算和内存搬运开销。

#### Experiments

在 Ascend 910B 上评估，NeutronSparse 相比 NPU 基线取得 1.26x-7.78x 加速比；相比 NVIDIA A100 上的领先 GPU 库 (cuSPARSE) 取得 1.03x-3.07x 加速比，展示了 NPU 在稀疏计算中未被挖掘的潜力。摘要未明确说明具体数据集、稀疏模式类型和评测模型。

#### Why It Matters

这是首个在稀疏矩阵乘法场景下使国产 NPU (Ascend 910B) 性能超越 NVIDIA A100 GPU 的工作，证明了通过系统级协调优化可以弥补甚至扭转 NPU 与 GPU 在稀疏计算上的差距，对国产 AI 芯片生态发展具有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。SpMM 是图神经网络、推荐系统等大规模稀疏计算的核心算子；在 MoE (混合专家) 模型中，稀疏门控路由也涉及类似的不规则稀疏计算模式。该工作关于异构计算单元协调、tile 编排和负载均衡的技术，可直接启发 LLM 推理系统中稀疏注意力、MoE 专家路由的 NPU 加速方案，以及分布式系统中跨计算单元的调度优化。

#### Abstract

Sparse matrix-matrix multiplication (SpMM) is a fundamental data operation for large-scale sparse data processing. With NPUs increasingly deployed in data centers for their performance and energy efficiency, accelerating SpMM on these platforms is a natural choice. However, high-performance SpMM on NPUs poses a data management challenge, as irregular sparsity demands efficient data organization and scheduling. On Ascend 910B, the official MindSpore implementation achieves only 36.3% of the performance of GPU-based sparse libraries such as cuSPARSE on NVIDIA A100. To this end, we conduct an in-depth architectural analysis of SpMM execution on NPUs versus GPU and identify that the key performance bottleneck for SpMM on NPUs lies in the lack of efficient coordination across heterogeneous compute units under tile-based execution model. Therefore, we propose NeutronSparse, a coordination-first SpMM framework for NPUs. NeutronSparse integrates two key techniques: (i) Sparsity-aware coordination of heterogeneous engines, which adaptively partitions and balances workloads between heterogeneous compute units to keep them busy, and (ii) Locality-aware tile orchestrating, which reorganizes and reuses data tiles to reduce redundant computation and memory movement overhead. Evaluations on Ascend 910B show that NeutronSparse achieves 1.26x-7.78x speedup over NPU baselines and 1.03x-3.07x speedup over leading GPU libraries on NVIDIA A100, revealing untapped potential of NPUs for sparse computation.

### [133] [Non-Uniform L2 Cache Latency Across the Streaming Multiprocessors of an NVIDIA L40](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22588)

*Faruk Alpay,Baris Basaran*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** 本文发现NVIDIA L40 GPU的L2缓存延迟并非统一的常数，而是取决于发出加载指令的物理SM，并利用该特性实现内核自定位和设备指纹识别，进而优化延迟敏感型工作负载。

#### Problem

NVIDIA GPU的L2缓存通常被建模为一个统一池且具有单一命中延迟，但本文发现这在内核看到的粒度上是不正确的——不同物理SM的L2命中延迟存在显著差异（52%的范围），这一差异被现有模型忽略。

#### Key Idea

通过轮询序列化、基于%smid解析的探测方法，一次性映射所有142个SM的L2命中延迟，发现延迟由SM项和分片项加性决定（$R^2=0.87$），且SM的延迟模式与AD102 GPC布局的二分对称性高度相关（$r=0.999$），表明该效应是物理层面的。

#### System/Method Design

提出了一种轮询序列化、SMID解析的延迟探测方法，单次内核启动即可映射所有SM的L2延迟。建立了加性模型 $L = \mu + a(\mathrm{sm}) + b(\mathrm{slice})$ 解释延迟变化。该方法可作为自定位和指纹识别原语：内核读取自身在设备上的物理放置位置和设备身份，不窃取其他进程的秘密数据。

#### Experiments

在NVIDIA L40（142个SM）上进行探测，L2命中延迟范围222-339周期（52%范围），噪声低于0.01周期。加性模型$R^2=0.87$（加一个秩1项达0.98）。SM项呈二分对称性（两半72个SM相关度$r=0.999$），独立访问模式每SM相关度$r=1.000$。该模式在Blackwell RTX 5090上同样有效。单个用户级探测可在设备内以92%准确率识别SM，区分两台物理相同的L40准确率100%（尽管平均延迟几乎相同，per-SM映射$r=0.63$）。延迟映射在满负载运行一小时后保持不变。利用该映射分布延迟受限工作可将完工时间缩短最多11%。

#### Why It Matters

该工作揭示了GPU微架构中一个被忽视的物理特性——L2缓存延迟的SM间差异性，并将其转化为一个实用的自定位和硬件指纹识别原语。这不仅可用于优化延迟敏感型内核的调度（最多11%的性能提升），还为GPU安全领域提供了硬件级设备识别能力，且不依赖任何秘密数据泄露。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。LLM推理中的注意力机制和MoE路由等任务对延迟敏感，本文揭示的L2缓存延迟SM间差异可用于优化内核在SM间的任务分布，减少延迟开销。同时，该硬件指纹识别方法对GPU系统安全、多设备环境下的身份验证有潜在应用价值。此外，该工作展示了微观架构特性（L2缓存分片、SM-GPC布局）对系统性能的显著影响，对理解GPU存储层次和调度优化具有参考意义。

#### Abstract

The NVIDIA L40 exposes a 96 MiB L2 cache usually modeled as one uniform pool with a single hit latency. We show this is wrong at the granularity a kernel sees: L2-hit latency depends strongly and reproducibly on which physical streaming multiprocessor (SM) issues the load. A turn-serialized, %smid-resolved probe maps the hit latency across all 142 SMs in one launch; it is not a constant near 279 cycles but spans 222-339 cycles (a 52% range), with per-repetition noise below 0.01 cycles. An additive model $L = μ+ a(\mathrm{sm}) + b(\mathrm{slice})$ explains $R^2 = 0.87$ (0.98 with one rank-1 term), and the SM term is two-fold symmetric (two halves of 72 SMs at correlation $r = 0.999$), following the AD102 GPC layout. Independent access patterns agree per SM at $r = 1.000$, so the effect is physical. The same probe on a Blackwell RTX 5090 shows it generalizes, while the per-die pattern is device-specific. Read as a fingerprint, a single user-level probe identifies the SM within a device at 92%, and two physically identical L40s are separated at 100% despite near-identical mean latency (per-SM map $r = 0.63$): a per-die hardware identity, not a clock artifact. This is a self-localization and fingerprinting primitive: a kernel reads its own placement and device, not a victim's, and extracts no secret data. The map is stable, unchanged after an hour at full utilization on both devices. As a consequence, distributing latency-bound work by the map cuts makespan by up to 11%. Single-thread capacity, line-tag, prefetch-modifier, and persisting-L2 results appear as controls. The artifact contains seeds, raw observations, the trained model, and regeneration scripts.

### [134] [Multi-Level Resistive Synapses for On-Chip Neural Networks: A Physics-Based Design of a Memristive Crossbar Fabric with Quasi-Continuous Conductance States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22621)

*David Alejandro Trejo Pizzo*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出了一种基于多电平忆阻突触的物理级片上神经网络设计，构建了支持密集电导状态的模拟存内神经处理器，并展示了其对大语言模型推理的显著能效优势。

#### Problem

传统CMOS架构和二进制ReRAM在运行大语言模型时面临严重的"权重搬运"开销（Von Neumann瓶颈），同时现有忆阻器件在支持多电平电导状态时受到热噪声、漂移和量子化电导的限制，难以实现高精度模拟计算。

#### Key Idea

基于离子输运物理建立忆阻器件的状态变量模型，量化噪声和漂移下的可存储子电平；将多电平忆阻突触集成到1T1R交叉开关阵列中，在模拟域中物理执行推理、反向传播和权重更新，实现完整的原生存内计算。

#### System/Method Design

采用HfO₂基材料堆栈，通过FEOL/BEOL CMOS流片集成工艺制造1T1R交叉开关阵列；设计差分突触结构实现符号权重；推导模拟VMM在线阻影响下的线性代数；设计模拟域多层流水线执行推理、反向传播和原位外积学习规则（离散化到电导格点）；包含忆阻-FPGA神经形态系统、电流模式translinear softmax的存内自注意力引擎，以及针对三元BitNet的数据通路。

#### Experiments

提供了能量、面积、容量和瓦片间通信模型；三元BitNet数据通路展示了比先进CPU/GPU高数个数量级的单token能效（per-token efficiency）。文中未提供与具体LLM基准测试的对比实验结果，主要基于理论建模和投影分析。

#### Why It Matters

该工作提供了从物理器件级到系统级的完整硬件原生蓝图，消除了权重搬运开销，展示了模拟存内计算在LLM推理上相对于数字CMOS的颠覆性能效潜力，为后摩尔时代AI加速器提供了切实可行的物理实现路径。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。该设计直接面向LLM推理加速，通过模拟存内计算从根本上消除权重搬运瓶颈；包含存内自注意力引擎和三元BitNet数据通路，直接针对Transformer核心计算；其多电平忆阻突触和模拟VMM对MoE架构中大量参数矩阵的存内计算具有启发意义；电流模式translinear softmax为端到端模拟推理提供关键组件；瓦片间通信模型涉及大规模分布式神经处理器架构设计。

#### Abstract

Building on resistive communication, this paper presents a physics-based design of an on-chip neural network with multi-level memristive synapses supporting a dense spectrum of conductance states. Derived from ionic transport physics, we develop a state-variable model and quantify storable sub-levels under thermal noise, drift, and quantized conductance. We assemble these devices into a 1T1R crossbar fabric, derive the linear algebra of analog vector-matrix multiplication (VMM) under wire resistance, and design a differential synapse for signed weights. A multilayer pipeline executes inference, backpropagation, and weight updates physically in the analog domain. We derive the in-situ outer-product learning rule, its discretization onto the conductance lattice, and the resulting quantization noise. We provide energy, area, capacity, and inter-tile models, showing this substrate is ideally suited for large language models (LLMs). Our design eliminates weight movement, surpassing binary ReRAM and traditional CMOS. We detail the material stack (HfO_2-based), the FEOL/BEOL CMOS foundry-integration flow, a self-contained SPICE model, the complete memristive-FPGA neuromorphic system, and an in-memory self-attention engine with current-mode translinear softmax. Finally, a ternary BitNet datapath shows projected per-token efficiency orders of magnitude better than advanced CPUs or GPUs. The result is a self-contained hardware-native blueprint for a high-density, analog, in-memory neural processor.

*Nika Mansouri Ghiasi,Konstantina Koliogeorgi,Onur Mutlu*

#### Problem

高通量、低成本的生物数据生成带来了巨大机遇，但传统计算系统无法跟上数据生成速率，且在能效、扩展性、隐私和安全性方面面临严重挑战，阻碍了生物医学技术的广泛应用。

摘要中未明确提及具体的实验设置、基准测试或实验结果。本文是一篇简短的白皮书/倡议介绍性质的文章。

该工作的重要性在于：它首次系统性地将计算机架构设计与医疗健康领域的计算需求联系起来，推动跨学科协作，有望引导计算系统设计者关注生物医学这一重要但被忽视的应用领域，从而加速精准医疗和个性化医疗的发展。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然本文未直接聚焦LLM或MoE，但高度相关于LLM/系统研究：生物数据分析中的高通量数据处理、能效优化、分布式扩展、隐私安全（如联邦学习）等挑战，与LLM训练/推理中的系统优化问题高度相似。Arch4Health探讨的计算机架构设计思路（如专用加速器、内存层级优化）对LLM推理加速、KV缓存管理、分布式并行计算等方向具有参考价值。

#### Abstract

Recent biotechnological advances enable high-throughput, low-cost, and accurate biological data generation. This wealth of data enables unique opportunities for advancing healthcare. Despite these opportunities, efficiently analyzing large-scale biological data poses significant challenges for conventional computing systems. These systems often cannot keep up with the high-throughput rate at which data is generated, and they face additional constraints related to energy efficiency, scalability, privacy, and security. Therefore, to facilitate the wide adoption of recent advances in healthcare, there is a need to optimize the computing systems to enable high-performance, energy-efficient, low-cost, private, and secure analysis of biological data.
  We introduce the Architecture for Health (Arch4Health) initiative, which aims to (i) identify and analyze key computational challenges in current and future health- and life science-related applications and (ii) explore how computer architects and computing system designers can advance healthcare by addressing these challenges. In this short paper, we first present the motivations behind the Arch4Health initiative and, second, elaborate on its vision and goals, related topics, Arch4Health workshops, and future outlooks.

### [136] [Clutch: High Performance Vector-Scalar Comparison using DRAM via Chunked Temporal Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22812)

*Daichi Tokuda,Tatsuya Kubo,Ismail Emir Yuksel,Ataberk Olgun,Haocong Luo,Tomoya Nagatani,Geraldo F. Oliveira,Abdullah Giray Yağlıkçı,Mohammad Sadrosadati,Onur Mutlu,Shinya Takamaeda-Yamazaki*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** Clutch提出了一种基于时序编码和查表的向量-标量比较加速方法，在PuD（Processing-using-DRAM）系统上实现了比最先进的按位串行PuD实现平均2.9倍吞吐量提升和3.0倍能效提升。

#### Problem

向量-标量比较是数据密集型负载中的基础操作，但由于计算强度低，执行受限于内存带宽。现有PuD方案采用按位串行执行模型，其比较操作的算法复杂度随操作数位宽增长，导致DRAM命令开销成为主要瓶颈，限制了应用级加速效果。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是：1) 使用时序编码（temporal coding）将向量值编码为前导1序列，从而将比较操作转化为对DRAM行的查表访问；2) 为控制高精度下的查找表内存开销，将操作数划分为多个多比特块（chunk），对各块独立使用紧凑查找表进行比较，再通过PuD高效的方式合并各块结果。

#### System/Method Design

Clutch包含三个关键技术组件：1) 时序编码：将每个向量值编码为前导1序列，使向量-标量比较变为对DRAM行的查表操作；2) 分块比较：将操作数拆分为多个多比特块，每个块使用紧凑的查找表独立比较，以控制内存占用；3) PuD高效的合并过程：将各块的比较结果合并得到最终结果。通过调整分块数量，可在吞吐量和内存使用之间灵活权衡。

#### Experiments

实验评估了两个应用场景：谓词评估（predicate evaluation）和决策树推理（decision tree inference）。对比基线包括高度优化的CPU和GPU实现，以及最先进的按位串行PuD实现。Clutch在端到端应用吞吐量上平均比CPU和GPU分别提升12倍和69倍，比最先进的按位串行PuD方案提升2.9倍；在能效上比CPU和GPU分别提升12倍和69倍（原文如此），比按位串行PuD提升3.0倍。

#### Why It Matters

这项工作首次将决策树推理映射到PuD执行，拓展了PuD的应用领域。Clutch解决了PuD系统中按位串行比较的高命令开销问题，为内存-bound操作提供了一种高效的替代方案，对数据密集型计算架构有重要参考价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然该论文主要面向数据库和决策树推理，但其PuD加速方法和时序编码思想对LLM系统有一定启发性：1) LLM推理中大量GEMV（门控矩阵-向量乘法）和MoE的稀疏计算同样面临内存-bound问题，PuD架构可能成为替代方案；2) 向量-标量比较是LLM中Top-K路由选择、阈值过滤等操作的基础原语，Clutch的高效比较方法可潜在加速MoE路由和推理预处理阶段；3) 该工作展示了在DRAM阵列内实现高效计算的新路径，对探索存内计算加速LLM推理有参考意义。

#### Abstract

Vector-scalar comparison is a fundamental computation primitive that compares each element in a vector against a single scalar value. It is widely used in various data-intensive workloads from databases to machine learning. Due to its low computational intensity, its execution tends to be memory-bound, limiting the utilization of compute resources. Processing-using-DRAM (PuD) is an emerging computing paradigm that performs massively parallel bitwise operations directly inside DRAM arrays, alleviating off-chip data movement. Existing PuD-based approaches require many DRAM commands because the comparison's algorithmic complexity grows with operand bit-width in the bit-serial execution model. This command overhead becomes the dominant bottleneck, limiting application-level speedup.
  We propose Clutch, a data representation and comparison algorithm that accelerates vector-scalar comparisons in PuD systems with high efficiency and scalability. Clutch first uses temporal coding, encoding each vector value as a sequence of leading ones, which enables lookup-based comparison against a scalar by accessing the corresponding DRAM row. To avoid the prohibitive memory footprint of lookup tables at high precision, Clutch partitions operands into multiple multi-bit chunks, compares chunks independently using compact lookup tables, and merges the per-chunk results with a PuD-efficient procedure. By adjusting the number of chunks, Clutch provides a flexible tradeoff between throughput and memory usage. Across predicate evaluation and decision tree inference, Clutch improves end-to-end application throughput and energy efficiency by an average of 12x and 69x over highly optimized CPU and GPU execution, and by 2.9x and 3.0x over the state-of-the-art bit-serial PuD implementation. We also present the first mapping of decision tree inference to PuD execution, extending PuD to a new application domain.

### [137] [MOCAP: Wafer-Scale-Chip-Oriented Memory-Orchestrated Chunked Pipelining Framework for Prefill-Only LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22968)

*Zichuan Wang,Huizheng Wang,Yuheng Xiao,Haonan Zuo,Taiquan Wei,Jinyi Deng,Chao Li,Yang Hu,Shouyi Yin*

Main category: `cs.AR`

**TL;DR:** MOCAP是一个面向晶圆级芯片(WSC)上长上下文LLM预填充阶段的内存编排分块流水线框架，通过均衡KV缓存内存分布和分块延迟来加速预填充推理。

#### Problem

长上下文LLM预填充阶段中，因果依赖导致各流水线阶段KV缓存积累不均，造成严重的内存失衡并限制了可处理的序列长度；同时，后续分块因依赖前面分块需要更多注意力计算，导致分块级别的延迟不均衡。

#### Key Idea

通过内存均衡的KV重分配来缓解流水线阶段间的内存不平衡，并通过延迟均衡的分块划分来平衡各分块的计算开销，从而在晶圆级芯片上实现高效的长上下文预填充流水线。

#### System/Method Design

MOCAP包含两个核心组件：(1) Memory-Balanced KV Reallocation (MBKR)，通过跨流水线阶段重新分配KV缓存来缓解内存不平衡，从而延展可行序列长度；(2) Latency-Balanced Chunk Partitioning (LBCP)，在注意力计算成本增长和KV重分配开销的双重约束下平衡各分块的执行成本，提升流水线效率。

#### Experiments

与GPipe相比，MOCAP平均降低了76.4%的端到端延迟并提升了3.24倍的吞吐量；与Terapipe相比，最大支持序列长度提升了1.31倍。

#### Why It Matters

该工作解决了晶圆级芯片上长上下文预填充推理的关键瓶颈——通信开销和内存/延迟不均衡问题，为利用WSC高通信带宽和大算力容量加速LLM预填充提供了实用方案，对推动超长上下文LLM推理具有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接针对LLM预填充阶段的长上下文推理加速问题，涉及KV缓存管理、流水线并行策略、内存均衡和延迟优化，属于LLM推理系统和分布式并行计算领域的前沿研究。

#### Abstract

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in prefill-only workloads, where end-to-end latency is dominated by the prefill phase. For long-context prefill, communication overhead grows with sequence length and quickly becomes a bottleneck on conventional GPU systems, making wafer-scale chips (WSCs) a promising substrate due to their high communication bandwidth and large aggregate compute and memory capacity. A natural way to accelerate prefill is to partition a long input sequence into multiple chunks and execute them in a finer-grained pipeline across devices. However, directly applying this idea to long-context prefill on WSCs remains challenging. First, causal dependency across chunks causes KV cache to accumulate unevenly across pipeline stages, creating severe memory imbalance and limiting the feasible sequence length. Second, later chunks require more attention computation because each chunk depends on preceding chunks, leading to chunk-level latency imbalance.
  To address these challenges, we present MOCAP, a memory-orchestrated chunked pipelining framework for prefill-only LLM inference on WSCs. MOCAP introduces Memory-Balanced KV Reallocation (MBKR) to alleviate memory imbalance by redistributing KV cache across pipeline stages, thereby extending the feasible sequence length. It further incorporates Latency-Balanced Chunk Partitioning (LBCP) to balance chunk execution cost under both attention-cost growth and KV reallocation overhead, improving pipeline efficiency. Experimental results show that, compared with GPipe, MOCAP achieves 76.4\% lower end-to-end latency and 3.24$\times$ higher throughput on average. MOCAP also extends the maximum supported sequence length by up to 1.31$\times$ compared with Terapipe.

### [138] [Towards CSI-Native Foundation Models: A Channel-Adaptive Roadmap for 6G](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20670)

*Chenyu Zhang,Xinchen Lyu,Chenshan Ren,Shuhan Liu,Qimei Cui*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出面向CSI原生基础模型的通道自适应统一框架，通过将预训练、位置建模和注意力控制与无线信道的物理几何特性对齐，实现高泛化、可扩展且高效的6G信道状态信息表征学习。

#### Problem

现有无线基础模型将CSI视为通用任务张量而非传播条件约束的信道响应，未能捕获无线环境内在的时-频-空几何结构，导致预训练方法在物理感知和泛化能力上存在局限。

#### Key Idea

将预训练、位置建模和注意力控制与三个信道物理需求对齐：(1) 尺度感知的异构曝光（适应不同天线规模）；(2) 物理时-频-天线坐标的位置编码；(3) 受相关性约束的token交互机制——使模型学习CSI原生的传播条件表征而非通用张量。

#### System/Method Design

提出一个统一的CSI原生基础模型框架，包含三个核心设计原则：(a) 尺度感知的异构预训练曝光，支持不同天线规模的泛化；(b) 基于物理时-频-天线坐标的位置建模；(c) 受信道相关性约束的注意力控制机制，限制token间交互范围，使其符合无线信道物理特性。

#### Experiments

在三个维度进行实验：(1) 零样本泛化：NMSE在时空频任务上降低超过4 dB；(2) 尺度外推：在8倍未见过的天线规模下获得高达5.4 dB增益；(3) 推理效率：移动感知处理加速最高18.8%。系统级评估（Sionna SYS）显示：仅需7.01%的密集导频开销，平均NMSE达-18.64 dB，净频谱效率比密集LMMSE提升36.6%、比WiFo提升15.5%。

#### Why It Matters

首次从物理信道几何特性出发系统性地设计CSI原生基础模型，证明了将物理先验融入预训练框架可以显著降低导频开销、提升频谱效率，为6G中可复用的无线信道智能奠定了新范式。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然不是直接针对LLM或MoE，但其核心思想——将物理先验（坐标位置、尺度感知、相关性约束）融入注意力机制和预训练框架——对LLM系统研究中如何引入结构化先验以提升效率有借鉴意义。其提出的尺度外推能力和效率加速方案（最高18.8%）对MoE推理加速、KV cache优化等系统研究方向具有方法论上的启发价值。

#### Abstract

Wireless foundation models offer a path toward reusable channel state information (CSI) intelligence for sixth-generation (6G) systems. However, existing generic-backbone adaptation and CSI pretraining methods often treat CSI as task tensors rather than propagation-conditioned channel responses, thereby failing to capture the intrinsic time-frequency-spatial geometry of wireless environments. This paper presents a channel-adaptive roadmap toward CSI-native foundation models, proposing a unified framework that aligns pretraining, positional modeling, and attention control with three channel requirements: scale-aware heterogeneous exposure, physical time-frequency-antenna coordinates, and correlation-bounded token interaction. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superiority of the proposed framework across three dimensions: zero-shot generalization, reducing NMSE by more than 4 dB across spatial-temporal-frequency tasks; scale extrapolation, yielding up to a 5.4 dB gain under 8 times unseen antenna scaling; and inference efficiency, accelerating mobility-aware processing by up to 18.8%. A system-level evaluation with Sionna SYS further shows that the proposed framework uses only 7.01% of dense-pilot overhead, reaches -18.64 dB average NMSE, and improves average net spectral efficiency by 36.6% over dense LMMSE and 15.5% over WiFo, indicating that CSI-native representation learning can support pilot-efficient radio access.

### [139] [NeuroShield: A Device-Agnostic Foundation Model for EEG Authentication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20673)

*Matin Fallahi,Patricia Arias-Cabarcos,Thorsten Strufe*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** NeuroShield 是一个面向 EEG 身份认证的可复用基础模型，通过双阶段 Transformer 架构从可变通道和可变长度的 EEG 信号中学习身份判别性嵌入，支持跨异构采集设置的知识迁移。

#### Problem

EEG 身份认证模型通常与训练时的采集设置（如头戴设备、通道布局、信号时长）紧密绑定，现有模型无法处理异构 EEG 数据，导致每个新数据集或新硬件都需要重新开发模型，限制了多数据集学习、知识迁移和模型复用。

#### Key Idea

利用双阶段 Transformer 架构学习与通道布局和信号时长无关的身份判别性嵌入，使得模型能够处理可变通道（不同头戴设备）和可变长度（不同采集时长）的 EEG 信号，从而实现跨异构采集设置的泛化。

#### System/Method Design

NeuroShield 是一个双阶段 Transformer 架构的预训练基础模型。第一阶段处理可变通道数的 EEG 输入，将不同通道布局的原始信号映射到统一嵌入空间；第二阶段处理可变长度的时序信号，捕获长时间依赖关系以增强身份判别性。模型在大规模多数据集上预训练后，可通过微调适配到未见过的下游数据集。

#### Experiments

使用三个公开 EEG 数据集进行预训练，涵盖 15,762 名受试者和 28,116 个会话。在两个未见过的下游数据集上评估迁移性能。微调后，NeuroShield 在等错误率（EER）上相比现有最优方法降低了 0.44–8.06 个百分点，并能泛化到训练时未见过的更长信号段和不同通道布局。

#### Why It Matters

这项工作解决了 EEG 身份认证领域中长期存在的"异构性"难题，首次提出了一个可跨硬件、跨通道布局、跨信号时长的可复用基础模型，大幅降低了新场景下的模型开发成本，并为 EEG 领域基础模型的标准化和社区共享提供了范例。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然 NeuroShield 聚焦于 EEG 认证而非 LLM 系统，但其双阶段 Transformer 架构、多数据集预训练+微调范式和跨异构设备泛化的思路对 LLM/MoE 系统研究有参考价值：1) 处理变长输入和异构通道的架构设计可类比于 MoE 中处理不同专家负载或模态对齐问题；2) 多数据集联合预训练策略对构建通用 LLM 基础模型有借鉴意义；3) 模型在不同硬件配置下的可迁移性对 LLM 推理系统的跨平台部署有启发。

#### Abstract

A central challenge in EEG authentication is that models are typically tied to the acquisition settings in which they are trained. In particular, variations in headset hardware, channel layout, and signal duration create heterogeneous recordings that existing models are not designed to handle, causing each new headset or dataset to be treated as a separate model-development problem. This fragmentation limits multi-dataset learning, hinders knowledge transfer, and reduces model reusability. To address this limitation, we present NeuroShield, a reusable foundation model for EEG authentication that learns identity-discriminative embeddings from variable-channel and variable-length EEG recordings through a dual-stage transformer architecture. We pretrain NeuroShield on three public EEG datasets comprising 15{,}762 subjects and 28{,}116 sessions, and evaluate transfer on two unseen downstream datasets. Our evaluations show that, after fine-tuning, NeuroShield reduces equal error rate by 0.44--8.06 percentage points relative to the state of the art. NeuroShield further generalizes to segments longer than those seen during training and operates across channel layouts not encountered during pretraining. These results establish NeuroShield as a reusable and adaptable EEG identity encoder across heterogeneous recording settings. We release NeuroShield as open source to support reproducibility and community adoption.

### [140] [Massive Activations Are Architecturally Robust: A Controlled Scratch/Commitment Residual Stream Test](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20743)

*Maruthi Vemula*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出 Ledger Residuals 架构，通过分离残差流为可写 Scratch 流和只读 Accumulator 流来检验大规模激活是否仅为残差流过载的伪影，发现模型在保护通道中仍会重建起始 token 上的 massive activations，证明其具有功能性而非偶然。

#### Problem

Transformer 模型中存在 massive activations（少数隐藏维度数值远高于中位数，且集中在序列起始 token 上）。学界对其成因存在争议：是残差流同时承担读写角色导致的"可移除伪影"，还是模型功能所需的必要组件。

#### Key Idea

直接通过架构干预检验"伪影假说"：如果将残差流拆分为可自由覆写的暂存流（Deliberation）和受保护的只读累加流（Commitment），若 massive activations 仅因读写冲突产生，则专用读出通道应消除其必要性。

#### System/Method Design

提出 Ledger Residuals 架构，将残差流拆分为两个通道：Deliberation（可变的暂存流，中间计算可任意覆写）和 Commitment（受保护的、仅用于解码的累加流，保存模型最终读出的表征）。模型从 Commitment 流中读取输出，Deliberation 仅用于中间计算。

#### Experiments

在 160M 和 290M 参数规模的匹配损失语言模型上进行实验。比较标准 Transformer 与 Ledger Residuals 中 massive activations 的表现。发现：保护通道中仍会出现固定维度、起始 token 上的 outlier，虽幅度小于标准 Transformer，但更集中；更强的稀疏性惩罚使其更持久、更集中，而非被消除。

#### Why It Matters

该工作通过直接架构干预提供了强有力证据，表明 massive activations 是 Transformer 的功能性组件而非偶然伪影，这对理解 Transformer 内部工作机制、设计更高效的架构（如量化、剪枝）具有指导意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。Massive activations 对 LLM 推理系统的量化（outlier 导致低比特量化困难）、KV cache 优化、MoE 路由等均有重要影响。本文证明其具有功能必要性，意味着系统优化不能简单移除它们，而需要专门设计以容忍或利用这些 outlier 特征。

#### Abstract

Trained transformers reliably develop massive activations, a small number of hidden dimensions whose magnitude is far above the median and which concentrate on the sequence-start token. Whether these outliers are a removable artifact of the residual stream's overloaded read and write role, or instead a functional necessity, is actively debated. We test the artifact hypothesis directly, with an architectural intervention. Our architecture, Ledger Residuals, splits the residual stream into a mutable scratch stream (Deliberation) that intermediate computation may freely overwrite and a protected, decode-only accumulator (Commitment) that holds the representation the model reads out. If massive activations exist only because one stream is forced to be both scratchpad and answer, then a dedicated answer channel should remove the need for them. We find that it does not. In matched-loss language models at the 160M and 290M scales, the model rebuilds the canonical fixed-dimension, start-token outlier inside the protected channel. The rebuilt feature is smaller in magnitude than in a standard transformer but more sharply concentrated on the start token, and a stronger sparsity penalty makes it more persistent and more concentrated still, rather than removing it. Massive activations therefore look architecturally robust: they re-emerge in whichever representation the model decodes from, which is what we would expect if they are functional rather than incidental. We release our architecture and measurement code.

### [141] [Load Testing for Machine Learning Model Serving Systems at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22013)

*Amr S. Abdelfattah,Nakul Tirumalai,Indu Mohanan,Xiao Li,Pengchao Wang,Dinakar Dhurjati,Eric Sung*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出了一种名为\sys的工业级ML模型服务系统负载测试框架，通过自适应、反馈驱动的搜索策略系统性地估算服务容量，从而在满足SLO约束下找到最大可持续吞吐量。

#### Problem

ML模型服务已成为GPU基础设施的主要消耗者，但其容量规划仍然高度依赖经验手段：资源不足会导致SLO违规和生产事故，而过度配置则造成大量资源浪费。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是利用实时性能信号，结合阻尼机制、尖峰容忍度和收敛检测，通过自适应、反馈驱动的搜索策略高效地识别在SLO约束下的最大可持续吞吐量。

#### System/Method Design

\sys是一个工业级负载测试框架，采用自适应、反馈驱动的搜索策略。它利用实时性能信号，集成了阻尼（dampening）、尖峰容忍度（spike tolerance）和收敛检测（convergence detection）等机制，在满足SLO约束的条件下系统性地寻找最大可持续吞吐量。

#### Experiments

通过14个工业案例研究进行纵向分析，覆盖推荐、排序、视觉和NLP四大ML架构类别。关键结果：使用录制流量进行工作负载校准可将估计误差从约30%降低到2-6%；正确的预热（warmup）处理使准确性提升22.2%。部署前大量模型发布存在资源不足导致的事故，部署后显著减少。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为ML服务系统的容量规划提供了系统化的工业级解决方案，将负载测试从经验做法转变为有可靠方法的工程实践，显著提升了GPU资源效率和运营可靠性。总结的六条经验和架构指导原则对构建可靠高效的ML服务系统具有实际指导意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。该工作直接针对ML推理服务系统的容量规划和负载测试问题，与LLM推理服务、MoE部署等场景紧密相关。其讨论的模型大小和共置效应（co-location effects）对预测误差的影响，以及工作负载校准、预热处理等技术细节，对LLM/MoE服务系统的资源调度、性能优化和可靠性保障具有重要参考价值。

#### Abstract

Machine learning (ML) model serving has become a dominant consumer of GPU infrastructure, yet capacity planning in these systems remains largely ad hoc. Under-provisioning leads to service-level objective (SLO) violations and production incidents, while over-provisioning results in substantial resource waste. This paper presents \sys, an industrial load testing framework for ML serving systems that systematically estimates serving capacity through an adaptive, feedback-driven search strategy. The approach leverages real-time performance signals, incorporating dampening, spike tolerance, and convergence detection to efficiently identify maximum sustainable throughput under SLO constraints. We evaluate \sys through a longitudinal analysis of 14 industrial case studies spanning four ML architecture classes: recommendation, ranking, vision, and NLP. This study demonstrates that systematic load testing leads to substantial improvements in GPU resource efficiency and operational reliability. Prior to adopting \sys, a significant fraction of model launches were under-provisioned, resulting in recurring incidents; these issues were substantially reduced after deployment. Our results show that ML-specific design decisions are critical to accurate capacity estimation: workload calibration using recorded traffic reduces estimation error from approximately 30\% to 2--6\%, while proper warmup handling yields a 22.2\% improvement in accuracy. Further analysis reveals key factors influencing prediction error, including model size and co-location effects. This paper distills six lessons and derive architectural guidelines for ML load testing, offering actionable insights for building reliable and efficient ML serving systems.

### [142] [CIExplainer++: Generating Causal and Interpretable Explanations for Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20747)

*Francisco Caldas,Sahil Satish Kumar,Ruben Belo,Cláudia Soares*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出CIExplainer（基于因果推断的扰动方法）和G2TeXplainer（子图到自然语言翻译器），分别用于识别图神经网络中具有因果影响的子图并将子图解释转化为可读的自然语言文本。

#### Problem

图神经网络（GNN）的可解释性面临两个瓶颈：（1）现有解释方法难以精确识别对模型输出真正具有因果影响力的子图结构；（2）即使获得了子图解释，这些子图仍难以被人类直观理解，缺乏从子图到可解释自然语言描述的桥梁。

#### Key Idea

将因果推断中的潜在结果框架引入GNN解释，通过扰动方法量化子图对GNN预测的因果效应；同时利用自然语言生成技术将因果子图转化为同时包含特征信息和关系信息的文本解释。

#### System/Method Design

提出两阶段方法：第一阶段CIExplainer，基于潜在结果框架（Potential Outcome Framework）的扰动方法，识别对GNN预测具有最高因果效应的子图；第二阶段G2TeXplainer，将因果子图转化为自然语言解释，捕捉特征级信息和关系级信息。

#### Experiments

在多种GNN架构（GCN、GraphSAGE、GAT、GIN）和多个数据集上进行评估，与基线方法进行比较。具体指标和数值结果在摘要中未明确给出。

#### Why It Matters

该工作同时解决了GNN可解释性中"因果归因"和"人类可理解"两个关键问题，首次将因果推断和自然语言生成有机结合到GNN解释流程中，朝着更可信、更可解释的图学习系统迈出了重要一步。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM系统的关联：G2TeXplainer将子图转化为自然语言解释，可与LLM结合用于生成更丰富的模型行为描述；在模型可解释性和可信AI方面为LLM系统提供方法论参考。与MoE/推理加速/系统方向无直接关联。

#### Abstract

Explainable Artificial Intelligence aims to make black-box models more trustworthy by presenting, in a human-understandable manner, the elements that lead to the model's output. This involves both (i) identifying components and connections with genuine causal influence on outputs and (ii) translating such structures into an interpretable representation. For the former, we introduce CIExplainer, a novel perturbation-based method grounded in causal inference for explaining Graph Neural Networks (GNNs). CIExplainer identifies the subgraph with the highest causal effects on GNN predictions using the Potential Outcome Framework. We evaluate and compare CIExplainer on various GNN architectures (GCN, GraphSAGE, GAT, GIN) and datasets.
  To bridge subgraph explanations with human interpretability, we further propose G2TeXplainer, a method that transforms causal subgraphs into natural language explanations that capture both feature-level and relational information.

### [143] [Evidential Fusion Network for Multimodal Survival Prediction under Missing Modalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20757)

*Yucheng Xing,Hailan Mo,Zi Wang,Ling Huang,Mengling Feng*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出EMMS模型，利用Dempster-Shafer理论和高斯随机模糊数进行多模态决策融合，在不需要生成缺失数据的情况下实现缺失模态下的生存预测，并提供校准的不确定性估计。

#### Problem

现有多模态生存预测模型假设数据完整，对真实临床场景中频繁出现的模态缺失情况缺乏鲁棒性。

#### Key Idea

将缺失模态视为空证据（vacuous evidence），避免干扰可用输入；利用Dempster-Shafer理论和高斯随机模糊数进行多模态决策融合，同时考虑偶然不确定性（aleatoric）、认知不确定性（epistemic）和模态可靠性。

#### System/Method Design

EMMS模型采用基于Dempster-Shafer证据理论和高斯随机模糊数（GRFN）的多模态决策融合方法，无需生成式阶段来补全缺失数据。模型将缺失模态视为空证据，使其不影响可用模态的输入，并自然反映不确定性增加。融合过程中同时考虑了偶然不确定性、认知不确定性以及各模态的可靠性。

#### Experiments

在四个癌症数据集上进行广泛实验，达到最先进性能（state-of-the-art），在不引入额外计算开销的情况下，提供了校准且可解释的不确定性估计。

#### Why It Matters

该工作解决了真实临床场景中模态缺失这一关键实际问题，提供了一种计算高效、无需生成缺失数据的解决方案，同时还能提供校准的不确定性估计，增强了临床决策的可信度和可解释性。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

论文提及的Dempster-Shafer证据融合和不确定性量化方法与多模态LLM系统中处理缺失模态的问题相关。虽然不直接涉及MoE或推理加速，但其"将缺失模态视为空证据"的思路和计算高效的多模态融合机制可启发LLM系统在不完整输入下的鲁棒设计和不确定性校准。

#### Abstract

Recent multimodal survival prediction models have demonstrated strong predictive performance by leveraging complementary information across modalities. However, such models generally assume data completeness and exhibit limited robustness toward missing modalities, which are frequently encountered in real-world clinical settings. We propose the Evidential Missing Modality Survival Fusion (EMMS) model for multimodal survival prediction under missing modalities. EMMS offers a straightforward, computationally effective approach to survival analysis without requiring a generative phase for missing data. By employing Dempster-Shafer theory and Gaussian Random Fuzzy Numbers for multimodal decision fusion, it considers both aleatoric and epistemic uncertainty alongside modality reliability for fusion. Moreover, the model treats missing modalities as vacuous evidence, preventing interference with available inputs and naturally reflecting increased uncertainty and calibrated predictions. Extensive experiments on four cancer datasets demonstrate state-of-the-art performance while providing calibrated and interpretable uncertainty estimates under incomplete multimodal observations, without introducing additional computational overhead.

### [144] [ELADO: Elliptic PDE Assessment Datasets for Operator Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20771)

*Frank Ehebrecht,Toni Scharle,Martin Atzmueller*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** ELADO是一个系统化的基准测试套件，通过构造具有可控难度的椭圆PDE数据集，揭示神经算子架构在求解椭圆PDE时存在的多种失效模式。

#### Problem

现有神经算子基准数据集主要关注平均性能，未能系统性地暴露神经算子架构在处理椭圆PDE问题时自然出现的各类困难（如重尾分布、频谱偏移、输入敏感性等），导致标准指标可能掩盖模型的实质性性能退化。

#### Key Idea

通过可控的数据生成过程，针对性地构造多个围绕Poisson方程和Helmholtz方程的数据集，每个数据集隔离一种特定的困难来源，从而系统性地量化神经算子在不同失效模式下的表现。

#### System/Method Design

ELADO包含基于Poisson方程和Helmholtz方程（均具有非常数系数）的多个数据集。数据生成过程可控，设计用于隔离五种困难来源：(1) 轻尾系数场导致的重尾解分布；(2) 输入数据的频谱分布偏移；(3) 轻尾系数场导致的解频域重尾分布；(4) 基于经验局部Lipschitz分析量化算子的输入敏感性；(5) 受控幅度归一化下输入信号复杂度对预测精度的影响。

#### Experiments

在ELADO所有数据集上评估了多种神经算子架构。结果显示，重尾目标、频谱偏移和输入敏感性会显著降低预测精度，而这些性能退化在标准数据集和指标（如平均相对L²误差）下可能被掩盖。

#### Why It Matters

该工作揭露了现有神经算子评估体系的盲区，为神经算子领域提供了更严格、更有诊断性的基准测试工具，有助于推动更鲁棒的神经算子架构设计。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

本文主要聚焦神经算子（Neural Operator）在科学计算（PDE求解）中的失效模式分析，与LLM/MoE/推理加速/分布式系统等领域的直接关联性较低。但其方法论——即构造可控难度的基准来暴露模型在非理想条件下的失效模式——对LLM系统的鲁棒性评估和基准设计具有方法论上的参考价值。

#### Abstract

We introduce ELADO (Elliptic PDE Assessment Datasets for Operator Learning), a systematic benchmark suite constructed to show and quantify failure modes of neural operator architectures when learning solution operators of elliptic PDEs. While the benchmarks of existing datasets focus on average case performance, the ELADO datasets are constructed to highlight challenges that arise naturally in elliptic PDE problems. In particular, we construct several datasets built around Poisson's equation and the Helmholtz equation, each with non-constant coefficients. We define a controllable data-generating process to create datasets, that are designed to isolate a distinct source of difficulty. Specifically, these are (1) heavy-tailed solution distributions arising from light-tailed coefficient field distributions, (2) spectral distribution shift of the input data, (3) heavy-tailed distributions in the frequency domain of solutions, arising from light-tailed coefficient field distributions, (4) input sensitivity of learned operators, quantified by an empirical local Lipschitz analysis, and (5) the effect of input signal complexity on prediction accuracy under controlled amplitude normalization. We evaluate several neural operator architectures across all datasets and show that heavy-tailed targets, spectral shift, and input sensitivity each cause substantial degradation of the prediction accuracy that standard datasets and metrics (e.g., the mean relative $L^2$ error) may obscure.

### [145] [B[FM]$^2$: Brain Foundation Model via Flow Matching with SplitUNet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20812)

*Jaedong Hwang,Kathleen Zhang,Wei Dai,Konstantinos Kontras,Maarten Vanmarcke,Maarten De Vos,Ila Fiete,Paul Pu Liang*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出 B[FM]²，一种基于流匹配（Flow Matching）直接在原始 EEG 信号上预训练的基础模型，无需分片、标记化或掩码，在 7/9 个下游任务上达到 SOTA，且预训练数据量仅为现有模型的 ~1/30。

#### Problem

现有 EEG 基础模型将连续多通道波形离散化为分片或码本 token，破坏了连续的脑节律，掩盖了细粒度的时间动态信息；同时多通道 EEG 信号存在时间和电极维度不对称的问题（时间轴密集采样且高度自相关，电极轴短且空间位置不同），给流匹配等连续生成方法带来架构挑战。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察有两点：(1) 放弃离散化预处理，直接在原始 EEG 信号上使用连续时间流匹配（Flow Matching）进行自监督预训练，保持脑信号的时间连续性；(2) 提出 SplitUNet 作为速度网络（velocity network），通过将每个网络块分解为独立的 1D 时间卷积和 1D 电极卷积，仅沿时间轴下采样，保留电极拓扑结构，解决时间-电极不对称问题。

#### System/Method Design

B[FM]² 采用流匹配（Flow Matching）框架在原始 EEG 信号上预训练。其核心架构 SplitUNet 是一个速度网络，设计上每个块分离为两个独立的一维卷积：一个沿时间维度，一个沿电极维度；仅在时间轴进行下采样，电极维度在整个网络层次中保持拓扑结构不变。整个训练过程不使用分片（patches）、标记化（tokenization）或掩码（masking）等离散化手段。

#### Experiments

在 9 个标准下游 EEG 分类任务上评估，B[FM]² 在 7 个任务上达到 SOTA。预训练预算仅 36,895 个片段（约 307 小时），比现有 EEG 基础模型所需数据量少 1-2 个数量级（约 30 倍）。此外，生成的合成 EEG 数据经过两名委员会认证的神经科医生进行图灵测试，无法与真实脑电数据区分（Cohen's κ = -0.096，表明识别结果与随机猜测无异）。

#### Why It Matters

这项工作证明了在 EEG 基础模型中保持信号连续性的重要性，以极少的预训练数据（~307h）达到 SOTA，极大降低了 EEG 基础模型的预训练门槛。同时具备高质量的合成 EEG 生成能力，有助于数据增强和隐私保护，对临床和脑机接口领域具有广泛价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽不直接涉及 LLM 或 MoE，但对推理/系统研究有参考价值：SplitUNet 的分解式 1D 卷积设计（时间+电极分离）可启发处理多维度不对称数据的架构设计；流匹配作为生成范式与扩散模型相关，可迁移至 LLM 的连续生成或表示学习；在 EEG 领域用极少量预训练数据高效训练基础模型的思路，对降低大模型训练成本有借鉴意义。

#### Abstract

EEG foundation models can learn generalizable representations from large-scale EEG corpora to enable single-backbone transfer across diverse clinical and brain-computer interface tasks. Existing models typically discretize the continuous multi-channel EEG waveform into patches or codebook tokens and train a transformer with masked self-supervision. Recognizing that this discretization fragments continuous brain rhythms and obscures fine-grained temporal dynamics, we present B[FM]$^2$(Brain Foundation Model via Flow Matching), whose inductive bias aligns with the data by pretraining directly on the raw signal using continuous-time flow matching without patches, tokenization, or masking. However, multi-channel EEG signals pose an architectural challenge for flow matching: time is densely sampled and highly autocorrelated (thousands of timepoints), while the electrode axis is short (tens of channels) at distinct scalp positions. To address this time-electrode asymmetry, we introduce SplitUNet, a velocity network that factorizes each block into separate 1D temporal and 1D electrode convolutions and downsamples only along time, preserving electrode topology throughout the hierarchy. B[FM]$^2$ sets a new state of the art on 7 of 9 standard downstream EEG classification tasks, using a pretraining budget of only 36,895 segments ($\approx$ 307h), 1-2 orders of magnitude ($\approx$ 30x) less than required by existing EEG foundation models. Further, it generates synthetic EEGs that two board-certified neurologists cannot distinguish from brain data (Cohen's $κ=$ -0.096). https://jd730.github.io/projects/BFM2

### [146] [CELEUS: Certifiable and Efficient LLM Evaluation via E-Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20820)

*Zhijian Zhou,Zesheng Ye,Zhaorun Chen,Bo Li,Feng Liu*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出Celeus框架，利用E-processes构建任意时刻有效的置信区间，实现可认证的高效LLM评估，在保证统计覆盖的同时减少54-62%的评估样本量。

#### Problem

现有LLM评估方法通过顺序采样并不断更新置信区间（CI）来覆盖真实性能，但由于CI被重复更新并用于决定何时停止，导致声称的覆盖率（如95%）在实际中失效，缺乏任意时刻有效性（anytime-validity），存在理论严谨性与实践之间的差距。

#### Key Idea

利用E-processes构建任意时刻有效的置信区间，结合不确定性引导采样（选择信息量大的样本）和替代模型近似（对未评估样本进行估计），并证明二者组合的信号在给定过去条件下对评估分数无偏，从而在统计上保证任意时刻有效的同时降低估计方差。

#### System/Method Design

Celeus框架包含三个核心组件：(1) 不确定性引导采样，主动选择信息量大的样本进行评估；(2) 替代辅助近似，对未评估样本进行估计以减少方差；(3) 基于E-processes构建任意时刻有效的置信区间。理论上证明了信号的无偏性、CI以近参数速率收缩（最多差对数因子），并分析了最优方差采样规则的oracle形式。

#### Experiments

实验设置（从摘要推断）：将Celeus与现有顺序评估基线方法对比，以目标精度为指标。核心结果：Celeus在保持任意时刻有效覆盖率的前提下，达到目标精度所需的评估样本量比基线方法减少54-62%。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次弥合了LLM评估中理论严谨性与实践之间的差距，提供了可认证的评估保证，使得评估分数不仅高效（样本效率提升50%以上），而且具有严格的统计可靠性，对LLM的可信部署具有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关于LLM评估系统：解决了LLM评估的统计可靠性和样本效率问题。虽然不直接涉及MoE或推理加速，但高效评估方法对LLM系统开发中的验证、基准测试和模型选择至关重要。减少评估样本量意味着降低评估成本，有助于大规模LLM系统的快速迭代和部署。

#### Abstract

Can we trust evaluation scores to capture an LLM's true real-world performance? Certifiable evaluation answers this question by providing guarantee for LLM evaluation. In particular, existing methods sequentially curate evaluation samples and keep updating confidence intervals (CIs) that cover the true performance with high probability (e.g., 95%) until some conditions are satisfied, e.g., the CI width reaches a target precision. However, existing methods are not generally anytime-valid: the claimed coverage (e.g., 95%) may fail when CIs are repeatedly updated and used to decide when to stop, leaving a gap between theoretical rigor and practice. This paper bridges this gap by proposing Celeus, a Certifiable framework for Efficient LLM evaluation, which leverages E-processes to build anytime-valid CIs. Concretely, we propose signals that combine two ingredients: (i) Uncertainty-guided sampling to select informative samples for evaluation, and (ii) Surrogate-assisted approximations for unevaluated samples. We prove that such signals remain unbiased for the evaluation score conditional on the past, enabling statistically-grounded and anytime-valid $e$-process CIs. More importantly, the two ingredients reduce estimation variance and help reach the target precision with fewer evaluated samples. We also prove that CIs obtained by Celeus can shrink at a near-parametric rate up to logarithmic factors and analyze the oracle variance-optimal sampling rule that motivates the empirical uncertainty-guided one. Experiments show that Celeus reaches the target precision using 54-62% fewer evaluated samples than baselines, while preserving anytime-valid coverage.

### [147] [Evolutionary Discovery of Developmental Reward Schedules in Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20858)

*Alan Nadelsticher Ruvalcaba*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出一个进化框架来自动发现强化学习中的发展性奖励调度，通过进化算法动态优化三种生物启发式动机分量（自主性、新颖性、反应性）的时变权重组合。

#### Problem

强化学习中奖励组合的时间结构通常由人工设计并在训练过程中固定不变，奖励动机优先级的动态演化规律尚未被充分探索。

#### Key Idea

将奖励调度视为一个可进化的对象，利用进化算法自动发现最优的时变权重序列，使三种生物启发的动机分量（agency、novelty、reactivity）在训练过程中动态调整。

#### System/Method Design

提出一个进化框架，将三种动机分量（自主性agency、新颖性novelty、反应性reactivity）通过时变权重组合，使用四种进化算法（CMA-ES、xNES、DE、L-SHADE）自动搜索最优的权重调度策略，并在稀疏奖励的MiniGrid任务上评估。

#### Experiments

在DoorKey-6x6和KeyCorridorS3R1两个稀疏奖励MiniGrid任务上评估，对比四种进化算法 vs. 纯外在动机基线（主要对比点）及三种手工设计方法。DoorKey-6x6上所有进化方法优于基线，L-SHADE最优（相对提升11.4%）；KeyCorridorS3R1上仅CMA-ES最优，其余进化方法泛化能力弱于基线。发现新颖性（novelty）在两个任务中均作为早期主导信号出现，与预设的发展顺序不同。

#### Why It Matters

首次将进化优化系统性地应用于发展性奖励调度的自动发现，揭示了进化找到的计算最优解与生物学最优解可能不同，为自动化设计RL训练过程中的动机演化提供了新路径。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/MoE系统研究无直接关联。本文聚焦于强化学习中的奖励调度进化优化，属于RL训练策略自动化领域，不涉及LLM推理加速、MoE架构、KV缓存或分布式系统等系统研究方向。

#### Abstract

The temporal structure of reward composition in reinforcement learning (RL) is typically hand-designed and held fixed throughout training, leaving the progression of motivational priorities largely unexplored. In this work, we propose an evolutionary framework for discovering developmental reward schedules, in which three distinct biologically inspired motivational components -- agency, novelty, and reactivity -- are combined through time-varying weights that dynamically shift over the course of training. Evaluated on two sparse-reward MiniGrid tasks: DoorKey-6x6 and KeyCorridorS3R1, our framework compares the generalizability of four evolutionary algorithms: CMA-ES, xNES, DE, and L-SHADE against an extrinsically motivated baseline (our main comparison point), and three additional hand-designed methods. On DoorKey-6x6, all evolved methods outperform the non-evolved baselines, with L-SHADE achieving the best performance -- an approximate relative mean improvement of 11.4% over the extrinsic only baseline. On KeyCorridorS3R1, CMA-ES achieves the best overall performance, with the remaining evolved methods showing weaker and less reliable generalization capability compared to the extrinsic only baseline. Interestingly, the discovered schedules diverge from our defined developmental ordering, with novelty consistently emerging as the dominant early signal during training, across both tasks. Collectively, our results position evolutionary optimization as a promising approach for developmental reward schedule discovery in deep reinforcement learning, and suggest that what evolution finds to be optimal in computational settings may differ from what it finds to be optimal in biology. The code for this project can be found at: https://github.com/alannadels/Evolutionary_RL.git.

### [148] [Machine Learning Classification of Cryopathy Syndromes: A Comprehensive Comparative Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20874)

*Nataliya Shakhovska,Valentyna Chopyak,Ivan Izonin,Vira Haievska*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出并比较了多种机器学习方法，用于从实验室数据中自动分类冷球蛋白血症综合征，其中软投票集成（随机森林+梯度提升树）取得了最佳多分类性能。

#### Problem

冷球蛋白血症综合征的分类困难，因为实验室模式在不同诊断类别之间常重叠，部分诊断罕见，导致常规解读挑战大且依赖专家判断。

#### Key Idea

利用临床知识指导的特征工程（特别是冷球蛋白衍生交互特征）结合集成学习方法，在高度不平衡和类别重叠的临床数据上实现可靠的自动化分类。

#### System/Method Design

分析了2686名患者的实验室记录，涵盖14个诊断类别。数据预处理包括清洗、编码、插补、归一化和构造临床信息交互特征。评估了12种建模策略：随机森林、梯度提升树、多层感知器、软投票集成、SMOTE类平衡、层次分类、周期感知模型、目标二分类器和概率校准。性能评估采用分层训练-测试评估和分层5折交叉验证。

#### Experiments

主要评估指标为宏平均F1分数、准确率、Top-3准确率和期望校准误差。软投票集成（随机森林+梯度提升树）取得最佳多分类性能。交叉验证确认了平衡随机森林的稳定表现。树模型始终优于神经网络。特征工程提升了判别能力，最有效的预测因子为冷球蛋白衍生交互特征。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为临床决策支持提供了一种实用策略，能够减少对专家判断的依赖，并系统性地比较了多种机器学习方法在罕见病分类中的适用性。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

不直接相关。本文聚焦于经典机器学习（树模型、集成方法）在临床分类任务中的应用，不涉及LLM、MoE、推理加速、KV缓存、分布式系统或计算机体系结构等方向。

#### Abstract

Cryopathy syndromes are difficult to classify because laboratory patterns often overlap across diagnostic categories, while some diagnoses are rare. This makes routine interpretation of cryoglobulin-related tests challenging and increases dependence on expert judgment. The aim of this study was to develop and compare machine learning approaches for automated classification of cryopathy syndromes from laboratory data and to identify a practical strategy for clinical decision support. Methods: We analysed laboratory records from 2,686 patients assigned to 14 diagnostic categories. The dataset included demographic variables, cryoglobulin measurements, precipitation tests, and hemagglutinin and hemolysin titers. Data preprocessing included cleaning, encoding, imputation, normalization, and construction of clinically informed interaction features. We evaluated 12 modelling strategies, including Random Forest, Gradient Boosted Trees, Multi-Layer Perceptron, soft-voting ensembles, class balancing with Synthetic Minority Over-sampling Technique, hierarchical classification, period-aware models, targeted binary classifiers, and probability calibration. Performance was assessed using stratified train-test evaluation and stratified 5-fold cross-validation. The main metrics were macro-averaged F1 score, accuracy, Top-3 accuracy, and expected calibration error. The overall task proved difficult because of marked class imbalance and clinical overlap between diagnoses. The best multiclass performance was achieved by a soft-voting ensemble of Random Forest and Gradient Boosted Trees. Cross-validation confirmed stable performance for the balanced Random Forest model. Tree-based methods consistently outperformed the neural network model. Feature engineering improved discrimination, and the most informative predictors were derived cryoglobulin-based interaction features.

### [149] [Understanding Latent Flow Models for Tabular Data Synthesis: Targets, Paths, and Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20878)

*Bahrul Ilmi Nasution*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文系统性地研究了表格数据潜空间流模型在不同学习目标、概率路径和采样动力学下的效用-风险权衡，并给出了可操作的配置建议。

#### Problem

在受监管领域中部署连续时间生成模型生成合成表格数据时，如何在分析效用、披露风险和计算成本之间取得平衡是一个关键挑战，而不同学习目标、概率路径和采样动力学在有限步积分和显式计算预算下的行为差异尚缺乏系统理解。

#### Key Idea

学习目标从根本上决定了效用-风险运行区间（速度/后验匹配倾向高效用，分数/噪声匹配倾向低披露风险），而配置和采样选择（如中点法、OT路径）可以进一步在固定预算或风险阈值下优化性能。

#### System/Method Design

论文对表格数据潜空间流模型进行了大规模实证研究，涵盖七种数据集，评估了四种学习目标（速度、分数、噪声、后验匹配）、两种概率路径（最优传输OT和方差保持VP）、ODE和SDE两种采样动力学，以及不同的积分预算设置。

#### Experiments

在七个数据集上进行了实验，评估指标涵盖分析效用和披露风险。主要发现：(1) 速度匹配和后验匹配倾向于产生更高的效用，而分数匹配和噪声匹配倾向于实现更低的披露风险；(2) 中点法常能提升分布保真度，OT路径比VP路径能更早停止采样，从而在固定预算或风险阈值下节省计算开销。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为实际部署合成表格数据生成模型提供了基于实证的配置指南和默认建议，帮助从业者在披露风险和资源约束下进行预发布模型选择，对受监管领域的数据共享有重要实践价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然本文专注于表格数据生成，但其研究的连续时间生成模型（流模型、ODE/SDE采样）、计算预算与效用/风险的权衡分析，以及OT路径相较于VP路径可提前停止采样以节省计算开销的发现，对LLM系统中的推理加速、计算资源调度和高效采样策略设计具有借鉴意义。

#### Abstract

Synthetic tabular data enables microdata sharing in regulated domains, yet deploying continuous-time generative models requires balancing analytical utility, disclosure risk, and computational cost. Latent-space flow models are flexible, but theoretical equivalences across learning targets, probability paths, and sampling dynamics can translate into different behaviour under finite-step integration and explicit compute budgets. We present an empirical study of tabular latent flow models across seven datasets, evaluating velocity, score, noise, and posterior matching objectives under optimal transport (OT) and variance-preserving (VP) paths, ODE and SDE sampling, and varying integration budgets. Our contributions are threefold: (1) we show that the learning target largely determines the utility-risk operating regime, with velocity and posterior matching tending to yield higher utility, while score and noise matching tend to achieve lower disclosure risk; (2) we demonstrate that configuration and sampling choices shift performance, with midpoint often improving distributional fidelity and OT paths often tolerating earlier stopping than VP, enabling compute savings under fixed budgets or risk thresholds; and (3) we distil these findings into actionable defaults and practical configuration guidance to support pre-release model selection under disclosure risk and resource constraints. The code implementation and supplementary materials can be accessed in https://github.com/rulnasution/tabular-latent-flow/.

### [150] [Temporal Causal Prior-Data Fitted Networks for Panel Data with Learned Reliability Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20889)

*Shravan Talupula,Saurabh Sharma*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** TCPFN是一个面向工业时间序列的零样本因果推断基础模型，能够同时输出条件平均处理效应(CATE)估计值和每对变量的可靠性信号，在19个基准数据集上取得了领先的因果发现性能，并在工业规模(变量数V=1275)上展现了相比传统方法数个数量级的加速。

#### Problem

现有因果基础模型(CausalPFN, CausalFM)仅支持静态横截面数据；神经时序方法(CRN, G-Net)需要针对每个数据集重新训练；已有的时序PFN方案未被验证可在工业规模上运行。此外，所有现有方法都不能在输出CATE估计的同时提供明确的每对变量可靠性信号。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是将Prior-Data Fitted Networks(PFN)扩展到时间序列因果推断场景，通过设计统一的混合先验训练策略覆盖多种因果机制(独立、直接、混杂、中介、时变混杂、反馈等)，并引入因果判断头(Causal Judgment Head)联合预测多个可靠性信号，实现零样本推理。

#### System/Method Design

TCPFN包含四个核心设计：(1) 因果判断头(Causal Judgment Head)，联合预测零效应概率、混淆强度、可识别性、中介比例和因果机制类型；(2) 混合训练先验，覆盖六种因果机制(独立、直接、混杂、中介、时变混杂、反馈)以及CausalFM风格的前门和工具变量先验；(3) 离散令牌面板数据结构，采用交叉注意力掩码防止跨时间步的信息泄露；(4) 基于FAISS的上下文选择和一步后验校正，支持工业规模的零样本推理。

#### Experiments

在跨五个领域的19个基准数据集上评估，零样本因果发现AUROC达到：Tennessee Eastman 0.96，SWaT 0.93，Causal Rivers 0.98，CAUSRCA 0.97。零效应检测器NullF1 0.94，AUROC 0.99。在专有纤维素纸浆数据集上，TCPFN在单GPU上6小时完成V=1275的推理；而CPU-only的PCMCI在V=666的子集上需81.5小时，外推至V=1275约需12.5天。TCPFN发现的top边能识别跨子系统的因果关系，而PCMCI仅发现仪器内部的控制-测量耦合。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次将基础模型范式成功应用于工业时间序列因果推断，同时解决了零样本推理、可靠性信号输出和工业规模可扩展性三大挑战，在因果发现领域展示了基础模型相较于传统方法的显著优势。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/系统研究的关联主要体现在：(1) 时序因果基础模型的零样本推理范式与LLM的前置训练-下游零样本迁移思路一致；(2) 跨注意力掩码设计防止信息泄露的技术对序列Transformer架构有参考意义；(3) FAISS结合一步后验校正的推理策略对大规模模型推理加速有借鉴价值；(4) 工业规模(V=1275)下相比传统方法(O(V²))的显著加速展示了基础模型在系统效率上的优势。

#### Abstract

Estimating causal effects in industrial time series requires handling temporal dynamics, time-varying treatments, and unobserved confounders. Existing causal foundation models (CausalPFN, CausalFM) operate only on static cross-sectional data; neural temporal methods (CRN, G-Net) require per-dataset training; and concurrent temporal-PFN proposals have not been demonstrated at industrial scale. None output explicit per-pair reliability signals alongside their CATE estimates.
  We introduce Temporal Causal Prior-Data Fitted Networks (TCPFN), a foundation model for zero-shot temporal causal discovery with learned reliability signals. TCPFN makes four contributions: (1) a Causal Judgment Head that jointly predicts null-effect probability, confounding strength, identifiability, mediation fraction, and causal regime; (2) a mixed training prior covering six causal regimes (independent, direct, confounded, mediated, time-varying confounded, feedback) plus CausalFM-style front-door and instrumental-variable priors; (3) a discrete-token panel-data architecture with cross-attention masking that prevents inter-horizon leakage; (4) zero-shot inference at industrial scale via FAISS-based context selection and one-step posterior correction.
