  On 19 benchmark datasets across five domains, TCPFN achieves competitive zero-shot causal discovery: AUROC 0.96 on Tennessee Eastman, 0.93 on SWaT, 0.98 on Causal Rivers, 0.97 on CAUSRCA. The null detector reaches NullF1 0.94, AUROC 0.99. TCPFN scales to V=1,275 on a proprietary Kraft pulp-and-paper dataset in 6 hours on a single GPU; PCMCI, a CPU-only library, on a V=666 sub-panel of the same data took 81.5 hours, extrapolating by O(V^2) to ~12.5 days at V=1,275. TCPFN's top edges identify cross-subsystem causal relationships while PCMCI's surface within-instrument controller-measurement coupling -- a scalability case study.

### [151] [MMGNN: Multi-level, multi-color graph neural networks for molecular property prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20906)

*Trung Nguyen,Duc Duy Nguyen*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** MMGNN提出了一种分层框架，将分子图分解为重叠的原子类型对特异性子图，通过化学着色（2D）和几何着色（3D）子图进行消息传递，提升了分子性质预测性能。

#### Problem

传统的分子消息传递神经网络通常通过单一图结构传播化学上多样化的相互作用，这种方式可能混合不同相互作用的信号，并且需要深层传播才能捕捉长程效应。

#### Key Idea

将分子图分解为多个重叠的、原子类型对特异性的子图（化学着色或几何着色），每个子图独立进行消息传递，再通过原子级别的聚合和分子读出合并表示，从而分离不同相互作用信号并更好地捕捉局部和长程信息。

#### System/Method Design

MMGNN包含两个变体：MMGNN-2D基于共价连接构建化学着色子图；MMGNN-3D基于空间邻近性构建几何着色子图，并增强其边的距离、角度和二面角描述符。两者均使用共享的通信消息传递骨干网络对每个子图进行处理，随后通过原子级聚合和分子级读出组合各子图的表示。

#### Experiments

在MoleculeNet的5个分类基准和3个回归基准上评估，使用标准scaffold划分和5次独立运行。MMGNN-2D在分类数据集上取得了最高宏平均AUC-ROC（0.838），在ESOL上最低RMSE（0.803）。MMGNN-3D在BBBP上取得最高平均AUC-ROC（0.956），在FreeSolv上最低RMSE（1.793）。结构分析和留一法分析进一步展示了子图分解对学习表示和原子类型对敏感性的影响。

#### Why It Matters

该工作验证了重叠的交互特异性图分解作为分子性质预测的一种有效策略，能同时利用拓扑和几何表示的互补优势，为分子图神经网络的设计提供了新思路。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该论文主要关注分子图神经网络架构，与LLM/MoE/推理加速/分布式系统等领域无直接关联。但其"多子图+共享骨干+聚合"的分层设计思路，类似于MoE中的专家分解和聚合思想，可能对设计模块化神经网络架构有启发意义。

#### Abstract

Molecular message-passing neural networks commonly propagate chemically diverse interactions through a single graph, which may mix interaction-specific signals and require deep propagation to capture long-range effects. We introduce the Multi-level, Multi-color Graph Neural Network (MMGNN), a hierarchical framework that decomposes a molecular graph into overlapping atom-type-pair-specific subgraphs while preserving atom-level resolution. MMGNN-2D constructs chemical-colored subgraphs from covalent connectivity, whereas MMGNN-3D constructs geometric-colored subgraphs from spatial proximity and augments their edges with distance, angular, and torsional descriptors. Both variants apply a shared communicative message-passing backbone to each subgraph and combine the resulting representations through atom-wise aggregation and molecular readout. We evaluated MMGNN on five classification and three regression benchmarks from MoleculeNet using common scaffold splits and five independent runs. MMGNN-2D achieved the highest macro-average AUC-ROC of 0.838 across the classification datasets and the lowest RMSE on ESOL (0.803). MMGNN-3D obtained the highest mean AUC-ROC on BBBP (0.956) and the lowest RMSE on FreeSolv (1.793), indicating complementary strengths of topological and geometric representations. Structural and leave-one-out analyses further illustrate how the subgraph decomposition affects learned representations and atom-type-pair sensitivities. These results support overlapping interaction-specific graph decomposition as a competitive strategy for molecular property prediction.

### [152] [Physics-Guided Dual-Stream Heterogeneous Graph Neural Network for Predicting Full-Field Structural Response of Stiffened Panels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20916)

*Yuecheng Cai,Jasmin Jelovica*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出了一种双流异构图神经网络（DS-HGNN），用于薄壁结构（如加筋板盒梁）的全场应力和位移预测，作为有限元分析的高效替代代理模型。

#### Problem

有限元分析（FEA）在大型复杂结构的迭代设计与优化中计算成本过高；现有神经网络代理模型难以处理变化的拓扑结构和复杂边界条件。

#### Key Idea

核心思路包括：(1) 构建面板级别的异构图表示；(2) 引入物理引导的边状态（融合边类型、空间信息和边界运动学）；(3) 双流消息传递分离纵向与横向结构信息并允许跨流交换；(4) 利用FiLM条件化的一维谱卷积结合几何与载荷效应；(5) 通过谱旁路低秩读取头重建物理场。

#### System/Method Design

DS-HGNN框架包含：(1) 面板级异构图表示；(2) 物理引导的边状态初始化（边类型、空间信息、边界运动学）；(3) 双流消息传递机制（纵向流与横向流分离，允许跨流信息交换）；(4) FiLM条件化的1-D谱卷积编码几何与载荷信息；(5) 谱旁路低秩读取头用于全场物理量重建。

#### Experiments

在具有不同几何形状、边界运动学、载荷条件和材料非线性响应的加筋板数据集上评估，对比六种异构GNN基准模型。DS-HGNN实现了最低的应力和位移RMSE，且仅需基准模型19%-38%的训练样本即可达到相当精度。专项实验显示模型能捕捉屈服及屈服后的应力特征。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为复杂薄壁结构的快速代理建模提供了新范式，在保持高精度的同时显著降低数据需求，有望加速航空、汽车等领域中大型结构的迭代设计与优化流程。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

本论文与LLM/MoE/系统研究的直接关联性较低，主要面向计算力学和结构代理建模。但其图神经网络架构设计（如双流消息传递、FiLM条件化机制、低秩读取头）中的模块化思路，对神经架构设计有一定的参考价值。

#### Abstract

Iterative design and optimization of large, complex structures require fast and accurate prediction of stress, displacement, and other fields. Finite element analysis (FEA) is computationally expensive for this task. Existing neural network surrogates often struggle with varying topologies and complex boundary conditions. This study proposes the novel Dual-Stream Heterogeneous Graph Neural Network (DS-HGNN) for full-field stress and displacement prediction in thin-walled structures, demonstrated on box beams made of stiffened panels. DS-HGNN operates on panel-level heterogeneous graph representations and introduces physics-guided edge states initialized from edge types, spatial information, and boundary kinematics. These states are updated through dual-stream message passing that separates longitudinal and transverse structural information while allowing cross-stream exchange. Geometry and loading effects are incorporated through Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM)-conditioned 1-D spectral convolutions, and physical fields are reconstructed using a spectral-bypass low-rank readout. The model is evaluated on stiffened panel datasets with different geometries, boundary kinematics, loading conditions, and material nonlinear responses. DS-HGNN achieves the lowest stress and displacement RMSE compared with six benchmark heterogeneous graph neural network models. It also reaches comparable accuracy to the strongest benchmark models using 19%-38% fewer training samples. A targeted evaluation further shows that DS-HGNN captures yield and post-yield stress features.

### [153] [The Energy Consumption of Transformer Fine-Tuning: A Roofline-Inspired Scaling Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23546)

*Mansour Zoubeirou a Mayaki*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出了一个用于预测 Transformer 模型在多 GPU 环境下训练能耗的框架，基于计算、内存流量和硬件效率的轻量级代理指标，并推导出可跨异构配置准确预测训练能耗的缩放律模型。

#### Problem

随着 Transformer 模型规模和并行度的不断增长，准确预测训练能耗变得至关重要，但现有方法缺乏一个能够跨不同 GPU 配置和并行策略进行能耗预测的建模框架。

#### Key Idea

受 roofline 模型启发，引入了一个基于加速比的硬件效率因子，用于捕捉张量并行和全分片数据并行对能耗的影响；通过将实测能耗与计算量、内存流量和硬件效率等轻量级代理指标关联，推导出能耗缩放律。

#### System/Method Design

提出一个多 GPU Transformer 训练能耗建模框架：1) 对 BERT 模型进行受控的架构扫描，收集实测能耗数据；2) 将能耗与计算量、内存流量等轻量级代理指标关联；3) 引入基于加速比的硬件效率因子，刻画张量并行和全分片数据并行策略的影响；4) 推导出缩放律模型，用于跨异构配置预测训练能耗。

#### Experiments

基于 BERT 模型的受控架构扫描实验，测量了不同模型规模和并行配置下的实际能耗。实验涵盖了张量并行和全分片数据并行等策略。论文声称该缩放律模型能够准确预测跨异构配置的训练能耗，但摘要中未提供具体的基线方法、指标数值或对比结果。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为可持续和成本感知的 AI 系统设计提供了关键的能耗预测能力，使研究人员和工程师能够在不同硬件和并行策略下提前估算 Transformer 训练成本，有助于推动绿色计算和能效优化。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。直接针对 LLM 训练能耗建模，涵盖张量并行和全分片数据并行等分布式训练策略，涉及 GPU 集群下的计算、内存带宽和硬件效率等系统级指标，对大规模 LLM/MoE 训练的能耗优化和资源调度具有重要参考价值。

#### Abstract

Transformer-based models underpin modern natural language processing but incur rapidly growing computational and energy costs. As training scales in both model size and parallelism, accurately predicting energy consumption has become critical for sustainable and cost-aware system design. We present a framework for modeling the energy consumption of Transformer training on multiple GPUs. Using controlled architectural sweeps of BERT models, we relate measured energy to lightweight proxies for compute, memory traffic, and hardware efficiency. Inspired by roofline models, our approach incorporates a speedup-based hardware-efficiency factor that captures the effects of tensor parallelism and fully sharded data parallelism. We derive a scaling law model that accurately predicts training energy across heterogeneous configurations.

### [154] [Short-Term Electricity Demand Forecasting for New England Using a Hybrid Transformer-XGBoost Framework with Weather, Calendar, and COVID-19 Indicators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20918)

*Reza Ghanavati,Behrooz Mosallaei*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出一种Transformer编码器与XGBoost结合的混合框架用于新英格兰地区日前电力需求预测，并揭示COVID-19特征在训练后因时间有效性衰减而沦为噪声导致过拟合的核心机制。

#### Problem

电力需求预测中，COVID-19流行病学变量在2020-2021年具有强预测信号，但到2022年中社会适应完成后，这些特征的时间有效性衰减，导致模型过拟合过时的疫情模式，反而降低预测性能。

#### Key Idea

通过消融实验、SHAP时间分析以及Diebold-Mariano检验，系统揭示了"时间有效性衰减"机制：疫情带来的行为扰动在2020-2021年驱动了强COVID-需求信号，但社会适应完成后，流行病学特征沦为噪声并放大过拟合。

#### System/Method Design

混合框架由两部分组成：(1) Transformer编码器用于时间特征提取；(2) XGBoost梯度提升决策树用于日前电力需求预测。输入特征包括新英格兰六州六城市气象观测、日历与节假日效应、自回归需求滞后项以及COVID-19流行病学变量。超参数优化使用Optuna与多变量Tree-structured Parzen Estimator，经500次试验调优，采用无数据泄漏的70/15/15时间顺序切分。

#### Experiments

混合模型测试RMSE为8,876 MWh，MAPE 2.05%，R² 0.906；纯XGBoost基线RMSE 9,304 MWh，MAPE 2.21%，R² 0.896。Diebold-Mariano检验(HLN修正)确认427.7 MWh差异在统计上不显著(DM=-1.126, p=0.262)。消融实验：移除COVID特征使混合模型RMSE恶化3.2%，却使XGBoost-only改善1.2%。SHAP时间分析显示，8个COVID特征中有5个在疫情后期测试集上的重要性排名高于疫情活跃的训练集，表明模型过度套用了已过时的疫情模式。

#### Why It Matters

该工作不仅提出了一个有效的混合预测框架，更核心的贡献在于系统揭示了时间相关特征在跨时间域泛化时的"时间有效性衰减"问题——这是一个在时序预测中常被忽视但普遍存在的机制，对构建鲁棒的、适应非平稳环境的预测系统具有重要指导意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然本文聚焦电力需求预测，但"时间有效性衰减"机制对LLM系统研究有重要启示：(1) LLM训练数据中的时间敏感特征（如新闻事件、流行术语）同样会因时间推移而衰减，导致模型过拟合历史模式；(2) 该工作采用的消融实验+SHAP时间分析的诊断方法可迁移至评估LLM对时序特征的依赖与过拟合程度；(3) Transformer编码器与树模型的混合架构思路可借鉴用于LLM推理加速或MoE路由中的特征融合设计。

#### Abstract

Accurate short-term electricity demand forecasting is critical for reliable power system operation, energy market planning, and infrastructure optimization. This paper presents a hybrid framework combining a Transformer encoder for temporal feature extraction with gradient-boosted decision trees (XGBoost) for daily electricity demand forecasting across New England. The framework integrates meteorological observations from six cities spanning all six New England states, calendar and holiday effects, autoregressive demand lags, and COVID-19 epidemiological variables. Hyperparameter optimization uses Optuna with a multivariate Tree-structured Parzen Estimator over 500 trials, with a leakage-free 70/15/15 chronological train-validation-test split. The hybrid model achieves a test RMSE of 8,876 MWh, MAPE of 2.05%, and R-squared of 0.906. A tabular-only XGBoost baseline achieves RMSE of 9,304 MWh, MAPE of 2.21%, and R-squared of 0.896. A Diebold-Mariano test (Harvey-Leybourne-Newbold correction) confirms the 427.7 MWh difference is statistically indistinguishable from noise (DM = -1.126, p = 0.262). An ablation study reveals COVID-19 features improved training accuracy but had asymmetric test effects: removal degraded hybrid RMSE by 3.2% while marginally improving XGBoost-only by 1.2%. A SHAP temporal analysis shows 5 of 8 COVID features rank higher on the post-acute test set than during pandemic-active training, indicating the model over-applies learned pandemic patterns. These findings establish temporal validity decay as a central mechanism: behavioral disruptions drove a strong COVID-demand signal during 2020-2021, but adaptation was complete by mid-2022, leaving epidemiological features as noise amplifying overfitting to stale pandemic patterns.

### [155] [$Ω$: Operator-based Mixture Ensemble for Generative Assimilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20920)

*Pouria Behnoudfar,Nan Chen*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出Ω框架，通过融合条件高斯代理建模、无监督分数学习和生成采样，实现高维非线性非高斯后验分布的高效数据同化。

#### Problem

在高维非线性部分观测系统中，传统方法（如集合卡尔曼滤波）对强非高斯后验不准确，而粒子滤波存在严重可扩展性问题；基于分数的生成方法虽好但需要监督训练，依赖难以获取的真实后验样本。

#### Key Idea

利用条件高斯代理提供解析的闭式条件后验作为基线，仅学习残差偏差（residual discrepancy），通过无监督分数匹配和退火朗之万采样逐步从基线向真实后验精细化，无需真实后验样本。

#### System/Method Design

Ω框架包含四个核心组件：(1) 条件高斯代理模型，提供非线性非高斯基线近似，对未观测变量有闭式条件后验；(2) 利用闭式条件分布解析恢复高维未观测分量，降低计算代价；(3) 仅通过集成轨迹的降噪分数匹配学习基线以外的残差偏差，无需监督；(4) 通过高斯混合表示重建完整的非高斯后验分布，并用退火朗之万采样迭代精化集成成员。

#### Experiments

在多个具有间歇性和极端事件的湍流模型上验证，结果表明Ω持续提升了后验准确性。具体基准方法、指标和量化结果在摘要中未明确给出。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次将条件高斯代理与无监督分数学习有机结合，无需真实后验样本即可高效处理高维非高斯数据同化问题，为大规模非线性动力系统的后验估计提供了可扩展的新范式。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

相关性间接。该框架中的混合模型表示（高斯混合）、基于分数的生成采样（如退火朗之万）以及降噪分数匹配等技术，与生成式AI和概率建模有共通之处。但论文聚焦于数据同化领域，未直接涉及LLM、MoE、KV cache、分布式训练/推理等系统研究主题。

#### Abstract

Characterizing non-Gaussian posterior distributions in partially observed high-dimensional nonlinear systems remains a fundamental challenge in data assimilation. Ensemble Kalman filters rely on Gaussian approximations that can be inaccurate for strongly non-Gaussian posteriors, whereas particle filters suffer from severe scalability limitations. Recent score-based generative approaches improve posterior characterization but typically require supervised training with ground-truth posterior samples, which are unavailable in most practical applications. We introduce $Ω$ (Operator-based Mixture Ensemble for Generative Assimilation), a scalable framework that integrates conditional Gaussian surrogate modeling, unsupervised score learning, and generative sampling. The conditional Gaussian surrogate provides a nonlinear non-Gaussian baseline approximation while admitting closed-form conditional posterior distributions for the unresolved variables. First, $Ω$ exploits these closed-form conditional distributions to analytically recover the high-dimensional unobserved component, reducing computational cost and mitigating the curse of dimensionality. Second, $Ω$ learns only the residual discrepancy beyond an analytical baseline through denoising score matching using ensemble trajectories alone, eliminating the need for ground-truth posterior samples and substantially reducing the learning burden. Third, $Ω$ reconstructs the full non-Gaussian posterior distribution of both observed and unobserved variables via a Gaussian mixture representation, capturing multimodal, skewed, and heavy-tailed statistics. Finally, $Ω$ employs annealed Langevin sampling to iteratively refine ensemble members from the baseline toward the target posterior. $Ω$ is validated on several turbulent models with intermittency and extreme events, consistently improving posterior accuracy.

### [156] [Hierarchical Pooling for Sheaf Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20932)

*Dionisia Naddeo,Carlo Abate,Pietro Liò,Nicola Toschi,Filippo Maria Bianchi*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** HiSP是一种基于局部谱粗化的、支持Sheaf神经网络的分层池化框架，通过投影到簇内Sheaf拉普拉斯算子的低频本征模构造粗尺度茎信号，并实现了兼容SNN的GNN池化层。

#### Problem

现有的Sheaf神经网络主要工作在固定的图分辨率上，缺乏一种原理性的池化机制来构建层次化表示，限制了其在需要多尺度分析的图任务上的应用。

#### Key Idea

利用局部谱粗化：对图的每个簇（partition），将细尺度茎信号投影到簇内Sheaf拉普拉斯算子的低频本征模上，从而构造粗尺度茎；并通过Galerkin算子实现细尺度能量在粗空间上的表示。

#### System/Method Design

HiSP框架包含以下核心设计：(1) 给定图的一个划分，对每个簇内部计算本地Sheaf拉普拉斯算子的低频本征模；(2) 利用这些本征模定义上链层面的延拓（prolongation）映射，将细尺度茎特征投影到粗尺度；(3) 通过Galerkin算子建模粗空间上的能量表示；(4) 将粗化产生的近似误差分解为截断损失（丢弃的高频模）和实现损失（投影算子用粗Sheaf表示时的误差）；(5) 提供兼容SNN的GNN池化层实现及PyG代码，支持批处理、提升Sheaf拉普拉斯算子和层次化架构。

#### Experiments

摘要中未明确给出具体的实验设置、基线、数据集或量化结果，仅说明提供了PyTorch Geometric（PyG）兼容的实现。

#### Why It Matters

这项工作首次为Sheaf神经网络提供了原理性的分层池化机制，弥合了Sheaf图表示学习与层次化图结构学习之间的鸿沟；其对粗化误差的理论分解也为理解Sheaf池化的信息损失提供了分析工具。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该工作主要面向图神经网络（GNN）和Sheaf神经网络，与LLM系统、MoE、推理加速、KV缓存等方向的直接关联性较低。但其提出的谱粗化池化思想在更广泛的图计算和层次化表示学习领域具有参考价值，理论上可被用于需要图层次化处理的系统架构中的表示压缩。

#### Abstract

Sheaf Neural Networks (SNNs) generalize Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) by replacing scalar node signals with stalk-valued signals and by using restriction maps to measure compatibility across edges. Unlike standard graph diffusion, which encourages neighboring node features to become similar, sheaf diffusion promotes consistency through the restriction maps and can therefore model more general relationships between neighboring nodes. However, existing sheaf neural architectures mainly operate at a fixed graph resolution and do not provide a principled pooling mechanism for building hierarchical representations. In this paper, we introduce Hierarchical Sheaf Pool (HiSP), a sheaf-aware pooling framework based on local spectral coarsening. Given a partition of the graph, HiSP constructs each coarse stalk by projecting fine stalk-valued features onto the low-frequency eigenmodes of the cluster-internal sheaf Laplacian. These local modes define a cochain-level prolongation map, which allows the fine sheaf energy to be represented on the coarse space through a Galerkin operator. We further analyze the approximation induced by coarsening by separating truncation loss, due to discarded local modes, from realization loss, due to representing the projected operator as a coarse sheaf. Finally, we implement HiSP as a GNN pooling layer compatible with SNNs and provide a PyG implementation supporting batching, lifted sheaf Laplacians, and hierarchical architectures.

### [157] [Towards Robust Training in NNGPT AutoML Pipeline: A Loss-Optimizer Pairing Selection Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20933)

*Anton Abramochkin,Radu Timofte,Dmitry Ignatov*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文对6种优化器与3种损失函数的全部18种组合，在33种异构架构和6个图像分类数据集上进行了系统性实证研究，发现不存在普遍最优的单一配对，但交叉熵与Adam/AdamW是最鲁棒的选择。

#### Problem

自动化架构搜索（AutoML）中，损失函数与优化器的配对选择对异构架构池的性能影响尚未被系统研究，不清楚是否存在一个通用的最优配方适用于所有架构。

#### Key Idea

通过对18种损失-优化器组合在33种结构多样的基础架构上进行大规模、系统化的对比实验，揭示不同配对在不同架构族和数据集上的表现差异，从而提供可操作的选型指导。

#### System/Method Design

论文采用LEMUR异构架构池中的33种兼容基础架构，对6种优化器（SGD+Momentum、Adam、AdamW、RMSprop、Adagrad、Adadelta）和3种损失函数（交叉熵CEL、负对数似然NLL、基因进化NGL损失）的全部18种组合进行实验。所有594个变体通过源码级注入流水线自动生成，并在固定超参数下评估，确保精度差异仅来源于配对选择。

#### Experiments

在6个图像分类数据集（CelebA-Gender、CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100、ImageNette、MNIST、SVHN）上进行实验，共产生594个模型变体。主要发现包括：（1）无单一配对普遍最优；（2）交叉熵+Adam/AdamW是最鲁棒的组合；（3）NGL在标准卷积分类器上与CEL有竞争力，但必须搭配自适应优化器，与SGD或累积方法搭配时性能大幅下降；（4）Adagrad和Adadelta在固定超参数下始终表现不佳。

#### Why It Matters

该研究为AutoML和异构架构搜索提供了关于损失函数与优化器选型的实证指南，避免了盲目选择带来的性能损失，尤其对NNGPT框架中的自动化配置具有直接指导意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

本文主要聚焦于图像分类领域的AutoML和异构架构搜索，与LLM系统、MoE、推理加速、KV缓存等方向无直接关联。但其关于损失-优化器配对选择的方法论和实证结论，对任何需要自动调优异构模型的系统（包括可能涉及MoE或LLM架构搜索的场景）具有一定的借鉴意义。

#### Abstract

The choice of loss function and optimizer is an important decision, that shapes further model training. Yet automated architecture search pipelines (AutoML) benefits significantly more from the optimal pairing selection and vice versa. This paper investigates whether a single recipe is sufficient for heterogeneous architecture pools, or whether the optimal pairing varies across structurally diverse models. We conduct a systematic empirical study of all $3 \times 6 = 18$ combinations of six optimizers (SGD+Momentum, Adam, AdamW, RMSprop, Adagrad, Adadelta), paired with three loss functions: Cross-Entropy (CEL), Negative Log-Likelihood (NLL), and the recently introduced genetically evolved NGL loss across the base models presented in LEMUR heterogeneous architecture pool on six image classification datasets (CelebA-Gender, CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, ImageNette, MNIST, SVHN). The 18 loss-optimizer configurations are applied to each of the 33 compatible base architectures taken from the LEMUR pool, resulting in 594 variants that were generated fully automatically by a source-level injection pipeline and evaluated under fixed hyperparameters, ensuring that observed accuracy differences are attributable solely to the loss-optimizer pairing. Our results confirm that no single pairing is universally optimal. Cross-Entropy with Adam or AdamW is the most robust choice across architecture families and datasets. NGL is a competitive alternative to CEL on standard convolutional classifiers, but only when paired with adaptive optimizers; it degrades substantially with SGD or accumulation-based methods. Adagrad and Adadelta consistently underperform under fixed hyperparameters regardless of loss function, highlighting their sensitivity to learning rate tuning. These findings provide actionable guidance for loss-optimizer selection within NNGPT Framework.

### [158] [Learning through Internalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20937)

*Nikolaos Tsilivis,Nirmit Joshi,Marko Medvedev,Julia Kempe,Nati Srebro*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文研究了基于神经网络的系统如何将显式计算过程"内化"到自身权重中，并首次提供了成功内化（以奇偶性学习任务为例）的可证明分析。

#### Problem

当前缺乏对"内化过程"——即神经网络模型将显式的链式思维（CoT）推理步骤吸收到自身权重中的机制——的理论理解和可证明分析，特别是哪些任务/自动机更难内化、内化对分布外性能的影响尚不清楚。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察是：Transformer可以通过逐步移除CoT令牌的方式，将外部的逐步推理过程（如半自动机模拟、奇偶性计算）内化到模型权重中，实现从"带CoT监督学习"到"直接端到端计算"的转变，且该过程与正分布偏移现象相关。

#### System/Method Design

论文通过理论分析和实验研究了Transformer内化半自动机模拟的过程；具体地，针对奇偶性学习任务，设计了一个简化的一层Transformer模型，证明其在有显式CoT监督时先学会目标，然后在CoT令牌逐步移除的过程中内化自回归生成，最终学会直接计算奇偶性。

#### Experiments

实验方面，论文研究了不同类别的半自动机在内化难度上的差异，并揭示了内化的负面效应——分布外性能的逐步退化。在奇偶性任务上，提供了严格的理论证明：没有CoT监督时该任务在计算上是难以从数据中学习的，而论文提出的内化过程可以成功实现学习。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次为神经网络的内化过程提供了可证明的理论分析，解释了CoT推理为何可以被"蒸馏"进模型权重中，揭示了内化与分布外性能退化之间的权衡，并为理解大语言模型从推理到直接响应的能力转变提供了理论基础。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。该研究直接分析了Transformer中链式思维（CoT）的内化机制，这对于理解LLM推理能力的压缩和加速（如用单次前向传播代替多步CoT）具有重要指导意义。内化过程与分布外性能退化的发现对模型部署中的鲁棒性评估有启示。此外，该工作与正分布偏移理论的关系也为LLM系统设计提供了新的理论视角。

#### Abstract

We study internalization processes, by which neural-network-based systems absorb an explicit computational procedure into their own weights, and how they facilitate learning. We investigate how transformers internalize the simulation of semiautomata by internalizing chain-of-thought (CoT) tokens, which classes of semiautomata are harder to internalize, and expose the flip side of internalization, that is, a progressive degradation of out-of-distribution performance. We then provide the first provable analysis of successful internalization: for the task of learning parities, we show that a simplified one-layer transformer provably first learns the target with explicit CoT supervision and then internalizes the autoregressive generation as CoT tokens are progressively removed, learning to directly compute the parity. This task is computationally hard to learn from data without CoT supervision. Finally, we discuss how learning through internalization relates to the \textit{Positive Distribution Shift} phenomenon recently introduced by~\citet{Med+26}.

### [159] [Grouped Query Experts: Mixture-of-Experts on GQA Self-Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20945)

*Vishesh Tripathi,Abhay Kumar*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** GQE（Grouped Query Experts）在分组查询注意力（GQA）的基础上引入混合专家层，通过路由为每个token选择k个查询头专家，在保持KV缓存优势的同时将活跃查询头计算量减半，且不损失下游任务精度。

#### Problem

标准密集注意力机制对所有token施加相同的注意力头集合，无法根据token难度或信息内容差异化分配计算资源；随着序列变长，注意力计算呈二次增长，浪费大量计算。

#### Key Idea

在GQA的每个组内引入路由机制，为每个token仅激活k个查询头专家（而非全部查询头），而所有KV头保持密集且不变，从而在保留GQA的KV缓存优势的前提下减少查询头的计算开销。

#### System/Method Design

GQE在分组查询注意力（GQA）的每个组之上叠加一个混合专家（MoE）层：每个GQA组内有一个路由器，为每个token选择k个查询头专家（query-head experts）进行激活，而所有键值头（KV heads）保持密集不变。这样既保留了GQA的KV缓存收益，又仅减少了活跃查询头的计算量。

#### Experiments

在250M参数规模、固定30B token预算下进行训练。GQE与全激活的GQA基线相比，每个token仅激活一半的查询头，但在下游任务精度上与之持平。

#### Why It Matters

GQE为长上下文场景下Transformer注意力计算的高效化提供了新思路，通过查询头的稀疏激活显著降低计算成本而不牺牲精度，这对于扩展Transformer到更长序列具有实际价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关：GQE将MoE思想引入注意力机制内部的查询头选择，属于LLM系统推理加速与稀疏计算的研究方向。它保持了GQA的KV缓存优势（对内存系统友好），同时通过查询头稀疏化降低计算量，对长上下文LLM的推理效率和系统部署有直接意义。

#### Abstract

Self-attention is central to Transformer performance and is often the most expensive part of the Transformer at long context lengths because its pairwise token interactions scale quadratically with sequence length. Standard dense attention also applies the same set of attention heads to every token regardless of token difficulty or information content. This uniform activation can waste compute, especially as sequences grow longer and attention cost increases rapidly. We propose Grouped Query Experts (GQE), a mixture-of-experts layer on top of grouped-query attention (GQA). Within each GQA group, a router selects k query-head experts per token while all key-value (KV) heads remain dense and unchanged. Thus, GQE keeps the KV cache benefits of GQA and reduces only the active query-head computation. On a fixed 30B token budget at the 250M parameter scale, GQE matches the all-active GQA baseline in downstream accuracy while activating half the query heads per token.

### [160] [A Gated Graph Neural Network Approach to Fast-Convergent Dynamic Average Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20955)

*Antonio Marino,Claudio Pacchierotti,Paolo Robuffo Giordano*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出了一种基于门控图神经网络（GGNN）的分布式动态平均估计方法，通过将估计过程建模为分布式自回归器，实现了比传统模型方法更快的收敛速度和更高的精度。

#### Problem

传统基于模型的动态平均估计方法面临收敛速度慢和对网络拓扑变化敏感的问题，难以在快速变化的环境中高效运行。

#### Key Idea

利用门控图神经网络（GGNN）的固有结构，将动态平均估计过程建模为分布式自回归器，从而实现快速收敛和稳定性；通过引入正则化项保证收敛，并设计编码-解码机制降低通信开销。

#### System/Method Design

提出基于GGNN的学习方法：将估计过程建模为分布式自回归器，利用GGNN处理图结构信息的能力实现全分布式估计；训练时引入正则化项以保证收敛性；采用编码-解码机制压缩通信信息，在保持精度的同时降低通信开销。

#### Experiments

通过大量数值实验，将所提方法与传统的基于模型估计器对比。结果表明，所提方法在收敛速度和估计精度上均显著优于传统方法。具体基线、数据集和度量指标在摘要中未明确说明。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次将图神经网络应用于动态平均估计问题，提供了一种可学习的替代方案，为多智能体系统在动态环境下的协同估计开辟了新路径，具有重要的理论和应用价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该论文聚焦于多智能体系统的分布式估计，与LLM/MoE系统的直接关联有限。但其中涉及的图神经网络用于分布式信息聚合、编码-解码机制降低通信开销、分布式自回归建模等思想，对分布式LLM推理中的通信优化、MoE模型中专家间的信息聚合策略等系统研究具有一定的启发意义。

#### Abstract

Dynamic average estimation is a critical problem in multi-agent systems, enabling agents to collaboratively estimate time-varying signals using only local information exchange. Traditional model-based approaches often face challenges related to convergence speed and sensitivity to network topology changes. This paper introduces a novel learning-based solution leveraging Gated Graph Neural Networks (GGNNs) for fast-convergent dynamic average estimation in a fully distributed manner. Taking advantage of the inherent structure of GGNNs, the proposed method models the estimation process as a distributed autoregressor, ensuring rapid convergence while maintaining stability. We incorporate a regularization term during training to enforce convergence guarantees and introduce an encoding-decoding mechanism to reduce communication overhead without sacrificing accuracy compared to standard GGNNs. Extensive numerical experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly outperforms conventional model-based estimators in terms of both convergence speed and precision, making it a promising alternative for multi-agent applications that require dynamic average estimation.

### [161] [Right Knowledge, Wrong Answer: Test-Time Steering for Temporal Fact Conflicts in Open-Weight Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20959)

*Elias Hossain,Sourav Saha,Umesh Chandra Biswas,Sanjeda Sara Jennifer*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出了一种无需重训练或外部检索的测试时干预方法（TAS），通过在检测到参数知识时间冲突时对关键层进行隐藏状态操控，选择性覆盖模型中的过时事实。

#### Problem

大语言模型在参数中同时存储了旧事实和更新的替代事实，但标准提示仍会输出过时答案。作者将其形式化为参数时间冲突（Parametric Temporal Conflict, PTC）问题。

#### Key Idea

通过检测模型内部表示中是否存在时间冲突，定位对事实更新最关键的层，然后在推理时通过激活修补（activation patching）将隐藏状态朝更新后的表示方向引导，从而在不重新训练或外部检索的情况下覆盖过时知识。

#### System/Method Design

TAS（Temporal Attractor Steering）是一个三阶段测试时干预方法：(1) 检测可能的时间冲突；(2) 识别冲突关键层（conflict-critical layer）；(3) 在该层将隐藏状态向新事实表示方向引导（steering），实现单层激活修补。

#### Experiments

构建了涵盖5个Wikidata关系的8,746条记录验证基准。评估了Qwen-2.5-1.5B/7B、Mistral-7B-v0.3、Llama-3.1-8B四个模型。单层激活修补在所有模型上实现0.72-0.85的答案翻转率。端到端TAS解决29-57%的PTC情况，同时在非冲突查询上保持85-99%的准确率，在四个模型中的三个上优于ITI基线。

#### Why It Matters

展示了过时的参数化知识可以在推理时被选择性覆盖，无需重训练或外部知识检索。这为模型事实时效性维护提供了一种轻量级、高效的替代方案。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。TAS是一种纯推理阶段的干预方法，可用于LLM系统的知识时效性管理。其核心机制（单层激活修补、隐藏状态操控）与模型内部机制可解释性研究高度相关。虽然不直接涉及MoE或分布式系统，但测试时干预的思路可推广到其他LLM推理加速或知识更新场景中。

#### Abstract

Large language models can store both outdated facts and newer superseding facts in their parameters, but standard prompting may still elicit the outdated answer. We formalize this problem as Parametric Temporal Conflict (PTC) and introduce Temporal Attractor Steering (TAS), a three-stage test-time intervention that detects likely conflicts, identifies a conflict-critical layer, and steers hidden states toward newer-fact representations without retraining or external retrieval. We construct an 8,746-record verified benchmark across five Wikidata relations and evaluate four open-weight language models from three families: Qwen-2.5-1.5B/7B, Mistral-7B-v0.3, and Llama-3.1-8B. Single-layer activation patching achieves answer-flip rates of 0.72-0.85 across all models. End-to-end TAS resolves 29-57% of PTC cases while preserving 85-99% accuracy on non-conflict queries, outperforming a matched ITI baseline on three of four models. These results show that outdated parametric knowledge can be selectively overridden at inference time.

### [162] [Is Our Benchmark Enough? An Analysis of Continual Learning for MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20961)

*Van-Tuan Tran,Shruthi Gowda,Merim Dzaferagic,Marco Ruffini*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文质疑多模态大语言模型持续学习中MLLM路由器的必要性，提出无训练、无重放的原型路由方法RePRo，并指出现有基准存在任务高度可分和固定任务顺序的结构性缺陷。

#### Problem

当前MR-LoRA方法假设持续学习中必须使用基于MLLM的路由器来处理复杂多模态输入，但这可能是不必要的开销；同时现有MLLM持续学习基准（MLLM-CL）存在结构性缺陷，导致评估结果不能反映真正的持续迁移能力。

#### Key Idea

路由不需要MLLM，简单的训练无关原型路由即可匹配MLLM路由器的性能；共享专家在MLLM持续学习中并无实际收益；现有基准的任务在表示空间中高度可分且采用固定任务顺序，导致评估偏向独立学习而非真正的持续迁移。

#### System/Method Design

提出RePRo（Replay-free Prototypical Router），一种无需训练、无需重放的原型路由方法：使用冻结的预训练特征和任务原型来匹配输入，替代MR-LoRA中基于MLLM的路由器，大幅降低计算成本。

#### Experiments

在MLLM-CL基准上与MR-LoRA方法进行对比。结果表明RePRo以远低于MR-LoRA的计算成本达到了与其MLLM路由器相匹配的性能。同时通过分析揭示了基准的两个结构性问题：任务高度可分和固定任务顺序导致结论对单一学习轨迹敏感。

#### Why It Matters

本文纠正了领域内对MLLM路由器必要性的错误认知，提出更轻量的替代方案，并为未来MLLM持续学习基准的设计提供了明确的方向，推动该领域向真正评估持续迁移能力的方向发展。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关：本文聚焦多模态大语言模型的持续学习，提出无训练的原型路由方法大幅降低推理开销；讨论了共享专家（MoE思想）在持续学习中的局限性；对MLLM系统的高效适应和部署具有参考价值。

#### Abstract

Continual adaptation is essential for multimodal large language models (MLLMs) deployed across evolving domains, but the state-of-the-art MR-LoRA method highly relies on the assumption that a MLLM-based router is necessary to process complex multimodal inputs. This paper revisits this claim on the MLLM-CL benchmark and argues for two claims. \textbf{First}, routing does not require an MLLM: a simple training-free, replay-free ptotypical routing method (\textsc{RePRo}), uses frozen pretrained features and task prototypes to match the MLLM-based router of MR-LoRA at far lower computational cost. \textbf{Second}, shared experts do not improve continual learning for MLLMs, despite their theoretical appeal. We show that these findings arise from two structural limitations of MLLM-CL: (1) its tasks are \textbf{highly separable} in representation space, and (2) its fixed task order makes conclusions \textbf{sensitive to a single curriculum} rather than robust across diverse continual-learning trajectories. As a result, the benchmark primarily rewards learning in isolation rather than genuine continual transfer. This motivates a new design for future benchmarks of continual MLLM learning, with overlapping task manifolds, multiple task orders, fine-grained domain shifts, and evaluation protocols that reward forward transfer as well as retention.

### [163] [Formalizing Task-Space Complexity for Zero-Shot Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20967)

*Jung-Hoon Cho,Heling Zhang,Siqi Du,Roy Dong,Cathy Wu*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出了一种基于性能的定向任务差异度量（signed divergence），用于量化策略在上下文动态系统中的零样本泛化能力，并通过贪婪源选择策略以最少策略实现可证明的泛化覆盖。

#### Problem

在上下文动态系统中，单一策略往往过于保守（无法适应多样条件），而完全自适应方案过于复杂。缺乏一种基于性能的任务相似性度量来指导如何选择源策略以实现对新环境的零样本泛化保证。

#### Key Idea

引入 signed divergence——一种以性能为中心的定向任务不相似度量，它可以直接上界从源上下文到目标上下文的泛化差距。该度量诱导出 ε-容差集，可认证源策略类何时能够泛化，并定义了任务空间复杂度的具体概念。

#### System/Method Design

(1) 定义 signed divergence 作为泛化差距的上界；(2) 基于 signed divergence 构造 ε-容差集，用于认证策略泛化；(3) 在性能局部光滑性假设下，给出容差集的内/外球认证和任务空间复杂度的实例相关体积界；(4) 在有限源场景下，将源选择问题建模为集合覆盖问题，采用贪心策略并证明其满足标准 H(n) 近似保证。

#### Experiments

在两个系统上验证：一是质量-弹簧-阻尼系统（使用LQR控制器），二是非线性CartPole系统（使用深度强化学习控制器）。实验表明，贪心策略在达到相同 ε-覆盖的情况下，所需策略数量少于均匀采样和随机基线方法。

#### Why It Matters

提供了一种基于性能而非特征距离的任务相似性度量，以及构建可泛化控制策略的实际认证工具。这使得我们可以用少量简单策略（而非复杂自适应方案）来实现对广泛任务条件的覆盖，具有良好的理论保证和实用性。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/MoE系统研究的关联：signed divergence 作为任务相似性度量的思想可类比于MoE中的专家路由选择问题——如何基于性能信号选择最合适的专家（类似于源策略）来处理不同输入（类似于目标上下文）。贪心集合覆盖的源选择策略与MoE中稀疏门控选择专家的思路有相通之处。同时，ε-容差集认证泛化能力可为LLM推理中不同上下文（如不同prompt分布）下的模型适配提供理论框架。

#### Abstract

Policies must operate across diverse conditions, yet a single policy is often conservative while fully adaptive schemes can be complex. We study zero-shot generalization in contextual dynamical systems and introduce a performance-centric, directional task dissimilarity--the signed divergence--that upper bounds the generalization gap from a source context to a target context. The signed divergence induces $\varepsilon$-tolerance sets that certify when a source policy class generalizes, and it yields a concrete notion of task-space complexity: the minimum number of source contexts needed so that every target context incurs at most $\varepsilon$ generalization gap. Under a mild local smoothness assumption on performance, the induced tolerance sets admit certified inner/outer balls and instance-dependent volume bounds on task-space complexity. In the finite-oracle setting, source selection reduces to set cover; a greedy strategy inherits the standard $H(n)$ approximation guarantee. Using a Mass-Spring-Damper system with linear-quadratic regulator (LQR) controllers and a nonlinear CartPole system with deep reinforcement learning controllers, we show that greedy selection achieves the same $\varepsilon$-coverage with fewer policies than uniform or random baselines. Our approach delivers a performance-based task similarity measure and practical certificates for building generalizable control with simple policies.

### [164] [Detecting Satellites in Radio-Frequency Data via Semi-Supervised Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20976)

*Cade W. Trotter,Maksim E. Eren,Justin C. Holmes,J. Brent Parham,David Ewing,Boian S. Alexandrov,Gian Luca Delzanno*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出一种结合非负矩阵分解（NMFk）、专家解释和分类器预测的半监督RF检测与分类流水线，用于卫星监测中的稀疏、少标签数据。

#### Problem

射频（RF）监测数据量大、可变性强、标签稀疏，传统监督深度学习方法需要大量标注样本且在RF条件变化时需重新训练，而解释这些数据通常需要专业领域知识。

#### Key Idea

利用半监督方法——先通过无监督NMFk自动确定聚类数量并发现潜在模式，再由领域专家为聚类赋予物理含义（如卫星信号、电离层环境等），最后用分类器进行预测，从而减少对大规模标注数据的依赖。

#### System/Method Design

三步流水线：（1）将RF观测数据表示为非负特征矩阵，应用带自动模型确定的NMFk（NMFk）估计最佳聚类数；（2）领域专家对聚类结果进行解释，赋予物理含义（如卫星检测、电离层背景、其他RF事件）；（3）基于解释后的聚类训练分类器，在测试集上评估性能并用于分类未来观测数据。

#### Experiments

摘要未提供具体的实验设置、基线方法、评估指标或定量结果。

#### Why It Matters

该工作提供了一种可解释且可迁移的半监督流水线，减少了RF监测中对大量预标注数据的依赖，使非专家也能借助专家解释的聚类结果高效识别卫星、空间碎片和电离层现象，具有实际应用价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/MoE/系统研究无直接关联。该工作聚焦于RF信号处理中的半监督学习与矩阵分解方法，不涉及LLM训练推理、MoE架构、KV缓存优化、分布式系统或并行计算等方向。

#### Abstract

Radio-frequency (RF) monitoring is essential for space domain awareness, but it often generates large, variable, and sparsely populated datasets with few labels. These observations can capture satellites, space debris, and the ionospheric background, yet interpreting them typically requires specialized subject-matter expertise. Supervised deep learning methods can perform well on labeled RF data, but they require many annotated examples and may need careful retraining as RF conditions change. Semi-supervised approaches offer a practical alternative for limited-data settings by using unlabeled observations to reveal latent patterns that experts can interpret. In this paper, we present a semi-supervised RF detection and classification workflow for satellite monitoring that combines Non-negative Matrix Factorization with automatic model determination (NMFk), expert-guided cluster interpretation, and classifier-based prediction. We first represent RF observations as a non-negative feature matrix and apply NMFk to estimate the number of clusters that best captures patterns in the unlabeled data. Subject-matter experts then assign physical meaning to the resulting clusters, including satellite detections, ionospheric environmental conditions, and other RF event categories. Finally, we train a classifier on these interpreted clusters to evaluate performance on a test set and categorize future observations. This pipeline reduces reliance on large pre-labeled datasets by pairing unsupervised factorization with expert interpretation, enabling an interpretable and transferable methodology for detecting, observing, and classifying behavior in RF data.

### [165] [Physics-Guided Fully Convolutional Spatiotemporal Learning Toward Digital-Twin-Enabled Microstructure Evolution Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20983)

*Michael Trimboli,Wenxi Liu,Xianqi Li*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出一种物理引导的全卷积时空学习框架，通过将热力学和动力学方程显式纳入训练目标，实现微观结构演化的高保真预测。

#### Problem

纯数据驱动的时空学习模型在预测微观结构演化时物理一致性不足，长期预测精度退化严重。

#### Key Idea

将控制微观结构演化的物理方程（热力学/动力学定律）作为残差正则化项显式融入训练目标，使学习到的动力学过程保持物理一致性，而不仅仅依赖数据拟合。

#### System/Method Design

提出一种物理引导的全卷积时空学习框架（physics-guided fully convolutional spatiotemporal learning framework），核心在于：(1) 采用全卷积架构保持可扩展性和计算效率；(2) 在训练目标中显式加入物理方程残差正则化项，约束模型预测符合已知物理定律；(3) 与以往自监督方法不同，该方法直接利用物理先验指导学习过程。

#### Experiments

以旋节线分解（spinodal decomposition）为实验场景，对比纯数据驱动基线模型。评估指标包括预测准确性、长期预测稳定性、跨空间分辨率鲁棒性、微观结构形态/统计量/演化趋势的保真度。结果表明物理引导残差正则化在各方面均优于纯数据驱动方法。

#### Why It Matters

该工作弥合了高保真物理仿真与数据驱动代理模型之间的鸿沟，在保持全卷积架构可扩展性和计算效率的同时提升了物理一致性，为数字孪生驱动的微观结构演化预测提供了可靠且高效的代理建模方案。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关性有限，属于材料科学+计算物理领域。但其核心思路——将物理/领域知识作为正则化项引入神经网络训练以提升长期稳定性和泛化能力——在LLM系统研究中有类比意义：(1) 可启发将符号规则或逻辑约束作为正则化项引入序列模型训练；(2) 全卷积架构的高效可扩展性设计思路与MoE的稀疏高效计算有交叉；(3) 长期预测稳定性问题是时序预测的共性挑战，对LLM推理中的长程依赖建模有参考价值。

#### Abstract

Understanding and predicting microstructure evolution is central to materials design, yet purely data-driven spatiotemporal learning models often suffer from limited physical consistency and degraded long-term prediction accuracy. In this work, we introduce a physics-guided fully convolutional spatiotemporal learning framework for microstructure evolution prediction. Unlike prior self-supervised approaches, the proposed method explicitly incorporates governing physical equations into the training objective, thereby encouraging the learned dynamics to remain consistent with known thermodynamic and kinetic laws. This physics-guided formulation improves predictive accuracy, long-horizon stability, and robustness across spatial resolutions and temporal prediction settings. Extensive experiments for spinodal decomposition demonstrate that incorporating physics-guided residual regularization leads to more faithful reproduction of microstructural morphology, statistics, and evolution trends compared with purely data-driven baselines. The proposed framework preserves the scalability and computational efficiency of fully convolutional architectures while bridging the gap between high-fidelity physics-based simulations and data-driven surrogate modeling, offering a reliable and efficient surrogate-modeling step toward digital-twin-enabled microstructure evolution prediction.

### [166] [Continuous-Time Probabilistic Correctors for Uncertainty-Aware Physics-Based Spacecraft Trajectory Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21021)

*Muhammad Bilal Shahid,Zhanhong Jiang,Soumik Sarkar,Cody Fleming*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出一个预测-校正框架，利用基于潜变量神经受控微分方程（Latent NCDEs）的连续时间概率校正器增强现有物理轨道传播器，实现长时域航天器轨迹预测的准确性和校准不确定性估计。

#### Problem

长时域航天器轨迹预测中，缺乏校正观测导致误差累积；高保真物理轨道传播器虽能提供精确的确定性预测，但在长时域上缺乏经过校准的不确定性估计，这对空间态势感知和交会评估等安全关键决策至关重要。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是为现有的确定性物理传播器包裹一个基于学习的连续时间概率校正器，该校正器建模预测误差的时空演化，从而同时提升预测精度并提供锐利且校准良好的全协方差不确定性估计。

#### System/Method Design

系统由两部分组成：(1) 基于物理的连续时间确定性预测器（如NASA的GMAT），负责前向轨迹传播；(2) 基于潜变量神经受控微分方程（Latent NCDEs）的概率校正器，建模预测误差的连续时间概率演化，支持不规则采样和缺失特征。引入新的损失函数促进长时域不确定性传播的校准性和锐利性。

#### Experiments

使用NASA的CDDIS真实数据，以GMAT为确定性基础传播器，在2-4天无观测的长时域预测任务和六个滚动测试窗口上进行评估。与确定性基线和基于潜变量神经ODE（Latent ODE）的校正器相比，所提方法在预测精度和不确定性校准上均取得一致性改进。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次将基于Latent NCDE的概率校正器无缝集成到现有物理传播器中，在提升长时域预测精度的同时提供校准良好的不确定性估计，对空间安全等高风险决策场景具有重要价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

间接相关。该论文的核心方法论——用Latent NCDE对时序误差进行连续时间概率建模——其思路可迁移到LLM/MoE系统中对推理误差或状态漂移的校准场景。论文中处理不规则采样和缺失特征的架构设计，对分布式系统中长序列推理和KV缓存管理的不确定性估计也有潜在借鉴意义。

#### Abstract

Long-horizon spacecraft trajectory forecasting suffers from error accumulation due to the absence of corrective observations in the forecast regime, making reliable uncertainty estimation crucial for safety-critical decision-making such as space domain awareness and conjunction assessment. While high-fidelity physics-based orbit propagators provide accurate deterministic forecasts, they typically lack calibrated uncertainty estimates over long horizons. We introduce a Predictor--Corrector framework in which a physics-based continuous-time $\textit{deterministic}$ forecaster is augmented with a learned continuous-time $\textit{probabilistic}$ Corrector that models forecast errors. The proposed Corrector can be wrapped around an existing deterministic propagator to improve forecast accuracy while producing sharp and calibrated full-covariance uncertainty estimates. The Corrector is based on Latent Neural Controlled Differential Equations (Latent NCDEs) and models the probabilistic temporal evolution of forecast errors in continuous time, naturally supporting irregular sampling and missing features. We further introduce a loss function that promotes calibration and sharpness in long-horizon uncertainty propagation. We evaluate the proposed framework on long-horizon spacecraft trajectory forecasting using real-world data from NASA's Crustal Dynamics Data Information System (CDDIS), wrapping the Corrector around NASA's General Mission Analysis Tool (GMAT). Across forecast horizons of 2--4 days without observations and six rolling test windows, the proposed approach consistently improves accuracy and uncertainty calibration compared to deterministic baselines and Latent ODE-based correctors, demonstrating the effectiveness of the continuous-time probabilistic Corrector for trajectory forecasting.

### [167] [Structure-Aware Graph Multi-Task Learning for Dynamic Sparse OD Demand Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21022)

*Ming Xu,Jiawei Cao*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出SAGMTL框架，通过结构感知的图多任务学习将动态稀疏OD预测分解为区域活动状态建模、OD连接状态判别和流量强度估计三个子任务，有效处理稀疏、长尾和零流量模式问题。

#### Problem

真实OD数据具有动态稀疏性、长尾分布和异构零流量模式，使得区分OD连接是否存在以及激活后产生多少需求变得困难。现有方法大多将其视为单一流量回归任务，难以建模低频率、间歇性和长尾的OD交互。

#### Key Idea

将OD预测分解为结构状态建模和流量强度估计两个子问题，通过多任务学习框架同时学习区域活动状态、OD连接状态和边级流量强度，利用结构感知表示显式处理稀疏性和零流量模式。

#### System/Method Design

SAGMTL包含三个核心组件：(1) 节点-边协同表示模块，通过交互式节点-边更新捕获区域语义、时间动态和空间先验，生成结构感知表示；(2) 基于这些表示联合建模稳定需求模式和短期波动来估计OD流量；(3) 多约束目标函数提升稀疏感知能力和结构一致性。

#### Experiments

在北京、成都和南京三个真实城市出行数据集上进行实验，与多个最先进基线方法对比，SAGMTL在整体性能上表现更优。消融分析验证了显式建模区域活动、连接状态和流量强度对动态稀疏OD预测鲁棒性的提升作用。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为智能交通系统中稀疏OD预测提供了一种新的多任务学习范式，通过结构性分解显式处理零流量和稀疏问题，对城市交通管理、出行需求预测等实际应用具有重要价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/MoE/系统研究的直接关联有限。但其中的多任务学习框架、结构感知图表示学习、以及处理动态稀疏数据的方法论，在LLM系统中可能启发对稀疏注意力模式或多任务MoE路由的建模思路。节点-边协同更新机制也可类比于Transformer中的token交互或图神经网络在分布式系统中的应用。

#### Abstract

Origin-Destination (OD) demand prediction is fundamental to intelligent transportation systems, yet real-world OD flows are often dynamically sparse, long-tailed, and characterized by heterogeneous zero-flow patterns. These properties make it difficult to distinguish whether an OD connection is active from how much demand it generates once activated. Many existing methods primarily treat OD prediction as a single flow regression task, which limits their ability to model low-frequency, intermittent, and long-tailed OD interactions. To address these challenges, we propose SAGMTL, a Structure-Aware Graph Multi-Task Learning framework for dynamic sparse OD demand prediction. SAGMTL decomposes OD prediction into structural state modeling and flow intensity estimation, jointly learning regional activity states, OD connection activity, and edge-level flow intensity within a unified framework. Specifically, a node-edge collaborative representation module captures regional semantics, temporal dynamics, and spatial priors through interactive node-edge updates, producing structure-aware representations for dynamic OD interactions. Based on these representations, SAGMTL estimates OD flows by jointly modeling stable demand patterns and short-term fluctuations. A multi-constraint objective further improves sparsity awareness and structural consistency. Experiments on three real-world urban mobility datasets from Beijing, Chengdu, and Nanjing show that SAGMTL achieves superior overall performance compared with state-of-the-art baselines. Further analysis demonstrates that explicitly modeling regional activity, connection states, and flow intensity improves the robustness of dynamic sparse OD demand prediction.

### [168] [Fed-CausalDiff: Decoupled Synchronization for Federated Do-Simulation and Policy Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22510)

*Pengfei Li,Mohammad Khalil*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出Fed-CausalDiff，一个联邦因果扩散框架，通过将潜在状态演化分解为全局因果得分函数和局部混淆得分函数，实现去中心化数据上的因果干预模拟与策略评估。

#### Problem

标准联邦学习仅对历史观测数据进行拟合，本质上无法支持干预推断（interventional inference）和策略评估（policy evaluation），因为顺序动作会动态改变未来状态，而纯观测模型无法捕捉这种因果机制。

#### Key Idea

将潜在状态的演化分解为两部分：全局因果得分函数（global causal score function，跨客户端共享）和局部混淆得分函数（local confounding score function，各站点特有），从而实现因果机制与混杂因素的解耦。

#### System/Method Design

Fed-CausalDiff是一个联邦因果扩散框架，核心在于解耦同步策略（Decoupled Synchronisation, DSS）：客户端在训练中仅聚合共享的因果机制部分（全局因果得分函数），而将站点特有的混杂因素保持在本地，从而处理数据异质性并支持do-simulation（干预模拟）。

#### Experiments

在四个数据集上进行了实验，评估指标为ATE（平均处理效应）和策略价值（policy-value）估计精度。结果表明Fed-CausalDiff在通信成本和推断保真度之间取得了更好的权衡。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次将联邦学习与因果扩散模型结合，解决了联邦场景下无法进行干预推断的根本性局限，对于医疗、政策分析等需要跨机构协作进行因果推理的应用具有重要价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/系统研究的相关性有限。其核心贡献在联邦因果推断领域，涉及的解耦同步策略（DSS）和通信-保真度权衡对分布式训练系统中的参数同步策略有一定参考价值，但不直接涉及LLM、MoE、推理加速、KV缓存等主题。

#### Abstract

While federated learning enables collaborative modelling on decentralised data, standard methods merely fit historical observations. This purely observational approach is fundamentally insufficient for interventional inference and policy evaluation, as sequential actions dynamically alter future states. We propose \textbf{Fed-CausalDiff}, a federated causal diffusion framework for do-simulation. The architecture decomposes the evolution of the latent state into a global causal score function and a local confounding score function. This design enables \emph{decoupled synchronisation} (DSS), where clients aggregate only the shared causal mechanism while retaining site-specific confounders locally to handle heterogeneity. Experiments on four datasets demonstrate that Fed-CausalDiff achieves better ATE and policy-value estimation accuracy, offering a favorable trade-off between communication cost and inference fidelity.

### [169] [Demystifying Numerical Instability in LLM Inference: Achieving Reproducible Inference for Mission-Critical Tasks with HEAL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21023)

*Zhenting Zhu,Lucas Thai,Shan Yu,Yicheng Liu,Yifan Qiao,Chenxi Wang,Harry Xu,Junyi Shu*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** HEAL 是一种通过 INT16 KV 缓存量化和基于 16-bit Tensor Core 的代数误差补偿策略，在保持 FP32 级别输出可复现性的同时，将性能开销降低 7.1 倍。

#### Problem

LLM 在使用 16-bit 精度部署到异构 GPU 时，由于 kernel 边界处的下转型截断误差，会导致输出灾难性不一致（即使使用贪心解码也无法避免）；而全局 FP32 管线会绕过 16-bit 硬件加速器降低计算效率，同时上转型 KV 缓存会使内存开销翻倍。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察有两点：(1) Q、K、V 张量的浮点格式未充分利用其位宽，因此可用 INT16 量化在不扩大 KV 缓存占用空间的前提下保持数值稳定性；(2) 通过代数误差补偿策略，在高速 16-bit Tensor Core 上合成高精度矩阵乘法，从而逼近 FP32 精度。

#### System/Method Design

HEAL 包含两个机制：一是对 Q、K、V 张量应用 INT16 量化，在不增加 KV 缓存开销的条件下保持数值稳定性；二是通过代数误差补偿策略，完全在高速 16-bit Tensor Core 上执行高精度矩阵乘法，避免使用低效的 FP32 计算路径。

#### Experiments

论文引入了面向关键任务可复现性评估的基准 MCR-Bench。实验结果表明，HEAL 在下游任务上实现了与 FP32 基线相同的可复现性，同时将性能开销降低了最多 7.1 倍。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次从 SASS 级分析揭示了 16-bit 精度下 LLM 输出不一致的根本原因（kernel 边界下转型截断误差），并提出了一个既能保证任务级可复现性又不牺牲硬件加速效率的实用方案，对 LLM 在金融、医疗、法律等关键领域的可靠部署具有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

高度相关。直接针对 LLM 推理中 KV 缓存的内存开销与数值精度问题，提出了一种混合精度方案；涉及量化（INT16）、Tensor Core 计算优化、数值误差补偿等系统级优化技术；对 MoE 等大规模 LLM 部署中的异构 GPU 一致性问题具有启发性。

#### Abstract

As Large Language Models (LLMs) deploy into mission-critical domains (e.g., finance, medicine, and law), output reproducibility has become a strict system requirement. While practitioners use greedy decoding to eliminate algorithmic stochasticity, empirical deployments with 16-bit precisions still exhibit catastrophic output divergence across heterogeneous GPUs. Through SASS-level profiling, we reveal that this inconsistency is fundamentally driven by truncation errors introduced during downcasting at kernel boundaries. However, achieving reproducibility via a global FP32 pipeline incurs prohibitive system penalties: bypassing 16-bit hardware accelerators hurts compute efficiency, while upcasting the KV cache doubles memory overhead. To bridge this gap, we propose Hybrid Error ALleviation (HEAL), a targeted intervention that approximates FP32 precision while resolving hardware constraints through two targeted mechanisms. First, recognizing that floating-point formats underutilize their bit-width for Q, K, V tensors, HEAL applies INT16 quantization that preserves numerical stability without expanding the KV cache footprint. Second, HEAL synthesizes high-precision matrix multiplications via an algebraic error compensation strategy, executing entirely on high-throughput 16-bit Tensor Cores. To evaluate our approach practically, we introduce MCR-Bench, a benchmark targeting reproducibility in mission-critical tasks. HEAL achieves the same level of reproducibility on downstream tasks as the FP32 baseline while reducing the performance overhead by up to 7.1x.

### [170] [An Efficient and Effective Architecture for Large-Scale Traffic Prediction via Geometry-Adaptive Square Partitioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21072)

*Yongfeng Su,Hongwen Li,Zijian Zhang,Ziquan Fang,Lu Chen,Christian S. Jensen*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** SqLinear 提出了一种结合几何自适应 Square Partition 分区算法和分层线性交互模块的高效大规模交通预测架构，以线性复杂度替代了注意力机制，显著提升了计算可扩展性。

#### Problem

现有基于神经网络的大规模交通预测方法在部署于数千个传感器场景时面临严重的计算可扩展性问题；而结合空间数据库分区技术的现有方法依赖手工几何启发式（如Grid、Quadtree、K-D Tree），会产生不规则或不均衡的数据分区，导致边界碎片化、过多填充开销和模型精度下降。

#### Key Idea

核心思路是：(1) 设计理论上可证明保证的 Square Partition 算法，将海量传感器分割成均衡、无重叠、近似正方形的空间区域；(2) 提出分层线性交互（HLI）模块，用轻量级线性交互方案替代Transformer中昂贵的注意力机制，以线性复杂度捕获局部区域内部动态和全局跨区域依赖。

#### System/Method Design

SqLinear 包含两个核心组件：(1) Square Partition——一种几何自适应分区算法，将大规模交通传感器划分成均衡、无重叠、近似正方形的空间区域，并在长宽比、均衡性和分区利用率上具有理论可证明的保证；(2) Hierarchical Linear Interaction (HLI) 模块——通过轻量级线性交互方案，高效捕获局部区域内动态和全局跨区域依赖，实现线性计算复杂度的时空建模，避免传统Transformer的高成本注意力机制。

#### Experiments

在四个大规模交通数据集和10个基线方法上进行实验，标准设置下平均MAE降低2.30%，在极端可扩展性设置下MAE降低5.81%；在空间扩展和时域扩展场景下，训练运行时间减少13.27%~30.84%。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为大规模交通预测场景提供了一种兼具高精度和高计算可扩展性的解决方案，其Square Partition提供了理论可证明的分区质量保证，HLI模块证明了线性复杂度模型可以超越昂贵的注意力机制，对实际智能交通系统的部署有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

论文聚焦于交通预测的时空建模，但其核心贡献——用线性复杂度分层交互替代注意力机制以减少计算开销，以及几何自适应数据分区以提高分布式计算效率——对于LLM推理加速、MoE专家负载均衡、分布式训练中的数据分区策略具有潜在参考价值。HLI的线性复杂度设计思路可为缓解Transformer系模型的长序列计算瓶颈提供启发。

#### Abstract

Traffic prediction is a core task in intelligent transportation systems and urban-scale decision making. Despite the effectiveness of mainstream neural-network based methods, their deployment in real-world settings with thousands of traffic sensors is jeopardized severely by their poor computational scalability. To address this, the community has attempted to incorporate spatial database partitioning techniques (e.g., Grid, Quadtree, and K-D Tree) to improve model scalability. However, these approaches rely on handcrafted geometric heuristics and often produce irregular or imbalanced data partitions, leading to boundary fragmentation, excessive padding overheads, and degraded model accuracy. In this paper, we propose SqLinear, an efficient and effective architecture for large-scale traffic prediction. First, we design Square Partition, a geometry-adaptive algorithm that partitions massive traffic sensors into balanced, non-overlapping, and near-square spatial regions. Unlike existing heuristic-based designs, Square Partition is theoretically grounded and provides provable guarantees on aspect ratio, balance, and partition utilization, establishing a high-quality foundation for downstream spatiotemporal modeling. Next, we propose a Hierarchical Linear Interaction (HLI) module that abandons the costly attention mechanisms commonly used in Transformer-based spatio-temporal models. HLI efficiently captures both local intra-region dynamics and global inter-region dependencies through a lightweight linear interaction scheme, enabling effective spatiotemporal modeling with linear computational complexity. Extensive experiments on four large-scale traffic datasets and 10 baselines show that SqLinear reduces MAE by 2.30% on average under standard setting and by 5.81% under extreme scalability settings, while reducing training runtime by 13.27%--30.84% in spatial- and horizon-scaling scenarios.

### [171] [Factored Gossip DiLoCo: Reducing Blocking Communication in DiLoCo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22768)

*Chamin Hewa Koneputugodage,Thalaiyasingam Ajanthan,Sameera Ramasinghe,Hadi Mohaghegh Dolatabadi,Shamane Siriwardhana,Gil Avraham,Violetta Shevchenko,Karol Pajak,James Snewin,Alexander Long*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出将DiLoCo的精确同步松弛为基于混合/ gossip的近似同步，通过分解同步步骤为非阻塞和阻塞两阶段，在低带宽环境下显著提升计算利用率，同时对延迟和故障具有更好的鲁棒性。

#### Problem

在低带宽、非数据中心环境下进行大规模分布式训练时，DiLoCo虽然通信频率低，但其外部同步仍然带宽密集且易受掉队者和临时故障影响，导致阻塞和高通信开销。

#### Key Idea

将精确同步松弛为基于混合/gossip的近似同步，使系统在延迟和通信故障下能优雅退化；进一步将同步分解为与计算重叠的无陈旧性非阻塞混合步骤和收紧工作节点一致性的阻塞混合步骤，实现计算利用率和优化稳定性之间的可调权衡。

#### System/Method Design

提出一种因子化同步框架：1）非阻塞混合步骤（non-blocking mixing），与计算重叠且不引入陈旧性；2）阻塞混合步骤（blocking mixing），用于收紧工作节点间的一致性。通过调整两个步骤的权重，可在计算利用率和优化稳定性之间进行权衡。

#### Experiments

在高达十亿参数的语言模型上，在低带宽设置下进行实验。结果表明，与DiLoCo相比，所提出的方法显著提升了计算利用率，训练进展从与DiLoCo相当到紧密匹配，并且对故障具有更强的鲁棒性。具体指标和数据在摘要中未详细说明。

#### Why It Matters

该工作使得大规模分布式训练在低带宽、不可靠的网络环境中变得实用，扩展了分布式训练的部署场景，降低了对高带宽数据中心基础设施的依赖。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。本文面向大规模分布式训练系统的通信优化，特别是针对低带宽环境下的LLM训练。其近似同步和分解式混合策略可应用于MoE模型训练中的专家通信优化、分布式推理系统中的梯度/参数同步，以及异构网络环境下的大模型训练加速。

#### Abstract

To make large-scale distributed training practical outside high-bandwidth datacenters, we must reduce blocking, high-volume synchronization. While DiLoCo communicates infrequently, its outer synchronization remains bandwidth-heavy and brittle to stragglers and transient failures. We relax exact synchronization to approximate synchronization via mixing/gossip, which degrades gracefully under delays and communication failures. This allows us to factorize DiLoCo synchronization into a non-blocking mixing step that overlaps computation with no staleness, and a blocking mixing step that tightens worker agreement, yielding a tunable trade-off between compute utilization and optimization stability. On up to billion-parameter language models in low-bandwidth settings, our framework substantially improves compute utilization compared to DiLoCo, with training progress ranging from comparable to closely matching it, and is more robust to failures.

### [172] [Sim2O: Efficient Offline-to-Online MARL via Joint Action Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21085)

*Bingchang Song,Yiqin Yang*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** Sim2O 提出了一种简洁的离线到在线多智能体强化学习框架，通过将联合动作分解为智能体级别的在线/离线动作组合，并利用集中式价值函数评估混合策略，实现了高效的协调适应。

#### Problem

离线到在线适应范式在单智能体强化学习中已被广泛研究，但在多智能体强化学习（MARL）中尚未被充分探索，而这一范式对于复杂协调决策场景至关重要。

#### Key Idea

将多智能体的离线到在线适应视为一个组合过程（compositional process），而不是一个单一的整体决策问题：通过动态混合各智能体的离线动作提案和在线动作提案来合成候选联合动作，并利用集中式价值函数来评估这些混合组合。

#### System/Method Design

Sim2O 框架的核心是：（1）为每个智能体分别生成离线动作提案和在线动作提案；（2）动态地将这些提案跨智能体混合，形成候选联合动作组合；（3）使用一个集中式价值函数评估这些混合组合，从而识别高价值的协调策略。该设计无需辅助训练目标或额外结构开销。

#### Experiments

论文在多个不同的基准测试上进行实证评估，Sim2O 显著优于现有的基线方法。具体的任务、基线方法和指标未在摘要中明确说明。

#### Why It Matters

该工作填补了多智能体离线到在线适应这一重要但未被充分研究的空白，并证明了极简设计（minimalist design）在此场景下不仅可行且非常有效，为后续研究提供了简洁而强大的基线。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

本文属于多智能体强化学习领域，与 LLM 系统、MoE、推理加速、KV Cache 等方向没有直接关联。但其"组合式适应"思想（将整体问题分解为可混合的子组件）在概念上对专家混合（MoE）系统中不同专家输出的动态组合有一定启发意义。

#### Abstract

Offline-to-online adaptation serves as a pivotal paradigm for mitigating the prohibitive cost of online exploration by bootstrapping reinforcement learning from offline datasets. While this paradigm has been extensively studied in single-agent settings, its extension to Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) remains largely unexplored, despite its critical relevance to complex coordinated decision-making. To bridge this gap, we introduce Sim2O, an elegant and minimalist framework for offline-to-online MARL. Rather than treating adaptation as a monolithic joint decision, Sim2O conceptualizes it as a compositional process. Specifically, candidate joint actions are synthesized by dynamically blending offline and online action proposals across agents. By leveraging a centralized value function to evaluate these hybrid combinations, Sim2O identifies high-value coordination strategies without requiring auxiliary training objectives or structural overhead. Empirical evaluations across diverse benchmarks demonstrate that Sim2O significantly outperforms existing baselines, underscoring that a minimalist design is not only viable but highly effective for multi-agent offline-to-online adaptation.

### [173] [BASIL: Bayesian Application for Scientific Iteration and Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21092)

#### System/Method Design

BASIL 是一个桌面应用程序，核心包括：(1) 图形化界面用于输入实验参数、优化目标和历史数据；(2) 预设的多种代理模型模板；(3) 专用采集函数，支持单目标和多目标优化；(4) 代理模型与采集函数耦合，迭代引导过程向目标方向优化。

#### Abstract

We introduce BASIL, a user-friendly desktop application for process optimization. BASIL employs a Bayesian approach, incorporating special acquisition functions that can be used to solve both single and multi-objective optimization problems. It provides a graphical interface that enables users to input their experimental parameters, optimization objectives, and legacy data. This is then used to build surrogate models, which are coupled with acquisition functions to guide and optimize a process towards a desired objective. To facilitate model building, BASIL provides a variety of predefined surrogate model templates. BASIL can be used to optimize any arbitrary experiment or process with known, user-defined input variables, optimization objectives, and defined output.

### [174] [SLeDGe: Semi-Supervised Learning on Data Streams with Graph Structure Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21096)

*Heechan Moon,Kijung Shin*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出SLeDGe，一种在严格内存和标签约束下，针对数据流半监督学习同时学习预测模型和自适应图结构的方法。

#### Problem

数据流半监督学习面临两大挑战：数据持续高速演进且标签稀缺；现有方法依赖固定的相似度度量或静态图结构，无法捕捉样本间关系随时间的演化。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是联合学习预测模型和自适应图结构——通过紧凑的记忆管理（有标签/无标签分别采用不同更新策略）平衡对新特征的快速适应与历史一致性保持，并通过图稀疏化过滤虚假连接以有效传播标签监督信号。

#### System/Method Design

SLeDGe维护两个紧凑的记忆库（有标签记忆和无标签记忆），采用不同的更新策略；同时学习一个自适应的关系图结构，并通过正则化鼓励图的稀疏性，从而剔除虚假连接、提升标签传播的有效性。

#### Experiments

在12个数据集上进行评估，与最先进的基线方法对比，在0.1%标签率下平均相对准确率提升31.7%，在1%标签率下平均相对准确率提升14.8%。

#### Why It Matters

首次将自适应图结构学习引入数据流半监督学习，在极低标签率（0.1%）下仍能大幅超越现有方法，为标签稀缺的流式场景提供了实用且高效的解决方案。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

论文关注数据流半监督学习，不直接涉及LLM、MoE、推理加速、KV缓存或分布式系统架构。但其紧凑记忆管理和自适应图结构设计对在资源受限环境中进行在线学习或持续学习的系统研究有一定参考价值。

#### Abstract

Semi-supervised learning (SSL) on data streams is challenging due to the continuous evolution of high-volume data and the scarcity of labels. Existing methods are limited in leveraging the intrinsic relationships among samples because they typically rely on fixed similarity measures or static graph structures, which cannot capture how relationships evolve over time. We propose SLeDGe, an SSL method for data streams that jointly learns a predictive model and an adaptive graph structure under strict memory and label constraints. SLeDGe maintains compact labeled and unlabeled memories using distinct update strategies, balancing rapid adaptation to novel features with the retention of historical consistency. In addition, by encouraging sparsity in the relational graph, SLeDGe filters out spurious connections and enables effective propagation of label supervision. Across 12 datasets, SLeDGe outperforms state-of-the-art competitors, achieving average relative accuracy gains of 31.7% with 0.1% labels and 14.8% with 1% labels.

### [175] [Efficient Network Inference via Hardware-Aware Architecture Search, Model Pruning & Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23210)

*Lucas Heublein,Mark Deutel,Axel Plinge,Felix Ott*

**TL;DR:** 该论文提出结合迭代结构化剪枝、训练后静态量化和硬件感知零样本神经架构搜索，在资源受限的嵌入式平台上实现GNSS干扰信号的高效实时推理与分类。

#### Why It Matters

为在极低功耗、小内存的嵌入式设备上部署先进的深度学习模型进行实时GNSS干扰监测提供了实用的方法指导和可行的技术路径，有助于提升关键基础设施中GNSS信号的安全性。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

虽然本文聚焦于GNSS干扰监测而非LLM，但其核心方法——结构化剪枝、后训练量化和硬件感知NAS——与LLM/MoE系统的推理加速和边缘部署高度相关。这些技术可直接迁移到LLM的小型化、KV缓存优化和嵌入式推理场景中，尤其是资源受限设备上的模型部署与压缩策略。

#### Abstract

Embedded global navigation satellite system (GNSS) interference monitoring requires fast and memory-efficient inference to process large volumes of raw in-phase and quadrature (IQ) samples in real time. At the same time, increasingly expressive deep neural networks (DNNs) are needed for robust interference classification and characterization across diverse signal conditions. This creates a fundamental tension between predictive performance and deployability on resource-constrained hardware. In this paper, we investigate efficient network inference for GNSS interference characterization using iterative structured pruning, post-training static quantization, and hardware-aware zero-shot neural architecture search (NAS). Starting from MCUNet as a compact baseline, we analyze how model compression and automated architecture optimization affect model size, computational complexity, and memory usage while maintaining task performance. Experiments on a GNSS interference dataset, covering both classification and generalized characterization, show the benefits of combining compression and hardware-aware design for embedded deployment. Our results provide practical guidance for developing compact machine learning (ML) models for real-time GNSS interference monitoring on embedded platforms (iMXRT1062 MCU, Raspberry Pi Zero 2W, and Raspberry Pi 5).

#### Abstract

Differential privacy (DP) has become the gold standard for ensuring the privacy protection of machine learning and statistical algorithms in recent decades. A plethora of algorithms and methods have been developed to enhance the utility of DP algorithms while maintaining the same level of DP. However, these are often overly complex or computationally ineffective. We propose a novel approach focusing on denoising the output of the simple additive Gaussian mechanism by adopting the idea of \textit{empirical Bayes estimation}. We highlight that the empirical Bayes approach can reduce the mean-squared error solely by taking the output of the Gaussian mechanism as input. Our numerical studies show that this simple yet powerful approach can be applied to improve upon various statistical problems, including histogram release, principal component analysis, and linear regression, often outperforming existing private algorithms.

化学扰动和基因扰动在共享靶标场景下的可互换性（跨模态翻译）缺乏系统性评估，现有工作通常分别研究化学响应预测或基因扰动预测，而未充分测试靶标匹配条件下的化学→基因翻译。
