#### Why It Matters

提供了一个可审计的框架，用于系统检验化学扰动与基因扰动在共享靶标下何时能够对齐，以及表示学习的提升是否有匹配的扰动证据支持，对生物医学发现中的跨模态建模具有重要指导意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

该工作涉及基础模型嵌入（foundation-model embeddings）的评估，与 LLM 在生物领域（如单细胞转录组）的表示学习相关；其系统化基准设计思路对 LLM 系统的评测框架构建有参考价值；但主要聚焦于计算生物学，与 MoE、推理加速、KV cache 等系统研究无直接关联。

#### Abstract

Virtual-cell and perturbation models are increasingly used to predict cellular responses for biomedical discovery, but chemical and genetic perturbations are not automatically interchangeable. Existing evaluations often study chemical response prediction or genetic perturbation prediction separately, leaving target-matched chemical-to-genetic translation under-tested. We introduce Chem2Gen-Bench, a benchmark comprising 260,084 chemical and 1,099,045 genetic perturbation profiles organized into cell-target contexts, and evaluate pairwise alignment, retrieval, protocol covariate associations, feature spaces, and foundation-model embeddings. Across matched contexts, translation fidelity is measurable but heterogeneous; background adjustment increases the association between pairwise similarity and retrieval success, while paired tests show lower mean retrieval success after adjustment under the evaluated settings. In a target-matched K562 audit, the evaluated foundation-model embeddings did not consistently improve over gene-delta baselines. Chem2Gen-Bench provides an auditable framework for testing when chemical and genetic perturbations align around shared targets and when representation gains are supported by matched perturbation evidence.

### [178] [What Accuracy and Gradient Cosine Miss: Evaluating Feedback Alignment via Scale Stability, Reference Validity, and Depth Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21126)

*Yuren Hao,Xiang Wan,ChengXiang Zhai*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文揭示了反馈对齐（FA）方法在评估中的两个隐蔽失效模式（测量简并和聚合坍缩），并提出了基于三项检查（尺度稳定性、参考有效性、深度效用）和逐层余弦报告的新型诊断评估协议。

#### Problem

当前FA方法仅依赖任务准确率和余弦相似度两项指标来评估其效果，但这一报告对存在严重缺陷：它无法检测两种独立且隐蔽的失效模式——测量简并（BP参考梯度坍缩至数值下限，使余弦不可解释）和聚合坍缩（聚合余弦掩盖了逐层异质性，导致信用集中在网络的一端）。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察是发现现有FA评估指标存在两个因果独立的隐蔽失效模式，并提出通过三项诊断检查（尺度稳定性、参考有效性、深度效用）结合逐层余弦报告来替代传统的聚合余弦报告，从而准确识别FA方法是否真正有效训练深层网络。

#### System/Method Design

提出了一套诊断评估协议，包含三项检查：(1) 尺度稳定性检查——检测残差尺度爆炸导致参考梯度坍缩的问题；(2) 参考有效性检查——验证BP参考梯度是否具有数值意义；(3) 深度效用检查——评估信用信号是否在整个网络深度上有效传播。同时将传统聚合余弦报告改为逐层余弦报告。此外，提出了逐块尺度惩罚来缓解第一类失效模式。

#### Experiments

在多种架构和方法上进行了审计测试。标准报告对在所有审计案例中均未给出任何失败信号；而本文提出的诊断协议在所有失败案例上均能以宽校准裕度识别出失效。两种失效模式被证明是因果独立的：逐块尺度惩罚缓解了模式1（残差尺度爆炸驱动参考坍缩），但不影响模式2（余弦排序与所有功能性指标相矛盾）。

#### Why It Matters

该工作的重要性在于揭示了FA领域广泛使用的评估标准存在系统性缺陷，可能导致研究者基于非功能性信用分配开展后续工作。提供了可操作的指导，帮助开发真正能够训练深层网络的FA方法，对推动生物合理性和硬件高效的深度学习训练具有重要意义。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/系统研究的关联在于：FA方法本身旨在替代BP实现更硬件高效的训练，对大规模模型训练（包括LLM）的分布式系统和硬件实现有潜在影响；诊断协议中的尺度稳定性和深度效用检查对于评估深层Transformer（如LLM中的残差架构）中的信用分配至关重要；文中专门提及terminal-LayerNorm残差架构（现代LLM常用结构）中的参考坍缩问题，直接关联到LLM系统的训练可靠性评估。

#### Abstract

Despite the success of deep learning, training deep networks in biologically plausible and hardware-efficient ways remains an open challenge. Feedback alignment (FA) methods address this by replacing backpropagation's symmetric backward weights with fixed random matrices, but their effectiveness depends critically on whether they can be accurately evaluated. The standard evaluation relies on two quantities: task accuracy and cosine similarity between the method's credit signal and the backpropagation gradient. We show that this reporting pair is insufficient by identifying two independent failure modes, both silent under current reporting: (1) measurement degeneracy, where the BP reference gradient collapses to the numerical floor in terminal-LayerNorm residual architectures, rendering cosine uninterpretable; and (2) aggregation collapse, where the aggregate cosine masks layerwise heterogeneity that concentrates credit at one end of the network. To address these limitations, we propose a diagnostic evaluation protocol based on three checks -- scale stability, reference validity, and depth utility -- together with per-layer rather than aggregate cosine reporting. Across multiple architectures and methods, the standard reporting pair gives no signal of failure in any audited case, while our protocol identifies all failures with wide calibration margins. The two failure modes are causally independent: a per-block scale penalty alleviates Mode 1 (residual scale explosion driving reference collapse) without affecting Mode 2 (cosine ranking that contradicts every functional metric we measured). Identifying these silent failures prevents researchers from building on non-functional credit assignment and provides actionable guidance for developing FA methods that genuinely train deep layers.

### [179] [Horizon Adaptive Offline Policy Learning via Value Stitching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21136)

*Kexin Zheng,Xianyuan Zhan,Xintao Yan*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出VAST方法，通过递归、自适应视界的价值拼接（value stitching）替代固定步长时序差分备份，实现更准确的离线策略学习。

#### Problem

传统TD学习方法的价值估计偏差会随任务视界累积；扩展视界方法（如n步TD、Q-chunking）采用固定的刚性好建模长度，无法灵活捕捉长视界、多阶段任务中复杂的价值结构。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是用动态视界组合（dynamic horizon composition）替代固定视界备份：通过一个以未来状态和视界长度为条件的辅助价值函数，结合一个拼接策略（stitching policy）来自适应地选择最优视界长度和未来子目标，实现变长回报的递归式价值拼接。

#### System/Method Design

VAST包含两个核心组件：(1) 未来状态和视界长度条件化的辅助价值函数，通过直接数据监督学习；(2) 拼接策略，用于选择最大化奖励的视界长度和未来子目标。两者协同实现地平线自适应的价值拼接，为离线策略优化提供准确且可贪心利用的价值监督信号。

#### Experiments

在OGBench的50个任务上进行评估，与固定步长方法、扩展视界方法和生成式价值离线RL基线对比。VAST在所有任务上表现优于这些基线，特别是在高复杂度、长视界决策任务上性能提升显著。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为离线强化学习中价值函数的长视界估计问题提供了一种自适应、灵活的解决方案，突破了传统固定步长备份的刚性限制，对复杂长视界决策任务具有重要实用价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/系统研究的关联性有限。但其中"自适应视界拼接"的思想在概念上与MoE中的动态专家路由、或LLM推理中自适应计算步长的思路有共通之处，都是通过条件化的动态选择来替代固定结构的刚性设计。不过论文本身核心是离线RL算法，不涉及LLM/MoE系统、KV cache、分布式计算或体系结构。

#### Abstract

Learning accurate value functions plays a decisive role for reinforcement learning (RL) agents to solve long-horizon, complex tasks. Conventional temporal-difference (TD) learning objectives suffer from value-estimation bias that accumulates over the horizon, while extended-horizon modeling methods, such as n-step TD backups and Q-chunking, adopt a rigid, fixed-horizon value-modeling recipe that is often not flexible enough to capture complex value structures in long-horizon, multi-stage tasks. In this paper, we show that enabling value updates with dynamic horizon composition can yield a strong offline policy learning scheme. Our method, Horizon Adaptive Offline Policy Learning via VAlue STitching (VAST), replaces fixed-horizon backups with recursive, horizon-adaptive value composition. Its key ingredient is to couple value optimization with a future state- and horizon-length-conditioned auxiliary value function that is learned through direct data supervision, and a stitching policy that optimally selects the reward-maximizing horizon length and future sub-goal to achieve horizon-adaptive value stitching. This design enables direct estimation and compositional "stitching" of variable-length returns grounded in actionable sub-goal states, providing an accurate and greedily exploitable value-supervision signal for offline policy optimization. Across 50 tasks on OGBench, VAST outperforms fixed-step, extended-horizon methods, and generative-value offline RL baselines, achieving strong performance particularly in high-complexity, long-horizon decision-making tasks.

### [180] [Dead-Direction Signatures: A Cheap Spectral Reading of Singular Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21158)

*Tejas Pradeep Shirodkar,P. J. Narayanan*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文提出Dead-Direction Signatures (DDS)，一种通过激活矩阵和Fisher-Gram谱的闭式线性代数替代昂贵SGLD后验采样、高效读取神经网络奇异几何中"死方向"（rank deficit）的方法。

#### Problem

传统估计Watanabe实对数规范阈值（RLCT）的局部学习系数（LLC）需要SGLD后验采样，每次检查点需10^4-10^6次前向-反向传播，且需逐任务校准，计算成本极高。

#### Key Idea

在奇异最小值处，激活侧谱与Fisher侧谱之间存在结构相关性；通过秩乘性体积恒等式，log det⁺(G)的斜率可计数死方向数量（rank deficit），且最小特征值对rank变化不敏感。

#### System/Method Design

DDS家族方法：读取网络某一层的激活矩阵或逐样本梯度的Fisher-Gram矩阵，用谱线性代数替代SGLD后验链；核心是dead-direction框架，通过active-volume log det⁺(G)的斜率追踪秩亏缺r，实现对死方向的闭式谱读数。

#### Experiments

在简化秩回归任务上（有闭式λ），校准LLC恢复λ的均值达99%，DDS观测值以框架预测的符号秩跟踪λ；在非线性模加Transformer上，DDS在18个数量级范围内区分d_model，而标准LLC在协议预算下呈rank-flat。

#### Why It Matters

DDS首次提供了一种廉价、闭式、逐层局部的谱方法直接读取神经网络的奇异几何结构（死方向），与LLC的集成式后验读数互补，大幅降低了理解网络复杂度的计算门槛。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关。DDS通过激活和梯度谱的闭式计算高效诊断网络奇异结构，可应用于LLM/MoE的秩分析、过参数化程度评估、模型压缩、以及理解大规模分布式训练中不同层的"有效自由度"，对推理加速和内存优化有潜在指导价值。

#### Abstract

Singular learning theory characterises the complexity of a deep network through the geometry of its loss singularities. The local learning coefficient (LLC), the standard estimator of Watanabe's real log canonical threshold (RLCT, $λ$), reads this geometry as an integrated Bayesian scalar through SGLD, which needs per-task calibration and $10^4$-$10^6$ forward-backward passes per checkpoint. We introduce Dead-Direction Signatures (DDS), a family of cheap closed-form spectral readings of singular structure: each reads a network's activation matrix or per-sample-gradient Fisher-Gram at a chosen layer, replacing the SGLD posterior chain with spectral linear algebra. The readings rest on a dead-direction framework that predicts a structural correlation between activation- and Fisher-side spectra at any singular minimum, and a rank-multiplicative volume identity that single-eigenvalue monitors cannot produce: the active-volume $\log\det^{+}(G)$ slope counts the dead directions, tracking the rank-deficit $r$ across $r \in \{1,2,3,4\}$ (slope ratios $2.0, 3.1, 4.0$ at $r{=}2,3,4$ against the predicted $2,3,4$), where the smallest eigenvalue is rank-blind. On reduced-rank regression with closed-form $λ$, calibrated LLC recovers $λ$ at $99\%$ mean and the DDS observables rank-track it at the framework-predicted sign; on a non-linear modular-addition transformer DDS separates $d_{\mathrm{model}}$ across eighteen orders of magnitude where calibrated LLC at the protocol budget is rank-flat. Complementary to LLC's integrated posterior reading, DDS gives a directional, layer-local handle on a network's dead directions, read in closed form from its activation and gradient spectra.

### [181] [Inverting the Bellman Equation: From $Q$-Values to World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21173)

*Alistair Letcher,Mattie Fellows,Alexander D. Goldie,Jonathan Richens,Jakob N. Foerster,Oliver Richardson*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文证明基于价值的强化学习智能体在足够丰富的奖励函数（如目标条件RL）训练下，会隐式编码一个准确的世界模型，并提出P-learning方法从Q值、策略和奖励中提取该隐式模型。

#### Problem

传统观点将基于模型和无需模型的强化学习视为两个独立范式，前者需要显式学习转移核P，后者仅估计与特定策略和奖励绑定的价值函数。本文挑战这一二分法，试图证明无需模型的智能体实际上隐式编码了环境模型。

#### Key Idea

核心洞察是：在足够多样的奖励函数（如多种目标）下训练的基于价值的智能体，其Q值、策略和奖励中隐式包含了转移核P的完整信息。P-learning作为Q-learning的逆过程，可以从这些量中解码出环境的内在模型。

#### System/Method Design

提出P-learning方法，它是Q-learning的逆类比：从智能体的Q值、策略和奖励中采样，解码出环境转移核P的隐式表示。论文还给出了充分条件，说明在何种类型和数量的目标条件下，智能体能够编码真实的转移核P，涵盖有限或连续状态空间上的随机和确定性MDP。

#### Experiments

在Reacher、MountainCar和随机化FourRooms环境中进行实验。即使充分条件被违反，仅使用少量奖励函数训练的智能体也能编码准确的动力学。特别地，仅在位置目标下训练的Reacher智能体，其隐式世界模型训练的policy在基于速度的分布外目标上仍能达到准最优性能。

#### Why It Matters

该工作从理论上桥接了基于模型与无需模型强化学习的鸿沟，揭示了无需模型RL智能体天然具备隐式建模能力。同时发现智能体存在隐藏的泛化能力，为理解目标条件RL的内部表征提供了新视角。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM/MoE/系统研究无直接关系，主要关注强化学习中模型学习与价值学习的理论联系。但其关于隐式表征和解码方法的思想，对理解大型模型中隐式编码的知识（如世界模型）具有潜在启发意义。

#### Abstract

Model-based and model-free reinforcement learning are traditionally viewed as separate paradigms: instead of learning a model of the transition kernel $P$, model-free agents typically estimate value functions tied to a specific policy and reward. In this paper, we challenge this dichotomy by proving that value-based agents trained on a sufficiently rich set of reward functions, e.g. using goal-conditioned RL, implicitly encode a unique and accurate world model. To extract this model in practice, we introduce \textit{$P$-learning}, an inverse analogue to $Q$-learning that samples from an agent's $Q$-values, policies and rewards to decode its internal model of the environment. We then provide sufficient conditions on the type and number of goals for which agents encode the true kernel $P$, covering both stochastic and deterministic MDPs over finite or continuous state spaces. Even when our assumptions are violated, we empirically demonstrate that agents trained on a handful of reward functions encode accurate dynamics in $\texttt{Reacher}$, $\texttt{MountainCar}$ and stochastic variants of $\texttt{FourRooms}$. Surprisingly, we find that policies trained exclusively on a \texttt{Reacher} agent's implicit world model are quasi-optimal on out-of-distribution, velocity-based goals despite position-only training -- suggesting that agents contain hidden generalisation capabilities and providing a new lens into the connection between model-based, model-free, and goal-conditioned RL.

### [182] [Rejections Based on Predictive Uncertainty Enable Reliable Routine Soil Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21179)

*Jonas Schmidinger,Robin Gebbers,Marc-Olivier Gasser,Viacheslav Barkov,G. Mick Wu,Viacheslav I. Adamchuk*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出"拒绝-重测"（reject-to-remeasure）框架，结合概率建模与不确定性引导的拒绝机制，在保证土壤属性预测精度的前提下降低测量成本。

#### Problem

光学光谱结合机器学习的土壤属性预测虽然快速低成本，但预测精度在不同土壤属性和样本间波动较大，导致其被认为不可靠，难以在常规实验室流程中实际部署。

#### Key Idea

核心思想是引入不确定性引导的拒绝机制：对于光谱预测不确定性超过预设质量阈值的样本，不采用预测结果，而是退回使用传统实验室方法重新测量，从而在成本与可靠性之间取得平衡。

#### System/Method Design

提出reject-to-remeasure框架：首先用光谱分析土壤样本并进行概率建模，计算每项预测的不确定性；若不确定性超过用户定义的质量约束，则拒绝该预测结果，将样本转由传统实验室方法重新测量。框架中使用了TabPFNv2.5和TabICLv2等现代基础模型进行概率建模。

#### Experiments

在加拿大魁北克地区的可见-近红外光谱土壤库上进行实验，展示了reject-to-remeasure框架与TabPFNv2.5和TabICLv2等基础模型的结合效果。实验表明该框架能够在满足用户定义精度要求的同时降低测量成本，但具体数值结果（精度提升百分比、成本降低幅度等）在摘要中未明确给出。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为光学光谱在土壤属性测量中的实际部署提供了一条可行路径，通过可配置的拒绝机制将快速低成本的光谱预测与高精度的传统实验室方法有机结合，有望推动土壤分析从纯实验室方法向混合工作流的转变，降低农业和环境应用的整体测量成本。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

相关度中等。该工作直接面向土壤科学和农业应用，而非LLM/MoE系统。但其中使用的TabPFNv2.5和TabICLv2属于表格数据领域的现代基础模型（foundation models），展示了基础模型在不确定性估计和预测拒绝方面的应用。其"拒绝-重测"框架中不确定性引导的决策机制和成本-精度权衡的思路，对LLM推理系统中的置信度校准、拒绝采样（rejection sampling）等研究方向有一定启发意义。

#### Abstract

Soil properties relevant to agricultural and environmental applications are conventionally measured using elaborate laboratory methods involving physical and chemical processing. While highly accurate, these conventional methods are costly and time-consuming. In contrast, optical spectroscopy paired with machine learning enables rapid and cost-effective predictions of multiple soil properties. However, spectroscopic modelling is often considered unreliable, as the predictive accuracy varies between soil properties and individual samples. To balance this trade-off between cost and reliability, we introduce reject-to-remeasure: an AI-based measurement framework that combines probabilistic modelling with uncertainty-guided rejection. In this framework, soil samples are first analysed using spectroscopy, after which predictions are rejected if their predictive uncertainty exceeds predefined quality constraints. Rejected samples are subsequently remeasured using conventional laboratory procedures. On a regional visible-near-infrared spectral soil library from Québec, we demonstrate that reject-to-remeasure with modern foundation models (TabPFNv2.5 and TabICLv2) can facilitate the integration of optical spectroscopy into routine laboratory workflows while meeting user-defined accuracy requirements and reducing measurement costs.

### [183] [TF-SNO: Time-Frequency Gated Spectral Neural Operators for Learning Non-Stationary Partial Differential Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21189)

*Yitian Zhou,Chaoning Zhang,Zhenzhen Huang,Haoxuan Yu,Jiaquan Zhang,Yiran Li,Fan Mo,Kuien Liu,Jie Zou,Caiyan Qin,Yang Yang*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出时间-频率门控谱神经算子（TF-SNO），通过状态自适应的可学习时频门控机制，使谱神经算子的频域响应随非平稳PDE系统的演化状态动态调整，从而提升长时程预测精度和鲁棒性。

#### Problem

现有的谱神经算子在求解非平稳PDE时，在整个 rollout 过程中使用共享的固定谱响应，无法匹配非平稳系统中随时间漂移的主频成分和能量分布，导致预测性能下降。

#### Key Idea

从当前演化状态中提取紧凑的频域和物理空间统计特征，生成调制系数，动态调整谱块内的谱响应，使网络能够自适应地跟随系统动力学演化，而不需要显式的时间维度或时间嵌入。

#### System/Method Design

TF-SNO 框架在谱块内部嵌入可学习的时频门控模块：首先从当前状态中提取频域和物理空间的紧凑统计量，然后通过这些统计量生成调制系数，动态控制谱响应。自适应算子块被级联堆叠以捕获多尺度特征，所有时间变化都隐式地从状态演化中学习。

#### Experiments

在6个非平稳PDE基准测试（1D和2D）上进行实验，与强基线方法对比。结果表明TF-SNO显著降低了预测误差并提升了鲁棒性，尤其在长 rollout 场景下增益明显，验证了状态依赖的谱自适应在非平稳物理系统建模中的有效性。

#### Why It Matters

该工作为解决非平稳PDE的长期演化预测难题提供了一种轻量级且有效的方案，避免了显式时间建模的复杂性，同时保持了谱方法的计算效率，具有较好的实用价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

间接相关。虽然论文聚焦于科学计算中的PDE求解，但其核心思路——根据输入状态动态调制网络内部谱响应——与MoE架构中根据输入动态选择专家、或与LLM推理中根据上下文动态调整注意力/FFN权重的思想有相通之处。状态自适应的门控机制设计对系统层面的动态资源分配和计算调度也有一定启发意义。

#### Abstract

Non-stationary partial differential equations (PDEs) arise throughout scientific computing, where the dominant frequency content and energy distribution can drift over time. While efficient in PDE solving, many spectral neural operators apply a shared spectral response across rollout stages, leading to mismatch with time-varying spectra in non-stationary systems. To address this issue, we propose Time-Frequency Gated Spectral Neural Operator (TF-SNO), a state-adaptive framework with learnable time-frequency gating inside spectral blocks. TF-SNO extracts compact frequency-domain and physical-space statistics from the current state to generate modulation coefficients, enabling the spectral response to evolve with the dynamics. TF-SNO learns temporal variation implicitly from the evolving state without introducing an explicit time dimension or time embedding, keeping the modeling complexity low. We further embed the adaptive operator blocks to accurately capture the multi-scale features, thereby improving long-horizon stability. Experiments on six non-stationary PDE benchmarks in 1D and 2D demonstrate that TF-SNO significantly reduces prediction errors and improves robustness compared to strong baselines, with particularly clear gains in long rollout, suggesting the effectiveness of state-dependent spectral adaptation in modeling non-stationary physical systems.

### [184] [DCD-PFN: A Decoupling-Aware Foundation Model for Causal Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21212)

*Zhengkang Guan,Yikang Chen,Yi He,Yunze Tong,Zijing Hu,Haoyuan Qian,Fei Wu,Kun Kuang*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出DCD-PFN，一种基于解耦感知的先验数据拟合网络（PFN）的因果发现基础模型，通过局部马尔可夫边界识别和并行化局部发现实现零样本因果图重构。

#### Problem

传统因果发现算法在处理高度非线性和强噪声系统时效果不佳，或存在严重计算瓶颈；现有基于PFN的表格基础模型在显式结构因果发现方面的潜力尚未被充分探索。

#### Key Idea

将全局因果图重构任务解耦为局部因果发现（马尔可夫边界识别），通过预训练学习样本级解耦权重，并利用并行化局部发现高效重构全局图。

#### System/Method Design

DCD-PFN采用解耦范式：在多样化的合成结构因果模型（SCM）上预训练，学习样本级解耦权重以实现马尔可夫边界（MB）识别；再通过并行化执行局部发现过程，高效重构完整因果图。该方法基于解耦因果发现的理论基础，并且是零样本的。

#### Experiments

在多样化的合成SCM数据上进行实验，评估零样本泛化能力。具体基线、指标和数值结果在摘要中未明确说明。

#### Why It Matters

首次将PFN基础模型的能力拓展到显式结构因果发现任务中，提出解耦感知的高效方案，兼具理论完备性和良好的零样本泛化能力，为因果发现提供了新的基础模型范式。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

与LLM系统研究的关联性较低，但PFN本身是一种基于Transformer的架构，其预训练-零样本推理范式的思路与LLM基础模型有共通之处。论文提出的并行化局部发现策略对分布式/并行计算有一定参考价值，但与MoE、KV cache、推理加速等方向无直接关联。

#### Abstract

Causal discovery is critical for understanding complex data-generating mechanisms, yet traditional algorithms often struggle with highly non-linear and noisy systems, or suffer from severe computational bottlenecks. Recent tabular foundation models based on Prior-Data Fitted Networks (PFNs) have demonstrated remarkable zero-shot inference capabilities, but their potential for explicit structural causal discovery remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose DCD-PFN, a decoupling-aware foundation model for causal discovery. Instead of directly amortizing global graph reconstruction, DCD-PFN focuses on local causal discovery through a decoupling-based paradigm. Through pre-training on diverse synthetic Structural Causal Models (SCMs), the model learns sample-wise decoupling weights that enable Markov boundary (MB) identification. Furthermore, by leveraging parallelized local discovery, DCD-PFN efficiently reconstructs global causal graphs while remaining grounded in the theoretical foundations of decoupling-based causal discovery. Experiments demonstrate that our foundation model achieves robust zero-shot generalization.

### [185] [Sakana Fugu Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21228)

*Yujin Tang,Edoardo Cetin,Jinglue Xu,Qi Sun,Stefan Nielsen,Vincent Richard,Haruto Goda,Iaroslav Tymchenko,Nhan Nguyen,Hyunin Lee,Mari Ashiga,Shashank Kotyan,So Kuroki,Tarin Clanuwat*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 提出Sakana Fugu，一组通过动态自适应编排（adaptive agentic scaffolds）协调多个LLM智能体协同工作的编排模型，在多项基准上达到SOTA性能。

#### Problem

不同LLM提供商在不同领域各有专长，但缺乏有效方法将这些个体专长组合成一个具备集体智能的系统。

#### Key Idea

训练一个语言模型作为"编排器"，使其能够理解用户查询并动态设计智能体编排方案（agentic scaffolds），从而按需调用和组合多个LLM智能体的能力。

#### System/Method Design

Fugu模型本身是语言模型，经过训练能够理解用户查询并动态地编排智能体团队（agentic scaffolds）来求解问题。训练范式包括大规模微调、进化算法和强化学习。发布了两个模型：Fugu（平衡性能与延迟，适合日常使用）和Fugu-Ultra（优先保证最难问题上的答案质量）。

#### Experiments

在SWE-Bench Pro、Terminal Bench、LiveCodeBench、GPQA-Diamond、Humanity's Last Exam、CharXiv Reasoning等多项挑战性任务上，与公开可访问的模型相比达到SOTA结果。

#### Why It Matters

展示了通过集体智能（多个专长LLM的协同）超越任何单一LLM能力上限的可行路径，并提出了一个端到端的生产级系统实现。推动了多智能体系统和动态查询自适应编排方向的研究。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关LLM系统研究：提出了全新的LLM编排范式，类似于MoE在模型层面对专家的路由，Fugu在系统层面对多个独立LLM进行动态路由与编排。涉及推理加速（Fugu平衡延迟与性能）、分布式系统（多智能体协作的编排基础设施）以及生产级系统设计。进化算法和强化学习的训练范式也值得关注。

#### Abstract

The capabilities of frontier Large Language Models (LLMs) continue to advance, with different providers increasingly specializing in distinct domains. This raises a natural next objective: how to combine the individual specializations of various LLMs into a collectively intelligent system. To this end, we report the development of Sakana Fugu, a family of orchestrator models that harness and amplify the capabilities of an LLM agent team. Fugu models are themselves language models trained to understand user queries and dynamically devise agentic scaffolds to solve them. Through these adaptive scaffolds, Fugu accesses performance beyond any individual LLM agent, achieving state-of-the-art results compared to other publicly accessible models across a range of challenging tasks, including SWE-Bench Pro, Terminal Bench, LiveCodeBench, GPQA-Diamond, Humanity's Last Exam, and CharXiv Reasoning. We release two models: Fugu, which balances performance with latency for everyday use, and Fugu-Ultra, which prioritizes answer quality on the hardest problems. We describe our training paradigm, which encompasses large-scale fine-tuning, evolutionary algorithms, and reinforcement learning approaches, along with the infrastructure and core design principles that turn these methods into a production system. We hope this report encourages further research into multi-agent systems and dynamic, query-adaptive agentic scaffolds as a path toward the next frontier of AI capabilities, accessed through collective intelligence.

### [186] [Comparative Evaluation of Machine Learning and Deep Learning Models for Wound-Rotor Synchronous Motor Performance Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21230)

*Kıvanç Doğan,Ahmet Orhan*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 本文系统比较了八种机器学习和深度学习模型（包括FT-Transformer等最新架构）在预测绕线转子同步电机（WRSM）转矩和效率方面的性能，通过多种子复现协议和Pareto分析发现神经网络模型显著优于树模型，FT-Transformer以R²=0.9928的精度和0.33毫秒的推理速度实现了对有限元分析（FEA）数个数量级的加速。

#### Problem

WRSM设计需要同时优化大量几何与电磁参数，传统有限元分析（FEA）计算成本极高，严重限制了设计空间的快速探索；现有基于机器学习的代理模型研究仅比较少数模型、未包含深度学习架构、且缺乏针对WRSM的综合基准测试。

#### Key Idea

对来自四个不同算法家族的八种ML/DL模型（包含FT-Transformer等现代深度学习架构）进行系统比较，采用多随机种子训练协议和超参数优化，并结合计算成本-精度的Pareto分析，提供全面的WRSM代理模型基准。

#### System/Method Design

使用拉丁超立方采样（LHS）在Motor-CAD仿真环境中生成3351个样本的数据集；对八种模型（涵盖四种算法家族）使用10种不同随机种子训练，并通过Optuna进行超参数调优；进行Pareto分析评估计算成本与预测精度的权衡。

#### Experiments

数据集为3351个WRSM样本（LHS采样）；评估指标包括R²、MAE、RMSE、MAPE；结果表明基于神经网络的模型系统性地优于基于树的模型；FT-Transformer取得最佳单模型精度（R²=0.9928），推理时间仅0.33毫秒，比FEA快数个数量级。

#### Why It Matters

首次为WRSM设计提供了覆盖多种算法家族的全面基准，展示了深度学习代理模型可大幅加速电机设计的参数空间探索，对消除稀土依赖的电机工程领域具有重要实用价值。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

本文聚焦于电机设计代理模型，与LLM系统/MoE/推理加速/KV缓存/分布式系统等领域无直接关联，但其方法学（多模型基准测试、超参数调优、计算成本-精度Pareto分析）对系统研究中的代理模型选择与评估具有方法论参考价值。

#### Abstract

Wound rotor synchronous motors have emerged as a strong alternative that eliminates dependence on REEs. However, WRSM design requires the simultaneous optimization of numerous geometric and electromagnetic parameters, and the high computational cost of conventional finite element analysis severely limits the rapid exploration of the large parameter space. Although there are machine-learning-based surrogate modeling studies in the literature, they generally compare only a limited number of models, exclude deep learning architectures, and do not provide a comprehensive benchmark specific to WRSM. In this study, the performance of a total of eight machine learning and deep learning models from four different algorithmic families was systematically compared for the prediction of WRSM torque and motor efficiency. On a dataset of 3351 samples generated using Latin Hypercube Sampling in the Motor-CAD simulation environment, each model was trained with 10 different random seed values and tuned via Optuna hyperparameter optimization. Different from the existing literature, this study jointly offers a broad model spectrum including recent deep learning architectures such as FT Transformer, a multi-seed reproducibility protocol, and a Pareto analysis of the computational cost-accuracy trade-off. The results revealed that neural-network-based models systematically outperform tree-based models. The FT-Transformer model achieved the highest single-model accuracy with R^2 = 0.9928, producing predictions in 0.33 milliseconds and thus obtaining several orders of magnitude speedup compared to FEA. Model performances were evaluated in a multidimensional manner using R^2, MAE, RMSE, and MAPE metrics.

### [187] [Does RoPE Prevent or Degrade Retrieval Heads? A Mechanistic Analysis Across Model Families](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21249)

*Cengizhan Bayram*

Main category: `cs.LG`

**TL;DR:** 该论文通过因果干预实验证明，检索头（retrieval heads）是长上下文召回的必要机制，且RoPE的旋转角度（频率）而非旋转位置编码（RoPE）本身是影响检索功能的关键因果变量，而RoPE的基超参数θ并不影响检索头的数量。

#### Problem

旋转位置编码（RoPE）的旋转操作是否会阻止检索头的形成，或者降低其功能？这是一个尚未被因果验证的假设性问题。

#### Key Idea

通过因果干预实验（头遮罩、维度归零、层聚类置换等）分离RoPE的基超参数θ与RoPE频率维度对检索头功能的影响，发现θ本身不影响检索头数量，而最低频RoPE维度的归零会剂量依赖地破坏召回能力。

#### System/Method Design

使用配对种子的"大海捞针"测试、层聚类置换、因果头遮罩等方法，对四个开放权重7-8B模型（OLMo-2, Qwen2.5, LLaMA-2/3.1, Gemma-2, Mistral）进行实验。特别地，基于Chiang & Yogatama (2025)的工作进行受控补丁实验：将检索头的最低频RoPE维度归零，并与随机维度归零对比。

#### Experiments

(i) 因果必要性：遮罩OLMo-2的87个检索头后召回率从1.00降至0.00，随机头无影响，且在Qwen中复现。(ii) θ不影响检索头数量：LLaMA-3.1（θ=500K）有47个检索头，LLaMA-2（θ=10K）有42个。(iii) 范数-效用关系具有模型家族特异性（Qwen d=-0.49, OLMo d=+0.50, LLaMA无显著），且非θ驱动。(iv) 低频RoPE维度归零剂量依赖地降低召回（从1.00降至0.18，32/128维归零时），随机维度归零仅降至0.98，效果在全部5个模型中一致。

#### Why It Matters

该工作首次从因果角度证实检索头对长上下文召回的必要性，并精确识别出RoPE频率（而非θ超参数或范数）是影响检索功能的因果变量，为理解RoPE的机制和优化长上下文模型提供了理论指导。

#### Relevance to LLM/MoE/System Research

直接相关：研究LLM中注意力机制的检索头与RoPE的因果作用机制，涉及长上下文召回、注意力头功能分析。对MoE系统而言，检索头的功能特异性可为专家路由或稀疏注意力提供参考；对推理加速和KV cache优化，理解哪些注意力维度对召回至关重要有助于设计更高效的缓存或剪枝策略。

#### Abstract

Retrieval heads, attention heads that copy information from earlier context to the current position, have been proposed as the mechanistic substrate for long-context recall. Rotary position embeddings (RoPE) rotate queries and keys by frequencies decaying with a base hyperparameter theta, and a natural hypothesis is that this rotation either prevents retrieval heads from forming or degrades their function. We test both across four open-weight 7-8B models spanning multi-head and grouped-query attention and a 100x range of theta, using paired-seed needle-in-a-haystack tests, layer-clustered permutation, and causal head-masking. (i) Retrieval heads are causally necessary: masking the 87 detected heads in OLMo-2 collapses recall from 1.00 to 0.00, while masking matched random heads has no effect; this replicates in Qwen. (ii) Higher theta does not reduce retrieval-head count (LLaMA-3.1 at theta=500K has 47 heads vs LLaMA-2 at theta=10K with 42), refuting the prevention hypothesis. (iii) The norm-utility relation is family-specific and significant in opposite directions (Qwen d=-0.49, OLMo d=+0.50, both significant; LLaMA null); since OLMo and LLaMA-3.1 share theta=500K yet differ, the effect is not theta-driven. (iv) Building on Chiang and Yogatama (2025), a controlled patch shows that zeroing the lowest-frequency RoPE dimensions of retrieval heads degrades recall dose-dependently (1.00 to 0.18 when 32 of 128 dimensions are zeroed, vs 0.98 for random dimensions); the effect is head-specific and task-specific. The causal variable is RoPE frequency, not norm-utility. The direction holds in all five models patched (OLMo-2, Qwen2.5-7B/14B, Gemma-2, Mistral) across four lineages and two scales. We do not claim cross-model magnitude. Code and a paired-seed harness are released.
